## 2026-07-22 - US-137: Wire the Digital Monster Color Version 5 evolution tree
- Renamed the `gazimon` seed line (US-046's pruned V5 tree) to `dmc-v5` and finished it: **ZERO new
  nodes and FOUR new edges.** 20 nodes in the line, 115 in the file, unchanged.
- Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (line rename x20, 4 new edges, 4 comments), `Resources/elements.json`,
  `Resources/moves.json`, `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`, `Sources/DexModel.swift` (lineTitles +
  a stale doc-comment example), `Tests/DMCVersion5TreeTests.swift` (new, 21 tests),
  `Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionGraphTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`,
  `Tests/DMCVersion2TreeTests.swift`, `Tests/RosterTests.swift`, `docs/evolutions-schema.md`.
- Build green, **1766 tests (1745 + 21), 0 failures.** Screenshotted on 41mm and 46mm.

- **Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE SECOND SIX-WIDE ROOKIE ALSO NEEDED NO CEILING RAISE — and this time the previous story had
  already run `ls` and STILL got it wrong.** US-136 correctly caught that V4's Palmon was not really
  six wide, then wrote that "US-137's Gizamon is a DIFFERENT case: US-046's notes say V5's only
  omission is Flymon, so Gizamon's drawable row really is five earned + junk = six edges, and that
  one probably WILL need the raise." The premise was right and the arithmetic was off by one:
  **six names minus one absent is FIVE drawable, which is four earned plus the junk fallback** —
  the five edges the `2...5` ceiling already allowed. Neither ceiling has moved in Phase E since
  US-134. The general lesson is sharper than "run `ls` first": **a row's edge count is
  `drawable − 1 + 1` only if the junk Champion is IN the row**, and in all five device trees it is
  (Numemon, Vegimon, Scumon, Nanimon, Raremon are each a Champion the document itself lists). So
  the edge count IS the drawable count, and the ceiling question is just "how many of the row have
  sheets?" Four earned is the hard limit anyway — `SeedRosterTests` wants distinct dominant
  energies and there are only four.

- **A Phase E story can add NO node at all.** US-133 added 10, US-134 13, US-135 3, US-136 1, this
  one 0. Every playable name in the Version 5 section was already a node (US-046) and the junk
  branches already existed (US-061); what was missing was four ARROWS the document draws. Orphans
  757 → 757 for the second story running. Counted with Appendix B over a regenerated
  `roster.generated.json` AND cross-checked by recomputing the count against
  `git show HEAD:Resources/evolutions.json` joined to the same roster — identical stage by stage.
  `DMCVersion5TreeTests.testTheStoryAddedNoNodesAndSoRemovedNoOrphans` pins it.
  **Expect the remaining Pendulum trees (US-138..143) to be the opposite shape**: none of them has a
  seed line at all, so every one of them is authoring from an empty start rather than finishing
  someone's pruned tree. US-137 is where the "rename and finish" pattern runs out.

- **The schema doc was already describing the tree this story built.** `docs/evolutions-schema.md`
  said the V5 line "leaves both Rookies with five Champions apiece, four of them shared" — which
  was true of the DOCUMENT and false of the DATA, where both Rookies had three. Prose in a doc is
  not a test. If a claim about the shipped data matters, it belongs in an assertion; the doc line
  had been wrong since US-046 and nothing caught it.

- **AC9 ("every edge has at least one condition with a non-empty hint") cannot be met literally,
  and every Phase E story has quietly re-read it.** `EvolutionCriteriaTests.testEveryJunkFallbackIsReachableByInaction`
  requires the `isDefault` edge to carry NO criteria — US-020's fallback ignores an edge's gates, so
  a gated junk edge is data that lies about how it is taken — and the Digitama/Baby rungs are
  unconditioned for the same reason. The honest reading, asserted here as three separate claims:
  every EARNED edge at Child-and-up is conditioned, every condition in the WHOLE file has a
  non-blank hint, and every junk edge is unconditioned. Say which reading you took in `notes`.

- **A line rename is still exactly six places, four trees running** (`elements.json` lineDefaults,
  `moves.json` lineDefaults, `MinigameAssignment.byLine`, `DexModel.lineTitles`,
  `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict, `SeedRosterTests`' `$0.line ==` filters) — **plus one
  this tree had that the others did not: OTHER stories' tests asserting on the old slug.**
  `DMCVersion2TreeTests` asserted `shared.line == "gazimon"` and that two `dmcv2_*` node comments
  contained the word "gazimon", because US-134 scoped Vademon and Ebemon AROUND this line. A
  `grep -rn '<old-slug>' Sources Tests docs Resources scripts` and reading every hit is what caught
  it; the node id `gazimon` is also a real id, so most hits must NOT change.

- **`extyranomon` is in `RosterTests`' alias list but is NOT a line-scoped alias.** It is the
  roster's `ex-tyranomon` with the hyphen dropped — one id in two spellings, not one Digimon in two
  trees like `dmcv2_vademon`. A test now pins the difference, because the list reads as though V5
  needed a scoped id when it is in fact the line that OWNS the plain `vademon`/`ebemon` ids US-134
  had to scope for V2. Phase E's alias tally is still four: `dmcv1_shinmonzaemon`, `dmcv2_ebemon`,
  `dmcv2_vademon`, `dmcv4_palmon`.

- **The Tsukaimon call, a fourth time, and it should stop being called a judgement.** Psychemon is
  in no source tree (US-061 invented it while a Child could carry two earned branches); giving
  Gazimon and Gizamon their full rows made its Devidramon redundant, and emptying it would have
  left a shipped Child that evolves into nothing. It keeps its branches. That is US-134's Geremon,
  US-135's Tsukaimon, US-136's Hyokomon/Muchomon and now this — **treat "the node keeps what it
  has" as the default and only deviate with a reason in the data file.**

- **"Mugendramon (Machinedramon)" is one Digimon.** The document writes the dub name in
  parentheses; `Machinedramon` matches nothing in the pack or the roster. A test pins that, because
  a parenthetical in a source tree reads exactly like a second name to wire.

- REMAINS: US-138 onward (24/56 passing). US-138 is Pendulum Color V1 Nature Spirits — the first
  Phase E tree with NO seed line behind it, so read the paragraph above about that before
  estimating it against US-135/136/137's size.

## 2026-07-22 - US-138: Wire the Pendulum Color V1 Nature Spirits evolution tree
- Authored `penc-nsp` from NOTHING — **30 new nodes**, the widest line in the file; 115 -> 145.
  **Orphans 757 -> 739 (18 removed.)** Betamon is the section's one absent sprite and its two
  Champions were rehomed. The tree renders in the Dex on both watch sizes.
- Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (+30 nodes), `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`
  (+30 entries each plus a `penc-nsp` lineDefault), `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`,
  `Sources/DexModel.swift`, `Tests/PendulumNatureSpiritsTreeTests.swift` (new, 24 tests),
  `Tests/EvolutionGraphTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionGraphValidatorTests.swift`,
  `Tests/ElementCatalogTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`,
  `Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift`, `Tests/RosterTests.swift`, `Tests/MinigameAssignmentTests.swift`,
  `Tests/EggHatchingTests.swift`, `Tests/DexMoveRowTests.swift`, `Tests/DexTypeBadgeTests.swift`,
  `Tests/DMCVersion5TreeTests.swift`, `docs/evolutions-schema.md`.
- Build green, **1789 tests (1765 + 24), 0 failures.** Validator: zero findings over the whole file.

- **Learnings for future iterations:**

- **AUTHORING FROM NOTHING IS A DIFFERENT JOB FROM FINISHING A SEED, and the cost is in the
  KNOCK-ON, not in the tree.** The 30 nodes were the easy half. What US-133..137 never had to touch,
  because they renamed an existing line rather than adding one, was **six tests that hard-code a
  fact about the WHOLE FILE**: `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict, `ElementCatalogTests`'
  and `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`' `graph.nodes.count == 115`, `EggHatchingTests`' set of
  seeded Digitama (a seventh line means a seventh starting egg), `SeedRosterTests`' `seedLines`
  junk-path literals, and `RosterTests`' exact alias list. Budget for those BEFORE writing data.
- **Three tests used a roster-only Digimon BY NAME as their "not in the graph" example, and this
  story ate it.** `megaseadramon` was that example in `ElementCatalogTests`, `DexMoveRowTests` and
  `DexTypeBadgeTests`. Phase E is pulling the whole roster into the graph, so **every one of those
  examples is on a timer** — all three now FIND one at run time (`roster.entries.first { graph.node(id:
  $0.id) == nil }`) instead of naming one. If you write a test that needs "something outside the
  graph", derive it; the next sweep will take whatever you hard-code.
- **THE LINES OUTGREW THE MINIGAMES.** `MinigameAssignmentTests.testEachShippedLineGetsADifferentGame`
  asserted a BIJECTION — six lines, six games — which held only because there happened to be six
  lines. `penc-nsp` is the seventh and US-139..143 add five more, so it is now "every line is in
  the table, all six games are reached", plus a test naming the one sharing pair
  (`palmon`/`penc-nsp`, both nature-flavoured). **Do not re-tighten it.**
- **A NEW LINE'S EGG MUST BE A REAL ROSTER DIGITAMA, NOT A LINE-SCOPED ALIAS — this is playability,
  not taste.** `maps.json` grants a Digitama by ROSTER id (all 57 sprite ids are placed, one per
  map), and a `pencnsp_digitama` alias has NO roster entry, so no map could ever drop it and the
  line would be unstartable however well it was wired. `Resources/roster.json` excludes alias ids
  even though `roster.generated.json` carries them. Pick from the 50 orphan Digitama, and prefer
  one belonging to a Rookie of the tree — this one took `tento_digitama` (Tentomon's, on
  08_jungle). It also buys an orphan.
- **An alias node removes NO orphan.** 30 nodes, 18 orphans. The 12 `pencnsp_` aliases share a
  roster entry that was already wired, so the arithmetic is "new nodes with a plain roster id",
  not "new nodes". Assert the split or the notes read as a miscount.
- **Twelve aliases is the new high-water mark and each one costs THREE entries** (node,
  `elements.json`, `moves.json`) **plus a signature name that must be globally unique** — so it
  cannot be copied from the Digimon it aliases. A Pendulum tree overlaps the Digital Monster trees
  heavily by design; expect US-139..143 to be the same shape. A quick way to price a tree before
  starting: how many of its names already have a node?
- **A DEXONLY ROOKIE COSTS MORE THAN A DEXONLY CHAMPION.** Every earlier Phase E absence was a
  leaf (Flymon, Kokatorimon, Nanimon) and was simply dropped. Betamon is a ROOKIE with two
  Champions and four Digimon above them: dropping it would have stranded six. **Rehome the
  orphaned subtree onto a sibling Rookie and prefer a pairing the FILE already makes** — Seadramon
  went to Agumon because `dmc-v1` already hangs a Seadramon off Agumon, which turns an invention
  into a precedent. Watch the Rookie's out-degree and the distinct-energy rule while you do it.
- **When a document draws no junk branch, you have to invent one, and it should come off ORPHAN
  sheets.** The five `dmc-v*` trees each name their own junk Champion; the Pendulum ones name
  none. PlatinumScumon -> Pumpmon -> NoblePumpmon were all unused, so the neglect path paid for
  itself in orphans instead of costing three more aliases. **Assert the invention** — a test greps
  the tree markdown for all three names and fails if any turns out to be in it after all — and add
  the Child-rung and Adult-rung ones to `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` or the junk-fallback test
  fails.
- **A "this story added no nodes" test must count ITS OWN LINE, never the file.**
  `DMCVersion5TreeTests` asserted `graph.nodes.count == 115` to say US-137 added nothing, and this
  story broke it by adding a tree somewhere else entirely. A global total cannot say anything
  about what one story did once another lands beside it.
- **`Resources/*.md` IS in the app bundle** (project.yml bundles the whole folder), so a test can
  read the source tree markdown at run time and assert what the document does and does not say.
  That is how "the junk chain is not from the document" became an assertion rather than a comment.
- **`-dexLineDemo=<line>` needs `-dexDemo`** (still true, US-137's note) and the Dex heading is a
  `navigationTitle` that truncates near fifteen characters on 41mm: "Pendulum NSp" fits, a longer
  "Pendulum Nature Spirits" would not have.
- REMAINS: US-139 onward (25/56 passing). US-139..143 are the other five Pendulum trees and are
  the same shape as this one — no seed line, heavy overlap with the Digital Monster trees, no junk
  branch in the document, and a Digitama to choose from the roster.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-139: Wire the Pendulum Color V2 Deep Savers evolution tree
- Authored `penc-ds` from NOTHING — **31 new nodes**, now the widest line in the file; 145 -> 176.
  **Orphans 739 -> 713 (26 removed.)** The first Phase E tree with NO absent name. The tree renders
  in the Dex on both watch sizes.
- Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (+31 nodes), `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`
  (+31 entries each plus a `penc-ds` lineDefault), `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`,
  `Sources/DexModel.swift`, `Tests/PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests.swift` (new, 24 tests),
  `Tests/EvolutionGraphTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionGraphValidatorTests.swift`,
  `Tests/ElementCatalogTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`,
  `Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift`, `Tests/RosterTests.swift`, `Tests/EggHatchingTests.swift`,
  `Tests/MinigameAssignmentTests.swift`, `Tests/PendulumNatureSpiritsTreeTests.swift`,
  `docs/evolutions-schema.md`.
- Build green, **1813 tests (1789 + 24), 0 failures** — and 1813 is exactly
  `grep -cE '^\s+func test' Tests/*.swift`, so the summary is not a crashed-host undercount.
  Validator: zero findings over the whole file.

- **Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A NAME WITH NO SPRITE IS USUALLY A NAME WITH ANOTHER SPELLING. `find -iname` ON THE DOCUMENT'S
  SPELLING IS HALF A SEARCH.** Six of this section's twenty-seven names would have been reported
  absent or dexOnly by the search every earlier Phase E story ran, and all six are playable:
  - **Nothing under the document's spelling, a real sheet under another** — Pichimon/`Pitchmon`,
    Bukamon/`Pukamon`, Syakomon/`Shakomon`, Dragomon/`Dagomon`. The first three are alternate
    romanizations the pack itself uses; the fourth is a dub name (Wikimon's Dagomon page gives
    Dragomon as the Japanese one).
  - **A dexOnly TWIN under the document's spelling** — the roster holds BOTH `octomon` (idle-only)
    and `octmon` (a real 48x64 sheet), and both `marinedevimon` (idle-only) and `marindevimon`.
    This is the nastier shape: `find -iname '*octomon*'` finds a file and the roster finds an
    entry, so the name looks present, and it is only the `dexOnly` flag that says otherwise.
  **Before calling a name absent, search the roster by SUBSTRING of the display name and check
  every hit's `dexOnly`, not just the exact spelling.** US-138 spent its story rehoming Betamon's
  subtree; this one would have had to do that twice (Dagomon → Pukumon behind Octmon, Leviamon
  behind MarinDevimon) and drop four more, for nothing.
- **Adding a line is now an EIGHT-place knock-on, not six.** US-138 listed six whole-file facts;
  two more surfaced here: `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` (a new tree invents a junk chain, and
  the Child-rung and Adult-rung targets must be named there or the junk-fallback test fails) and
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`' shared-game assertion. The full list, in the order they fail:
  `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict; `graph.nodes.count` in `ElementCatalogTests` AND
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; `EggHatchingTests`' seeded-Digitama set; `SeedRosterTests`'
  `seedLines`; `RosterTests`' exact alias list; `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`;
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`' sharer map.
- **US-138's own tree test asserted the GLOBAL node count and this story broke it** — the exact
  mistake US-138's notes had already named for US-137's. A story's "I added N nodes" claim must be
  `graph.nodes.filter { $0.line == line }.count`, never `graph.nodes.count`, however obviously
  true the global number is on the day it is written. Rewritten in place here.
- **The lines have outgrown the games AGAIN, and the shared-game test needs a MAP, not a pair.**
  `testTheOnlySharedGameIsTheTwoNatureLines` was written for exactly one sharing pair; `penc-ds` is
  the eighth line and the second sharer (Crown Sprint, beside `dmc-v3`). It is now
  `testTheSharedGamesAreExactlyTheTwoAuthoredPairs` and asserts the whole
  game -> [lines] dictionary, which scales to US-140..143 by adding a line to a literal.
- **An alias's plain id need not belong to a Digital Monster tree any more.**
  `pencds_megaseadramon` and `pencds_metalseadramon` shadow ids US-138 gave to `penc-nsp`. The
  Pendulum trees overlap EACH OTHER as well as the dmc-v* ones, so from US-140 on, price a tree by
  checking the plain id against the WHOLE file rather than against the five device trees.
- **`json.dump` cannot rewrite `evolutions.json`: the file is mixed-encoding.** Older comments hold
  `—` escapes and the US-136-and-later ones hold literal em dashes, so neither
  `ensure_ascii=True` nor `False` round-trips — a dump reformats ~30 unrelated lines either way.
  Append the new nodes TEXTUALLY (`json.dumps` each node, indent it four spaces, splice before the
  final `\n  ]\n}`), and do `elements.json` / `moves.json` by string insertion too, since their
  entries are one-line objects that any dump would explode. Keep non-ASCII out of new comments.
- **The notification alert ate the first screenshot pass again** — it survives uninstall, exactly
  as the pattern above says, and `simctl erase` is still the only fix. Budget the erase into the
  FIRST run rather than discovering it on the shot.
- REMAINS: US-140 onward (26/56 passing). US-140..143 are the last four Pendulum trees, the same
  shape as this one — no seed line, no junk branch in the document, a Digitama to choose from the
  roster, and now overlap with the other Pendulum trees as well as the Digital Monster ones.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-140 (Wire the Pendulum Color V3 Nightmare Soldiers evolution tree)

Authored `penc-nso` from nothing, the third Phase E device tree with no seed line to rename.
**31 nodes, 176 -> 207**, tying `penc-ds` as the widest line in the file.
**ORPHANS 713 -> 692, 21 removed**, counted with Appendix B over a regenerated
`roster.generated.json` (Digitama 49->48, Baby I 37->36, Baby II 41->40, Child 100->97,
Adult 149->144, Perfect 135->129, Ultimate 186->182; Armor-Hybrid unchanged at 16). The other 10
new nodes are line-scoped `pencnso_` aliases and remove nothing.

The tree, from `Resources/Digimon_Color_And_Pendulum_Color_Evolution_Trees.md` line 124:
Baku Digitama -> Mokumon -> PetiMeramon, forking to Bakumon / Candmon / PicoDevimon, seven
Champion-to-Mega threads above them, and Gokimon -> Darumamon -> Deathmon as the invented junk
chain. Egg is `baku_digitama` (Bakumon's own, already dropped by `03_ocean`, so maps.json was not
touched).

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`,
`Sources/DexModel.swift`, `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`,
`Tests/PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests.swift` (new, 25 tests),
`Tests/EvolutionGraphTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionGraphValidatorTests.swift`,
`Tests/ElementCatalogTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`,
`Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift`, `Tests/RosterTests.swift`, `Tests/EggHatchingTests.swift`,
`Tests/MinigameAssignmentTests.swift`, `docs/evolutions-schema.md`.

Build green, **1838 tests (1813 + 25), 0 failures** - and 1838 is exactly
`grep -cE '^\s+func test' Tests/*.swift`, so the summary is not a crashed-host undercount.
Validator: zero findings over the whole file.

- **Learnings for future iterations:**

- **GREP THE WHOLE DOCUMENT BEFORE CHOOSING A JUNK NODE.** The junk chain is invented off orphan
  sheets, and the only thing that makes an orphan safe to spend is that no LATER tree needs it.
  US-140's first choice for the junk Perfect was WaruMonzaemon; the story's own
  "none of these three is in the markdown" grep caught it in the **Version 5** Metal Empire
  section (line 162, `Champion: Mekanorimon -> Ultimate: WaruMonzaemon -> Mega: VenomMyotismon`),
  which is US-142's. Taking it would have forced US-142 into an alias for its own earned Ultimate
  AND made a junk node an earned one two stories later. Darumamon replaced it. Write that grep
  FIRST, not as a closing assertion.
- **The same section also spends VenomVamdemon**, which this story wired as an earned Mega. US-142
  will need `pencv5_venomvamdemon`. The Pendulum sections overlap each other more than they overlap
  the dmc-v* ones, so from here on price a tree against the whole file AND against the remaining
  document sections.
- **A dub name can differ from the sprite name by a whole word, not just a letter.** US-138/139's
  lesson was romanization drift (Pichimon/Pitchmon); this section is worse - `Mammothmon` is
  `Mammon`, `Wizardmon` is `Wizarmon`, `Pumpkinmon` is `Pumpmon`, `Piedmon` is `Piemon`,
  `Myotismon` is `Vamdemon`, `Candlemon` is `Candmon`. **A `find -iname '*<documentname>*'` that
  returns nothing is not evidence of absence; try the JAPANESE name.** Nine of this section's
  twenty-eight names would have been called absent by the search every earlier story ran, which
  would have cost the tree a third of its nodes.
- **A tree can be missing a whole RUNG, not just a leaf.** The unlockable slot 6 here has no
  Rookie and no Champion with a sheet, but its Ultimate and Mega both do. The move that saved it
  was checking Wikimon for what actually sits between the surviving rungs (Loogarmon), then
  re-homing that Champion under a Rookie the same page links it to. **Do not drop a thread because
  its bottom is missing** - price the rehome first, and record the reference in the node comment
  (a test greps for "Wikimon").
- **`ConditionContext` in the reachability fixture cannot express a battle win RATIO.** It has
  `battlesLifetime` and no wins, so `care.battleWinRatio` on a CHILD's earned edge makes
  `testEachRookiesEarnedBranchesAreAllReachable` fail with a bare `nil`. Earlier trees only ever
  used that metric at Adult, where no test walks it. Keep `care.battleWinRatio` off Child edges, or
  extend the fixture.
- **The knock-on list is stable at eight places** (US-139's list, unchanged, all eight fired):
  `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict; `graph.nodes.count` in `ElementCatalogTests` AND
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; `EggHatchingTests`' seeded-Digitama set; `SeedRosterTests`'
  `seedLines`; `RosterTests`' exact alias list; `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`;
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`' sharer map. US-139's rewrite of that last one into a
  game -> [lines] dictionary paid off exactly as intended: one literal.
- **`json.dump` still cannot rewrite `evolutions.json`** - mixed encoding, as US-139 recorded.
  Splice new nodes TEXTUALLY (`json.dumps` each node, indent four spaces, insert before the final
  `\n  ]\n}`), and do `elements.json` / `moves.json` by string insertion. Keep new comments ASCII.
- **A generator script is worth writing, and worth re-running rather than patching.** The whole
  31-node tree came out of one `/tmp` python script; when the junk Perfect had to change, reverting
  the three JSON files with `git checkout` and re-running was cleaner than hand-editing 31 nodes.
  But CHECK EVERY `str.replace` LANDS - two of the fix-up replacements silently matched nothing
  because of line wrapping, and the resulting node (PetiMeramon with no edges at all) passed the
  validator and only failed on reachability.
- REMAINS: US-141 onward (27/56 passing). US-141..143 are the last three Pendulum trees, same
  shape - no seed line, no junk branch in the document, a Digitama to choose from the roster, and
  now overlap with the other Pendulum trees as well as the Digital Monster ones.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-141 (Wire the Pendulum Color V4 Wind Guardians evolution tree)

Authored `penc-wg` from nothing, the fourth Phase E device tree with no seed line to rename.
**31 nodes, 207 -> 238**, joining `penc-ds` and `penc-nso` as the widest lines in the file.
**ORPHANS 692 -> 667, 25 removed**, counted with Appendix B over a regenerated
`roster.generated.json` (Digitama 48->47, Baby I 36->35, Baby II 40->39, Child 97->94,
Adult 144->138, Perfect 129->123, Ultimate 182->175; Armor-Hybrid unchanged at 16). The other 6
new nodes are line-scoped `pencwg_` aliases and remove nothing - the best ratio of any Pendulum
tree so far.

The tree, from `Resources/Digimon_Color_And_Pendulum_Color_Evolution_Trees.md` line 138:
Flora Digitama -> Nyokimon -> Pyocomon, forking FOUR ways to Piyomon / Floramon / Mushmon /
Pteromon, seven Champion-to-Mega threads above them, and Zassoumon -> TonosamaGekomon ->
ElDoradimon as the invented junk chain. Egg is `flora_digitama` (Floramon's), already dropped by
`14_farmland`, so maps.json was not touched.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`,
`Sources/DexModel.swift`, `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`,
`Tests/PendulumWindGuardiansTreeTests.swift` (new, 27 tests),
`Tests/EvolutionGraphTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionGraphValidatorTests.swift`,
`Tests/ElementCatalogTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`,
`Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift`, `Tests/RosterTests.swift`, `Tests/EggHatchingTests.swift`,
`Tests/MinigameAssignmentTests.swift`, `docs/evolutions-schema.md`.

Build green, **1865 tests (1838 + 27), 0 failures** - and 1865 is exactly
`grep -cE '^\s+func test' Tests/*.swift`, so the summary is not a crashed-host undercount.
Validator: zero findings over the whole file.

- **Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A tree can be missing a MIDDLE rung and a TOP rung, not just a bottom one, and the same rehome
  move fixes all three shapes.** US-140 rescued a thread whose Rookie and Champion were undrawn;
  this section has no `Deramon` (the Perfect between Kiwimon and Griffomon) and no
  `Crossmon`/`Eaglemon` (the Mega above Garbagemon). Wikimon's own Evolves From / Evolves To lists
  name a stand-in that sits on the SAME thread in each case - Blossomon is listed both as a
  Kiwimon evolution and as a Griffomon prior form, Rafflesimon as a Gerbemon evolution - so the
  document's arrows survive intact. **Fetch the Wikimon page for the rung ABOVE and the rung BELOW
  the gap and intersect the two lists**; that is a five-minute lookup that saved six nodes here.
- **Do not trust a substring search that finds nothing when a letter is INSIDE the name.**
  `Jureimon` is not a substring of `Jyureimon`, so the document's own bracketed spelling misses its
  own sheet. `grep -i` on a prefix (`jure` -> nothing, `jyu` -> the file) is the fix. Two of this
  section's names hid this way and both were nearly reported absent.
- **`garbamon` is NOT `Garbagemon`.** The roster's nearest substring hit is a different Digimon and
  dexOnly, while the real sheet is `Perfect/Gerbemon.png` under the Japanese name - so the name
  looks simultaneously present and unusable, and both readings are wrong. US-139's Octomon/Octmon
  rule with an extra turn of the screw: after checking every substring hit's `dexOnly`, KEEP
  LOOKING under the Japanese name rather than concluding the Digimon is idle-only.
- **An egg does not have to be the default Rookie's own, and pretending otherwise wastes a story.**
  Every Pendulum tree so far took its In-Training's default Rookie's egg; here that egg
  (`piyo_digitama`) went to `dmc-v4` in US-136, because the Digital Monster Ver.4 tree is Piyomon's
  too. The rule that actually matters is only "a real roster Digitama that some map drops" - see
  `flora_digitama`'s comment. **Check the map that drops it and name that map correctly**: the
  first draft of this comment said `02_forest`, which is not even a map in this app; `14_farmland`
  is. A wrong map id in a comment is a lie a later story will act on.
- **The unlockable-slot Rookie is drawable again**, so US-138/139's conditioned In-Training edge
  came back after lapsing in US-140. If a section marks a Rookie "Unlockable Slot N", check for its
  sheet before assuming the shape is gone: Pteromon has one, and its whole thread (Galemon,
  GrandGalemon, Zephagamon) is the only one in this section drawn whole AND unrespelled.
- **A four-way fork at Baby II is fine and is now the widest in the file.** Four Rookies means four
  edges, one per energy type, which is exactly the ceiling `SeedRosterTests`' distinct-energy rule
  allows. No out-degree ceiling moved (still 2...5, unchanged since US-134) because the Child and
  Adult rungs are only two and three wide here.
- **The knock-on list is stable at eight places for the third tree running** (US-139's list,
  unchanged, all eight fired): `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict; `graph.nodes.count` in
  `ElementCatalogTests` AND `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; `EggHatchingTests`' seeded-Digitama
  set; `SeedRosterTests`' `seedLines`; `RosterTests`' exact alias list;
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` (BOTH the Adult and the Perfect junk node);
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`' sharer map. Watch the SORT ORDER in `RosterTests`: `pencwg_` sorts
  after `pencnsp_`, not after `pencnso_`.
- **Terminal nodes in `evolutions.json` OMIT the `evolutions` key entirely** rather than carrying
  `[]`. The decoder accepts both, so this is style, not correctness - but a generator that always
  writes the key produces a 47-node inconsistency in one commit. Emit it only when non-empty.
- **`json.dump` still cannot rewrite `evolutions.json`** - mixed encoding, as US-139 recorded.
  Splice new nodes TEXTUALLY, and do `elements.json` / `moves.json` by string insertion. Keep new
  comments ASCII. The whole 31-node tree came out of one `/tmp` python script, and it was reverted
  with `git checkout` and re-run THREE times (duplicate signature names, the `evolutions: []`
  style, a wrong map id) rather than hand-patched. That is the right move every time.
- **Check new `signatureName`s against the WHOLE file, not just your line.** Three of the first
  draft's collided with the `palmon` line's (Flower Cannon, Thorn Whip, Petal Puff) - unsurprising,
  since this tree draws Togemon, Lilimon and Rosemon too, and a flower tree runs out of flower
  words. `MoveCatalogTests` catches it, but only after a full 23-second test run.
- REMAINS: US-142 onward (28/56 passing). US-142 (Metal Empire) and US-143 (Virus Busters / ZERO)
  are the last two Pendulum trees. US-140's notes already flag two names US-142 must handle:
  WaruMonzaemon is its earned Ultimate over Mekanorimon, and VenomVamdemon is already spent by
  `penc-nso`, so US-142 needs `pencv5_venomvamdemon`.
