## 2026-07-22 - US-142 (Wire the Pendulum Color V5 Metal Empire evolution tree)

Authored `penc-me` from nothing, the fifth Phase E device tree with no seed line to rename.
**32 nodes, 238 -> 270 - the widest line in the file on its own**, past the three-way tie at 31.
**ORPHANS 667 -> 643, 24 removed**, counted with Appendix B over a regenerated
`roster.generated.json`, with the pre-story 667 REPRODUCED in a `git worktree` at HEAD rather than
trusted from US-141's notes (Digitama 47->46, Baby I 35->34, Baby II 39->38, Child 94->90,
Adult 138->131, Perfect 123->117, Ultimate 175->171; Armor-Hybrid unchanged at 16). The other 8 new
nodes are line-scoped `pencme_` aliases and remove nothing - the WORST alias ratio of any Pendulum
tree, because this section shares Agumon's whole thread with two other trees.

The tree, from `Resources/Digimon_Color_And_Pendulum_Color_Evolution_Trees.md` line 152:
Funbee Digitama -> Choromon -> Caprimon, forking four ways to ToyAgumon / Kokuwamon / Hagurumon /
Junkmon, nine Champion-to-Mega threads above them, and Raremon -> Locomon -> GrandLocomon as the
invented junk chain. Egg is `funbee_digitama`, dropped by `06_industrial`, so maps.json was not
touched.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`,
`Sources/DexModel.swift`, `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`,
`Tests/PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests.swift` (new, 28 tests),
`Tests/EvolutionGraphTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionGraphValidatorTests.swift`,
`Tests/ElementCatalogTests.swift`, `Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`,
`Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift`, `Tests/RosterTests.swift`, `Tests/EggHatchingTests.swift`,
`Tests/MinigameAssignmentTests.swift`, `Tests/DexScreenTests.swift`,
`Tests/PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests.swift`, `docs/evolutions-schema.md`.

Build green, **1894 tests (1865 + 28 new + 1 backfilled), 0 failures** - and 1894 is exactly
`grep -cE '^\s+func test' Tests/*.swift`, so the summary is not a crashed-host undercount.
Validator: zero findings over the whole file. The app was also installed and launched on the 46mm
Simulator and drew its Dex, which is the cheap proof that no `bundled` catalog traps at launch.

- **Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A tree can be broken at BOTH ends of one thread, and the two breaks fail DIFFERENTLY.** The
  unlockable slot here is Junkmon -> Machmon -> Rebellimon -> HeavyMetaldramon. `Machmon` is
  US-139's twin trap - it IS in the roster and its PNG IS on disk, so `find` and a substring search
  both say "present", and only `dexOnly` says it can never sit on an edge. `HeavyMetaldramon` is
  the other shape: absent from the pack under every spelling tried (`heavymetal*`, `metaldra*`,
  `heavy*` -> only HeavyLeomon). **Run BOTH checks on every name: does a sheet exist, and is the
  roster entry playable.** Either one alone gets one of these two names wrong.
- **The rehome-by-intersection move works on a thread broken twice.** Wikimon lists Minotaurmon in
  Junkmon's *Evolves To* AND in Rebellimon's *Evolves From*, and Gundramon in Rebellimon's
  *Evolves To*: two pages, four lists, and the whole thread survives with the document's arrows
  intact. US-140 did this for a missing bottom, US-141 for a missing middle and a missing top;
  this is both ends of one thread at once. Fetching the page for the rung above the gap and the
  rung below it remains a five-minute lookup that saves a subtree.
- **A junk pick must be grepped against the SECTION, not the whole document - and the whole
  document, not just the section.** Both greps matter and they answer different questions.
  `Raremon` is drawn three times by the Digital Monster Ver.5 tree fourteen lines further up the
  same file, so a whole-file grep would have rejected a pick that is completely fine here (it is
  simply `pencme_raremon`, an alias). `Locomon` and `GrandLocomon` had to clear the whole-file
  grep, because a name a LATER section draws cannot be spent on junk. The test in this story does
  both, and says which is which.
- **US-140's marker test fired exactly as designed and cost nothing.** It asserted
  `XCTAssertNil(graph.node(id: "warumonzaemon"))` with a comment saying US-142 would break it. It
  broke on the first run of this story, pointed straight at the reason, and was rewritten into the
  claim it was always guarding (WaruMonzaemon is a node, it is `penc-me`'s, and it is nobody's junk
  fallback). **Leave the marker; it is worth more than a note in a file nobody greps.**
- **A hard-coded "the roster dwarfs the graph" threshold is on the same timer as a hard-coded
  roster-only example.** `DexScreenTests.testMostOfTheShippedRosterHasNoCandidates` asserted
  `> 800` and this story took it to exactly 800. Fixed by making it a PROPORTION
  (`> Roster.bundled.entries.count / 2`), which survives every remaining sweep. US-138's lesson
  about derived examples applies to derived COUNTS too - Phase E moves both numbers every story.
- **`DexModel.lineTitles` had no test at all, and a missing entry is invisible.** The fallback
  heads the section with the raw slug (`penc-me`), which is cosmetic and would never fail a build.
  Backfilled as a derived test over `EvolutionGraph.bundled`'s lines, so the next tree is TOLD to
  add its title. The eight-place knock-on list has always included this file; it just had nothing
  enforcing it.
- **This tree's threads MERGE, which no earlier one did, and it is the graph shape to expect from
  here on.** Tankmon and Thunderballmon both climb to Knightmon, and the document draws Andromon
  twice - over Revolmon toward Machinedramon and over Guardromon toward HiAndromon. One node
  carries both, so `pencme_andromon` is the file's only Perfect with two parents AND two children,
  and the only one whose second outgoing edge had to be EARNED rather than the usual single
  `isDefault` climb. Nothing in the suite objected: the 2..5 out-degree rule and the junk-fallback
  rule are both scoped to Child and Adult, so a Perfect may branch freely as long as exactly one
  edge is `isDefault`.
- **An egg need not belong to the tree at all.** US-141 found the egg was not the DEFAULT Rookie's;
  here not one of the four Rookies has a Digitama on disk, so all that survives of the rule is "a
  real roster Digitama that a map drops". `funbee_digitama` was chosen off `06_industrial`, the
  machine map, and the comment names that map - a wrong map id in a comment is a lie a later story
  acts on (US-141 shipped `02_forest`, which is not a map in this app).
- **Nine of this section's twenty-eight names are the ONLY one of a pair that exists**, and five
  need the drift rules: Kapurimon/`Caprimon`, Deputymon/`Revolmon`, Mekanorimon/`Mechanorimon`,
  Machinedramon/`Mugendramon`, VenomMyotismon/`VenomVamdemon`. Nothing new in kind - but the count
  has not dropped in five trees running, so budget for it.
- **The knock-on list is stable at eight places for the fourth tree running** (US-139's list, all
  eight fired): `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict; `graph.nodes.count` in
  `ElementCatalogTests` AND `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; `EggHatchingTests`' seeded-Digitama set;
  `SeedRosterTests`' `seedLines`; `RosterTests`' exact alias list; `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`
  (BOTH the Adult and the Perfect junk node); `MinigameAssignmentTests`' sharer map. Add TWO more
  this story found: `DexScreenTests`' roster-vs-graph threshold, and any earlier tree's marker test.
  Watch the SORT ORDER in `RosterTests`: `pencme_` sorts after `pencds_` and before `pencnso_`.
- **`penc-me` takes the last unshared-but-one minigame.** Button Masher now has `dmc-v1` beside it;
  Power Meter (`dmc-v2`) is the only game a single line still holds. The next tree has no
  unshared game left to take, so US-143 will be picking a SECOND sharer for some game - the
  tie-break to use is the one every story since US-138 has used: fewest Digimon behind the game,
  flavour breaks ties.
- **`json.dump` still cannot rewrite `evolutions.json`** - mixed encoding, as US-139 recorded.
  Splice new nodes TEXTUALLY, and do `elements.json` / `moves.json` by string insertion; the diff
  for those two was 34 added lines each and nothing reformatted. The whole 32-node tree came out of
  one `/tmp` python script with a PRE-FLIGHT CHECKER beside it (sprite on disk, roster stage and
  spriteFile agree, not dexOnly, rung transitions, out-degree, junk-edge shape, distinct earned
  energies, signature names unique against the whole file). The checker caught three signature
  collisions before a 23-second test run did, which is the right place to catch them.
- REMAINS: US-143 onward (29/56 passing). US-143 (Virus Busters / ZERO) is the LAST Pendulum tree
  and the last of the eleven device trees; US-144..169 are the 26 orphan sweeps over the remaining
  643. Two names US-143 must handle are already spent: `greymon`/`metalgreymon`/`wargreymon` are
  now THREE nodes each (dmc-v1, penc-nsp, penc-me), so its Agumon thread needs a fourth copy, and
  Garurumon's thread is already a triple.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-143 - Wire the Pendulum Color V0 Virus Busters / ZERO evolution tree

Authored `penc-vb` from nothing: 30 nodes, 270 -> 300. It is the LAST of the eleven device trees,
so every `### Version` section of `Resources/Digimon_Color_And_Pendulum_Color_Evolution_Trees.md`
now has a line in the graph, and Phase E's first half is done. Orphans 643 -> 628, 15 removed
(counted with Appendix B, after `python3 scripts/build_roster.py`).

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (+30 nodes), `Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json`
(+30 entries and a `penc-vb` lineDefault each), `Sources/DexModel.swift` (line title),
`Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift` (Power Meter), new `Tests/PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests.swift`
(27 tests), `docs/evolutions-schema.md`, and the eight-place knock-on list plus three marker tests.
Build green, 1921 tests, 0 failures, validator zero findings.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE FIRST TREE WITH NOTHING ABSENT.** All twenty-six names the section draws have a playable
  48x64 sheet, so no Wikimon stand-in and no rehomed rung were needed - the first since US-139.
  Five are filed under a spelling the document does not use, and the drift rules found every one:
  SnowBotamon/`YukimiBotamon` (a dub name, `find -iname '*snowbotamon*'` returns NOTHING),
  Salamon/`Plotmon` and Gatomon/`Tailmon` (bracketed by the document itself), Wizardmon/`Wizarmon`
  and Stefilmon/`Stiffilmon`. Two letters inside a word again - `Stefilmon` is not a substring of
  `Stiffilmon`, US-140's prefix-search lesson.
- **A DOCUMENT CAN DRAW ONE DIGIMON TWICE UNDER TWO NAMES.** The section draws
  "Angemon -> HolyAngemon -> Seraphimon" and "Wizardmon -> MagnaAngemon -> Cherubimon (Virtue)" -
  and MagnaAngemon IS HolyAngemon, the dub name, with ONE sheet between them. Wired as one node
  with two parents and two children (the `pencme_andromon` shape from US-142: one `isDefault`
  climb, one EARNED second climb). The check that catches this class of thing is the one this
  story added: sweep every `*mon` word out of the section's own text and assert each resolves to a
  playable roster entry under its own spelling or a recorded substitution. Do that instead of
  eyeballing the bullet list - it is what turned MagnaAngemon from a missing name into a duplicate.
- **HALF this tree is aliases, and that is what a LATE device tree costs.** Fifteen of thirty nodes
  are `pencvb_`, the worst ratio in the file, because the V0 device is the one every earlier tree
  borrowed from - Agumon, Gabumon and everything above them were spent by US-133/US-138/US-142
  before this story reached the tree that owns them. Both of the file's triples became QUADRUPLES.
  Expect the orphan yield of a tree to fall as Phase E goes on: 24 removed in US-142, 15 here.
- **The two triple-count marker tests fired exactly as designed, and cost nothing.** US-142's
  `testTheGreymonThreadIsDrawnByExactlyThreeTrees` and US-140's Garurumon equivalent both asserted
  a count with a "has a fourth copy" message; both broke on the first run and both were rewritten
  into the same claim one number higher. Keep writing them. US-138's Omegamon doc-comment ("the
  only tree that holds BOTH of that recipe's parents") was prose, not an assertion, and had to be
  found by hand - if a claim is worth writing, write it as XCTAssert.
- **The junk chain can be chosen for MEANING, not just for being spare.** Turuiemon ->
  Andiramon (Virus) -> Cherubimon (Vice) is the Lopmon line's fall, every arrow of it drawn by
  Wikimon, and its top is the counterpart of the Cherubimon (Virtue) this same document draws as an
  earned Mega - so neglecting a Virus Buster ends it as the thing the tree exists to fight. Two
  sheets of one Digimon, one earned and one junk, in ONE line, which no earlier tree had. Note the
  ONE arrow that is NOT canon: Turuiemon's earned way back up to Asuramon is flavour, and the
  node's `comment` says so rather than implying Wikimon draws it. Do not launder a choice as a
  citation.
- **`penc-vb` takes Power Meter, and the game table is now exactly 2 lines per game.** Twelve
  lines, six games, six pairs - the sharer dictionary in `MinigameAssignmentTests` is at its
  symmetric point. The 26 orphan sweeps (US-144..169) do not add lines, but if anything ever does,
  the next sharer makes a TRIPLE, and the tie-break is unchanged: fewest Digimon behind the game,
  flavour breaks ties.
- **The knock-on list is stable at eight places for the fifth tree running**, plus the two marker
  tests: `EvolutionGraphTests`' per-line count dict; `graph.nodes.count` in `ElementCatalogTests`
  AND `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; `EggHatchingTests`' seeded-Digitama set; `SeedRosterTests`'
  `seedLines`; `RosterTests`' exact alias list (sort order: `pencvb_` after `pencnso_`/`pencnsp_`,
  before `pencwg_`); `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` (both rungs); `MinigameAssignmentTests`'
  sharer map; `DexScreenTests`' line-title assertion. ONE more this story found:
  **`elements.json` and `moves.json` need a `lineDefaults` entry for the new line**, not only the
  per-id ones - `ElementCatalogTests.testEveryGraphLineHasALineDefault` and its moves twin.
- **The pre-flight checker beside the authoring script earned its keep a third time.** It caught
  eight signature-name collisions and one id that should not have been an alias at all (`filmon`
  was in no other line, so `pencvb_filmon` would have spent an alias and removed no orphan) before
  a 23-second test run could. Check "is this plain id already a node?" for EVERY node, not just the
  ones you expect to collide.
- REMAINS: US-144 onward (30/56 passing). The eleven device trees are done; US-144..169 are the 26
  orphan sweeps over the remaining 628, which by stage are Ultimate 166, Adult 129, Perfect 114,
  Child 88, Digitama 45, Baby II 37, Baby I 33, Armor-Hybrid 16.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-144 - Orphan sweep: Digitama A-K

The first of Phase E's 26 sweeps, and the first story since US-008 to open a line that is not a
device tree. 30 nodes, 300 -> 330. Digitama orphans 45 -> 23; whole-file orphans 628 -> 598 (the
extra 8 are the Baby I this sweep opened, which the Appendix B rule counts as connected the moment
they have an in-edge).

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (+30 nodes), `Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json`
(+30 entries and 5 `lineDefaults` each), `Sources/DexModel.swift` (5 line titles),
`Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift` (5 assignments), `Sources/EvolutionGraph.swift`
(`reachesUltimate(from:)`), `Sources/MainScreenModel.swift` (starting-egg filter), new
`Tests/DigitamaSweepTests.swift` (15 tests), `docs/evolutions-schema.md`, and TEN existing test
files. Build green, 1936 tests, 0 failures, validator zero findings.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE SWEEP'S RULE, and it is the one US-145..169 should reuse.** A sweep has no document, so
  what stands in for one is: (1) an egg whose species is ALREADY a node hangs off that species'
  line and hatches onto that line's Baby I, adding no rung at all; (2) an egg whose species is NOT
  in the graph opens a thread and brings its own Baby I, taken from Wikimon two hops down. Twelve
  of twenty-two went the first way and ten the second. The first way is what keeps the phase from
  producing dozens of one-node lines, which is an explicit acceptance criterion.
- **AUTHORING ONTO AN EXISTING LINE BREAKS SIX EARLIER STORIES' TESTS, and that is the real cost of
  this story.** 32 failures on the first run, every one of them an assertion that a line has ONE
  egg or has exactly N nodes. Budget for it: the fix is mechanical but it is ten files. The
  generalisation to make is "reachable from ANY egg of the line", and for a count, EXCLUDE the
  sweep's eggs by name (`$0.line == line && !sweepEggs.contains($0.id)`) rather than bumping the
  total — bumping it silently changes what the earlier story's notes claimed.
- **`EvolutionNode` has NO `comment` property.** The key is authored in `evolutions.json` and never
  decoded; a test that wants to grep a comment loads the raw JSON out of `Bundle.main` and reads
  `nodes[]["comment"]`, exactly as every Pendulum tree test already does. Cost one build.
- **The two ACs a Digitama sweep cannot meet literally, with the reasons, so US-145 need not
  re-derive them.** "Every Digimon in the range gets an in-edge" — nothing evolves INTO an egg.
  "No edge is unconditional" — `EggHatcher` ignores `conditions`, and with one hatch edge per egg a
  condition that WAS honoured could leave a player's only egg unable to hatch. Both are recorded in
  `notes` and both are stated as a test rather than left as prose.
- **Nine knock-on places, and the list is different from a device tree's.** `EvolutionGraphTests`'
  per-line dict; `graph.nodes.count` in `ElementCatalogTests` AND `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`;
  `EggHatchingTests`' candidate set; `MinigameAssignmentTests`' sharer map; `DexModel.lineTitles`;
  `MinigameAssignment.byLine`; `elements.json`/`moves.json` `lineDefaults`; `EvolutionTreeTests`'
  `dmc-v1` layout counts; and every tree test of a line the sweep touched. NOT on the list this
  time: `RosterTests`' alias list and `SeedRosterTests`' `seedLines` — a sweep authors PLAIN roster
  ids only (that is the entire point of it), so no alias is created and no seed line changes.
- **The pre-flight checker earned its keep for the fourth story running.** Roster stage vs authored
  stage, sprite on disk, dexOnly, one-rung transitions, CROSS-LINE edges, symbol+tint uniqueness
  within a line, signature-name uniqueness against the whole file, and `testElementsVaryWithinALine`
  (>1 element per line — easy to trip with a 2-node line). It came back clean first try and the
  only failures the build found were in OTHER stories' tests, which is where a checker cannot look.
- REMAINS: US-145 onward (31/56 passing). US-145 is the other half of the Digitama, 23 eggs for 25
  still-orphaned Baby I — read the allocation pattern at the top of this file BEFORE choosing
  targets, because doubling up an egg there permanently strands a Baby I. Orphans by stage now:
  Ultimate 166, Adult 129, Perfect 114, Child 88, Baby II 37, Baby I 25, Digitama 23, Armor-Hybrid 16.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-145 - Orphan sweep: Digitama L-Z

The second of Phase E's 26 sweeps, and the one that CLOSES the Digitama stage: 23 eggs wired, all
57 playable eggs now carry their single hatch edge. 35 nodes, 330 -> 365. Digitama orphans 23 -> 0;
Baby I 25 -> 13; whole-file 598 -> 563.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (+35 nodes), `Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json`
(+35 entries and 2 `lineDefaults` each), `Sources/DexModel.swift` (2 line titles),
`Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift` (2 assignments), new `Tests/DigitamaSweepLToZTests.swift` (15
tests), `docs/evolutions-schema.md`, and NINE existing test files. Build green, 1951 tests, 0
failures, validator zero findings.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE SWEEP'S RULE HAD TO BE TIGHTENED, and the arithmetic is what tightened it.** US-144's rule
  was "an egg whose species is already a node joins that species' line and adds no rung". That is
  the wrong default once the eggs are nearly gone: `EggHatcher.hatchTarget` reads
  `evolutions.first`, so an egg has ONE hatch edge and a Baby I's only possible in-edge is an egg.
  Every egg spent on an already-reachable Baby I is a Baby I nobody can ever hatch. The rule that
  ships is: **an egg opens the Baby I Wikimon puts two rungs below its species, and doubles up only
  when it has no choice** — and "no choice" is one of five checked facts, not a preference:
  species already wired (4), species idle-only (3), species has NO sheet at all (1, Liollmon), the
  species' own Baby I is idle-only (1, Meicoomon), every candidate Baby I is already in the graph
  (2, Phascomon and Vorvomon). `testEveryDoubledUpEggSaysWhyItHadNoChoice` checks each reason
  against the roster and the graph, so a lazy doubling cannot hide behind a comment.
- **PROVE THE CEILING BEFORE APOLOGISING FOR IT.** Twelve looks short against 25 orphaned Baby I,
  so the story computes the maximum instead of asserting one: build the bipartite graph of "egg's
  species descends from this Baby I" off Wikimon and find the largest matching. Only 13 of the 25
  are on a thread reaching any of these 23 species, and Leafmon and Pururumon are BOTH reachable
  only through `worm_digitama` — so 12 is the most any authoring could have opened. That number is
  now a test (`testTheBabyIStillOrphanedCannotBeReachedByAnyRemainingEgg`, paired with "no unspent
  egg exists"), which is what turns "we ran out" into a handover US-146 is told about.
- **A BABY I WHOSE BABY II IS ALREADY ON THE LINE IS WORTH TWO THAT ARE NOT.** `pipimon` went to
  `palmon` and `tsubumon` to `dmc-v3` because Tanemon and Tokomon are already those lines' Baby II,
  so US-147 closes those dead ends with an EDGE and no new node — and no new line was needed for
  either. Check `Baby I -> Evolves To` against the nodes already in the graph before opening a line;
  it is the cheapest line-count saving in the phase.
- **TWO NEW LINES FOR TWELVE THREADS, and grouping is what bought that.** Four of the twelve are
  Tamers partners (Lopmon, Monodramon, Renamon, Terriermon) and joined US-144's `tamers`, which is
  now 15 nodes. Five more share a device: Wikimon's **Virtual Pets section is machine-readable**
  (`<span class="mw-headline" id="Vital_Bracelet_Digital_Monster">`), so "these five are Vital
  Bracelet Digimon" is a checked fact and not a vibe — that is what `vital` is. Grouping by a
  franchise or a device you can VERIFY beats naming a line after each species.
- **Wikimon parsing, refined from US-144's recipe.** `re.split(r'<span class="mw-headline" id="([^"]+)"', html)`
  gives id/body pairs for the WHOLE page including h3/h4 — US-144's `<h2>` split misses
  `Evolves_From`/`Evolves_To`, which sit under h3, and silently returns empty lists. Read names out
  of `title="..."` and drop anything containing "Card Game" (the Digimon Card Game colour tables
  inject Greymon/Scumon/Koromon into every Evolves From list and they are not evolutions).
  **Fetch the middle rung's page, not the top one**: 50 `curl`s on the Baby II gave the whole
  Baby I -> Baby II -> Child map in one pass, which is what the matching needed.
- **A "one egg per line" assertion can survive US-144 and still bite.** `PendulumWindGuardiansTree
  Tests` seeded its reachability BFS from `flora_digitama` alone; US-144 generalised the other five
  tree tests and missed that one, because no egg had landed on `penc-wg` yet. When a story adds an
  egg to a line, grep that line's test file for BOTH the egg list and the BFS seed.
- **A ledger belongs in the newest story that changed it.** The whole-file dead-end list moved from
  `DigitamaSweepTests` to `DigitamaSweepLToZTests` (8 -> 20 entries) and US-144's version was
  narrowed to "my eight are still dead ends" with a pointer. The next sweep looks at the newest
  sweep; a ledger left in an older file gets edited by nobody.
- **US-144's marker test worked exactly as advertised** — `testTheDigitamaOrphansLeftAreExactly
  TheLToZOnesForUS145` failed on the first run of this story, explained itself, and was rewritten
  into the claim it guarded. Keep leaving them.
- REMAINS: US-146 onward (33/56 passing). US-146 is Baby I, and it inherits a HARD fact: 13
  playable Baby I can never be given an in-edge, because every Digitama is spent. Its AC "every
  Digimon in the range gets at least one in-edge" therefore cannot be met literally either — say
  which reading is taken, the way US-144 and US-145 both did. `ketomon` and `bommon` are the two
  Baby I whose canonical Baby II is idle-only and which need a stand-in from US-147. Orphans by
  stage now: Ultimate 166, Adult 129, Perfect 114, Child 88, Baby II 37, Armor-Hybrid 16, Baby I 13.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-146 (Orphan sweep: Baby I)

Wired the WHOLE Baby I rung. 38 new nodes and 33 new edges; `Resources/evolutions.json` 365 -> 403,
plus the matching rows in `elements.json`/`moves.json`, two new lines in `Sources/DexModel.swift`
and `Sources/MinigameAssignment.swift`, a new `Tests/DigitamaSweepBabyITests.swift` (16 tests), and
ELEVEN existing test files. Build green, 1967 tests, 0 failures, validator zero findings.

Orphan count for the stage: **Baby I 13 BEFORE, 0 AFTER.** Whole file 563 -> 525; Baby II fell
37 -> 12 as a side effect of authoring the rung above.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE STORY'S SCOPE WAS THE RUNG, NOT THE 13 NAMES.** The PRD's Appendix A lists 38 orphaned
  Baby I and US-144/US-145 de-orphaned 25 of them by giving them an in-edge from an egg — which
  left the OTHER half of the same AC ("and at least one out-edge") unmet on all 38. Reading the
  scope as "the 13 still orphaned today" would have shipped 20 Baby I that still lead nowhere and
  handed US-147 a rung it is not named for. When a sweep's range has been partly eaten by an
  earlier story, check WHICH criterion that story met before deciding what is left.
- **AN AC THAT CANNOT BE MET IS PINNED AS A LIST, NEVER RELAXED TO A SKIP.** 13 Baby I can never
  have a parent (all 57 eggs spent, one hatch edge each, and US-145 proved 12 was the ceiling), so
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.testEveryNonEggNodeIsReachableFromSomeDigitama` — a GLOBAL zero since
  US-008 — became a 21-name list: the 13, plus the 8 Baby II only they feed. It still fails on a
  22nd, and a second assertion proves each stranded Baby II has no reachable parent, so the list
  cannot quietly absorb a Baby II nobody bothered to wire. Same shape in the two device-tree
  reachability tests that gained a stranded node (`penc-ds` one, `penc-vb` two).
- **THAT GLOBAL REACHABILITY TEST IS THE ONE TO GREP FOR BEFORE AUTHORING, and it is not where you
  would look.** `EvolutionCriteriaTests`, not `EvolutionGraphTests`. The six `Pendulum*TreeTests`
  and five `DMC*TreeTests` each have a per-line twin (`testEveryNodeInTheLineIsReachableFrom...`),
  so a node with no in-edge breaks the test of WHATEVER LINE it lands on. That constraint, not
  flavour, is what decided most of this story's line assignments: eleven of the thirteen went onto
  sweep lines (`tamers`, `wanyamon`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`) or the two
  new ones, and only Puyomon and Pusumon had to touch a device line — because Pukamon and Herissmon
  are the only nodes on disk their threads can possibly reach.
- **A MISSING RUNG AT BABY II IS A REHOME ON THE RUNG ABOVE — fetch the Baby II's own page even
  though it is not on disk.** Wikimon has pages for Digimon the sprite pack lacks, so
  `curl wikimon.net/Gurimon` still yields "Evolves To: Koemon", and the stand-in is whichever Baby
  II ON DISK also evolves into Koemon (Wanyamon). Four of the thirteen went this way (Gurimon,
  Kyaromon-idle-only, Bosamon, Puyoyomon). One sweep of 37 `curl`s over every orphaned Baby II,
  parsed for `Evolves_From`/`Evolves_To`, answered every pairing question in the story AT ONCE —
  including which Baby I each Baby II wants — and US-147 can reuse the same dump.
- **Wikimon's `Evolves To` at Baby I can be a DigiXros list, not an evolution.** Bombmon's is three
  fusions (Mega Decker Greymon, Monochromon, Shoutmon X7) and no ordinary arrow at all, so it has
  no Baby II on any page. Its comment says FLAVOUR in capitals and a test greps for that word —
  the one honest way to author a pairing that has no citation. Do not let a fusion list read as an
  evolution because it is sitting under the right heading.
- **`graph.nodes(at: .babyI)` is 45 and the roster's playable Baby I is 43.** `piyo_yuramon` and
  `pencnsp_botamon` are line-scoped aliases — graph nodes with no roster entry of their own. Assert
  the SHAPE of a rung over graph nodes and its COVERAGE over roster entries; a test that iterates
  roster entries silently skips every alias.
- **The knock-on list for a rung this size, all eleven files, in the order they bit:** node count in
  `ElementCatalogTests` AND `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; line sizes in `EvolutionGraphTests`;
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`' game -> [lines] literal; `MoveCatalogTests` wants a UNIQUE
  symbol|tint per line AND a globally unique `signatureName` (three of mine collided with eggs
  authored five stories ago); `ElementCatalogTests.testElementsVaryWithinALine` forbids a
  single-element line, which a 2-node line trips instantly; and `EggHatchingTests`' two starting-egg
  lists move whenever a thread newly reaches an Ultimate.
- **FINISHING a thread promotes its egg, and the promotion is silent.** `lala_digitama` and
  `luce_digitama` became starting-egg candidates the moment Pipimon and Tsubumon got their Baby II,
  because Tanemon and Tokomon already reached an Ultimate. US-145 flagged those two as the cheap
  closes and it was right — they were the only two edges in the story that changed what a new game
  can start on.
- **A ledger belongs in the newest story that changed it, and this one MOVED UP A RUNG.** The
  whole-file dead-end list is now
  `DigitamaSweepBabyITests.testTheOnlyDeadEndsBelowUltimateAreTheBabyIIThisSweepOpened` — 25
  entries, all Baby II. US-144's and US-145's copies were flipped in place to "my Baby I are no
  longer dead ends", so wiring them back into leaves fails too.
- REMAINS: US-147 onward (33/56 passing). US-147 is Baby II and inherits a rung that is 25/37 done:
  every Baby II it needs to wire already has its in-edge, so its whole job is the out-edge to a
  Child plus the 12 Baby II still orphaned (`arkadimon_baby`, `budmon`, `chicchimon`, `cupimon`,
  `hiyarimon`, `kozenimon`, `meicoobaby`, `pokomon`, `sunmon`, `tokomon_x`, `torikaraballmon`,
  `upamon`). Eight of the 25 it wires onward are on the stranded list, so
  their Children will be unreachable too; that is expected and must NOT be authored away by
  inventing an in-edge. Orphans by stage now: Ultimate 166, Adult 129, Perfect 114, Child 88,
  Armor-Hybrid 16, Baby II 12, Baby I 0.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-147 (Orphan sweep: Baby II)

Wired the WHOLE Baby II rung. 51 new nodes (the 12 Baby II nobody had wired + the 39 Children the
rung now evolves into), 12 new branch edges at Baby I, 38 Baby II out-edges; `Resources/evolutions.json`
403 -> 454, plus the matching rows in `elements.json`/`moves.json`, a new `Tests/BabyIISweepTests.swift`
(19 tests) and TEN existing test files. NO new lines. Build green, 1986 tests, 0 failures, validator
zero findings.

Orphan count for the stage: **Baby II 12 BEFORE, 0 AFTER.** Whole file 525 -> 475; Child fell
88 -> 50 as a side effect of authoring the rung above.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE ONLY WAY TO GIVE A BABY II AN IN-EDGE IS TO BRANCH A BABY I, and that spends an invariant
  three stories old.** Every Baby I had exactly ONE edge from US-008 to US-146, and US-146 pinned
  that as a claim. Twelve Baby II had no parent and no Digitama is left to open a thread, so nine
  Baby I gained a second edge (Puttimon, Kuramon and Piyo's Yuramon a third). US-146's
  `testBabyIEdgesAreTheDefaultAndUnconditional` was rewritten into
  `testEveryBabyIsFallbackEdgeIsUnconditional` and the "exactly one edge" half MOVED to
  `BabyIISweepTests.testEveryBabyIThatBranchesDoesSoForAnOrphan`, which names the nine and fails if
  a tenth branch is authored for convenience. **The Child sweeps face the same shape one rung up** —
  a Child's only possible parent is a Baby II — so expect to branch a Baby II and to edit that test.
- **AN IN-EDGE FORCES THE LINE, and that is what decides where a sweep node lives — not flavour.**
  `testNoEdgeCrossesALine` means a Baby II sits on its parent's line and a Child on its Baby II's.
  Cupimon, Tokomon X and Upamon went onto `dmc-v3` because Puttimon and Tsubumon are the only
  parents Wikimon gives them, and Hiyarimon onto `penc-vb` for the same reason. **Touching a device
  line is the US-146 precedent and it costs four test edits every time:** the line's node count in
  `EvolutionGraphTests`, the `inLine.count` in that tree's
  `testEveryNodeInTheLineIsReachableFromItsDigitama`, and the `sweepEggs` exclusion set plus the
  `mine.count`/`plain.count` totals in its "N of the M nodes carry a plain roster id" test. That
  exclusion-by-name set is the mechanism those files already provide for exactly this — add the new
  ids to it rather than bumping the totals, or the story's own claim stops being the claim.
- **A SWEEP THAT OPENS A RUNG AS LEAVES BREAKS "EVERY CHILD HAS A JUNK FALLBACK".** Two device tree
  files (`PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests`, `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests`) run
  `XCTUnwrap(node.evolutions.first(where: \.isDefault))` over every Child on their line, and a
  brand-new leaf Child has no edges at all. Add `&& !node.evolutions.isEmpty` to the `where`. The
  Child sweeps will hit the mirror image at Adult.
- **AN EGG'S PROMISE IS A TEST, AND IT IS THE ONE THAT CAUGHT A REAL GAP.** US-144/145 hung 57 eggs
  on threads; a thread that never arrives at the egg's own species is a promise the file does not
  keep. `testTheEggsWhoseSpeciesThisRungReachesNowArriveAtIt` BFSes from twenty eggs to the Child
  they name and failed on `lala_digitama`, because Lalamon had been hung off Budmon and the egg
  opens Pipimon -> Tanemon. The fix was a second, cited parent (Tanemon -> Lalamon), not a smaller
  list. Run that BFS BEFORE choosing which parent gets a Child; the egg allocation is the constraint.
- **THE LINE-SCOPED ALIAS IS THE ANSWER WHEN A CITED TARGET BELONGS TO ANOTHER LINE.** Monimon's
  only Wikimon Child is Hagurumon, which is already `penc-me`'s, and `line` is single-valued — so
  `xros_hagurumon` is a second node on the same art, the `pencnsp_koromon`/`dmcv4_palmon` pattern.
  Cost: one entry in `RosterTests`' alias list (it asserts the EXACT set of graph ids with no roster
  entry) and a note that `Roster.bundled.entry(id:)` returns nil for it. The first attempt used
  Solarmon as a rehome instead and had to be undone: Wikimon's Virtual Pets section proved Solarmon
  is on no Xros device at all, which would have made the line's name a lie. **Check the device
  before the arrow.**
- **`Roster.bundled` (Resources/roster.json, sprite-derived) AND `roster.generated.json` ARE
  DIFFERENT SETS.** The generated file mirrors graph ids, so an alias appears in it; roster.json
  does not. Appendix B's orphan count reads the generated one; a test asserting a rung's roster
  count must use the bundled one (Baby II: 49 graph nodes, 47 roster entries).
- **Wikimon's `Evolves From` is EMPTY for more Digimon than you expect, and that is the honest
  FLAVOUR case.** Chicchimon, Kozenimon, Arkadimon (Baby) and Torikara Ballmon have no parent
  anywhere; Torikara Ballmon has neither direction. Each says FLAVOUR in capitals and a test greps
  for the word. What made the pairings defensible was a checkable fact from the page itself rather
  than a resemblance: Chicchimon's own `Evolves To` are already Children of the bird line, and
  Torikara Ballmon's Reference Book profile says it FLIES.
- **The knock-on list for this rung, all ten files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests` AND
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`; line sizes in `EvolutionGraphTests` AND `DigitamaSweepTests`
  (the older sweep pins `tamers`/`wanyamon` because that is where those lines were opened); the
  stranded list in `EvolutionCriteriaTests`; three of US-146's claims in `DigitamaSweepBabyITests`;
  the three Pendulum tree files above; and `graph.parents(of:) == [x]` assertions in
  `DMCVersion4TreeTests` and `SeedRosterTests`, which become `.contains(x)` the moment a node gains
  a second parent. `MinigameAssignmentTests` and `EggHatchingTests` did NOT move: no new line, and
  no thread newly reached an Ultimate.
- REMAINS: US-148 onward (34/56 passing). US-148..150 are the Child rung, and it is 39/89 done:
  every Child this story opened has its in-edge and needs an Adult, and the 49 still orphaned need
  both. Nine of the 39 are on the stranded list, so their Adults will be unreachable too; that is
  expected and must NOT be authored away by inventing an in-edge. The dead-end ledger is now
  `BabyIISweepTests.testTheOnlyDeadEndsBelowUltimateAreTheChildrenThisSweepOpened`, 39 entries, and
  the Child sweeps are meant to edit it down. Orphans by stage now: Ultimate 166, Adult 129,
  Perfect 114, Child 50, Armor-Hybrid 16, Baby II 0.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-148 (Orphan sweep: Child A-F)

Wired the A-F third of the Child rung. 43 new nodes — the 14 orphaned Children A-F, the 23 earned
Champions above the whole A-F range, and 6 junk Champions for the lines that had no Champion rung at
all — plus 14 new branch edges across 9 Baby II, and out-edges on the 9 Children US-147 had opened
as A-F leaves. `Resources/evolutions.json` 454 -> 497, the matching rows in `elements.json` /
`moves.json`, a new `Tests/ChildSweepAToFTests.swift` (22 tests) and NINE existing test files. NO
new lines, and NO aliases — new nodes and orphans removed are the same number for the first time
since US-135. Build green, 2008 tests, 0 failures, validator zero findings.

Orphan count for the stage: **Child 50 BEFORE, 36 AFTER — Child A-F 14 BEFORE, 0 AFTER.**
Whole file 475 -> 432; Adult fell 129 -> 100 as a side effect of authoring the rung above.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A CHILD SWEEP IS THREE RUNGS OF WORK, NOT ONE, AND THE THIRD IS THE ONE NOBODY BUDGETS FOR.**
  Giving a Child an in-edge branches a Baby II (expected, US-147 said so). Giving it an out-edge
  costs a Champion — but `EvolutionCriteriaTests.testEveryNonTerminalChildAndAdultHasTwoToFiveOut
  goingEdges` means TWO out-edges, and `...FallsToAJunkEvolution` means one of them lands on a junk
  Champion of the Child's OWN line. Six lines (`algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon`, `penc-sw`,
  `tamers`, `wanyamon`) were Digitama-to-Child threads with no Champion rung at all, so each needed
  a junk floor invented before ANY of its Children could branch. That is 6 of the 29 Champions, and
  it is a fixed cost US-149 and US-150 will NOT pay again — every line those two touch now has one,
  except whatever they open. Check `graph.nodes.filter { $0.line == L && $0.stage == .adult }`
  before estimating.
- **JUNK CHAMPIONS CAN COME OUT OF THE ORPHAN POOL INSTEAD OF BEING ALIASES.** The obvious move was
  six line-scoped aliases (`pencme_raremon` precedent), which cost a `RosterTests` alias-list entry
  each and remove NO orphan. The roster still had six junk-flavoured Adults nobody had wired:
  Numemon X, Manekimon, Mimicmon, Troopmon, Damemon, Tsuchidarumon. Using them removed six orphans
  instead of none. `junkIds` is a TEST's list, not a validator rule — US-138/139/140/143 already set
  the precedent of picking a thematically-junk unused sheet — so the only real constraint is that
  the pick reads as junk. Search the orphan pool by flavour before reaching for an alias.
- **THE FOUR ENERGIES ARE A HARD CEILING OF FOUR BRANCHES PER BABY II, and it is what decides where
  a variant lives.** `BabyIISweepTests.testEachBabyIIsBranchesAskForADifferentEnergy` plus
  `EvolutionEngine`'s `dominant == requiredEnergy` filter means a Baby II can carry at most four
  edges, ever. Koromon and Pyocomon were both already full, which is why Agumon 2006 could not go on
  Agumon's own line and Elecmon Violet could not go on its only cited parent's. Run
  `{vitality,strength,spirit,stamina} - used` over every candidate parent BEFORE promising the AC's
  "variants hang off their base form's line" — the honest version is "with its base form OR with its
  variant thread", and `tokomon_x` (US-147's X-Antibody In-Training) took all three X-Antibody
  Children for exactly that reason.
- **A CHILD'S JUNK EDGE SHARES ITS EARNED EDGE'S ENERGY and sits below it on `minEnergy`.** That is
  the Agumon/Numemon shape from US-061 and it is REQUIRED reading: the distinct-energy rule is
  scoped to EARNED edges (`SeedRosterTests`, `BabyIISweepTests`), so a two-edge Child does not need
  two energies, and giving the junk edge its own energy would make it unreachable whenever the
  player's dominant type is the other one.
- **`SeedRosterTests.patamonLineVerifiedSet` IS A WHOLE-LINE CHECK ON `dmc-v3`, and any sweep that
  puts a Champion there trips it.** It reads "every Adult-or-later node on dmc-v3 is in the US-043
  verified set" — a list of DISPLAY NAMES, not ids. Four of US-148's Champions landed there because
  Tokomon X and Upamon are dmc-v3's. Add to the set with a note, the way KingEtemon was added in
  US-061; do not scope the check down.
- **`EvolutionTreeLayoutTests.testTheBundledVersionOneLineIsABranchingTree` pins the dmc-v1 LAYOUT,
  not just its size** — node count, the Adult column's id list IN ORDER, `rowCount` and the
  connector count. Four earlier stories added only Digitama and could leave the branch shape alone;
  the first story to hang a new Child off Koromon moved all four numbers. Anything that widens a
  device line's Adult column has to update it.
- **THE ADULT MIRROR OF US-147's CHILD GUARD LANDED EXACTLY WHERE US-147 PREDICTED.**
  `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests` runs "every Champion on this line falls to Darumamon" over
  `$0.stage == .adult`, and a brand-new leaf Champion has no edges at all; it needs
  `&& !$0.evolutions.isEmpty`. The Adult sweeps (US-151..153) will hit the Perfect version of this.
- **THE STRANDED LIST GREW BY TWO, AND ONLY TWO, BECAUSE `penc-sw` HAS NO DIGITAMA.** Fujamon was
  already stranded, so the two Champions hung over it are too. That is inherited arithmetic, not an
  omission — but it is worth checking BEFORE choosing a parent: `funbeemon`'s cited parent Puroromon
  is also stranded, and moving it to Tanemon (equally cited) kept a whole thread reachable for free.
  Look up `EvolutionCriteriaTests`' stranded lists while picking parents, not afterwards.
- **The knock-on list for this rung, all nine files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests` AND
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests` (454 -> 497); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`; line
  sizes in `DigitamaSweepTests` AND `BabyIISweepTests`; `junkIds` and the stranded lists in
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests`; the dmc-v1 layout in `EvolutionTreeTests`; the dmc-v3 verified set in
  `SeedRosterTests`; and three places in `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests`. Plus the
  `greymon_x` example in BOTH `MoveCatalogTests` and `ElementCatalogTests`, which US-138's own
  learning had predicted: **a test that needs "something OUTSIDE the graph" must DERIVE it.** Both
  are now `roster.entries.first { catalog[...] == nil && graph.node(id:) == nil }`.
  `MinigameAssignmentTests` and `EggHatchingTests` did NOT move: no new line, and no thread newly
  reached an Ultimate (every new Champion is a leaf).
- **The authoring script pattern is worth repeating.** `/tmp/us148/author.py` held the whole story
  as data — parents, energies, conditions, comments, elements, moves — and REFUSED TO WRITE until
  it had checked, in one pass: no id already a node, no edge crossing a line, no Baby II branching
  twice on one energy, no repeated symbol|tint within a line, no repeated `signatureName` globally,
  and no digit in any hint. It caught three duplicate signature names before a single byte hit the
  repo. Splice `evolutions.json` textually (mixed encoding, see US-136), and note that the nine
  US-147 leaves are matched on their literal `"evolutions": []` line, which makes the replacement
  a one-line regex per node.
- REMAINS: US-149 onward (35/56 passing). US-149 (Child G-L) and US-150 (Child M-Z) face the same
  three-rung shape; the dead-end ledger is now
  `ChildSweepAToFTests.testTheOnlyDeadEndsBelowUltimateAreTheOnesTheSweepsHaveOpened`, 59 entries —
  30 Children for US-149/US-150 and 29 Champions for US-151..US-153 — and both halves are meant to
  be edited down. Orphans by stage now: Ultimate 166, Perfect 114, Adult 100, Child 36,
  Armor-Hybrid 16.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-149 (Orphan sweep: Child G-L)

Wired the G-L third of the Child rung. 51 new nodes — the 18 orphaned Children G-L, 31 earned
Champions and 2 junk Champions (`xros` and `vital` were the last two lines with no Adult rung at
all) — plus 18 new branch edges across 15 Baby II, and out-edges on the 14 Children US-147 had
opened as G-L leaves. `Resources/evolutions.json` 497 -> 548, the matching rows in `elements.json` /
`moves.json`, a new `Tests/ChildSweepGToLTests.swift` (23 tests) and TWELVE existing test files.
NO new lines, and NO aliases, so new nodes and orphans removed are the same number.
Build green, 2031 tests, 0 failures, validator zero findings; the 23 new tests also observed passing
on their own.

Orphan count for the stage: **Child 36 BEFORE, 18 AFTER — Child G-L 18 BEFORE, 0 AFTER.**
Whole file 432 -> 381; Adult fell 100 -> 67 as a side effect of authoring the rung above.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **`roster.generated.json` CONTAINS THE LINE-SCOPED ALIASES AND `Roster.bundled.entries` DOES NOT,
  so a range counted off the generated file is wrong by exactly the aliases in it.** Scoping this
  story off `roster.generated.json` gave 45 G-L Children; the test, which reads
  `Roster.bundled.entries`, gave 43 — `pencvb_gabumon` and `xros_hagurumon` are nodes on borrowed
  art with no roster entry. One of them (`xros_hagurumon`) was IN scope and had to be swept, so
  `sweptChildren` is deliberately not a subset of the range and there is a separate test saying so.
  Use the generated file to count ORPHANS (it mirrors the graph, which is what the Appendix B rule
  needs) and `Roster.bundled` to define a RANGE.
- **A DEVICE TREE PINS ITS OWN In-Training's BRANCH LIST AND EDGE COUNT, and a sweep that hangs one
  more Child off that Baby II breaks a test with nothing to do with counts or lines.** Two fired
  here: `SeedRosterTests.testPagumonBranchesToBothRookiesAndEachReachesUltimate` spells Pagumon's
  targets out as a sorted list, and `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests.testTheInTrainingRungIs
  UnconditionedBecauseTheUnlockableRookieHasNoSheet` asserts Peti Meramon has exactly three edges
  and that NONE is conditioned — which a sweep's earned branch necessarily is. The fix for the
  second is to scope the claim to the three Rookies the TREE draws rather than to the rung; the
  tree still conditions nothing. `grep -rn '<parent-id>' Tests` before choosing a device-tree
  Baby II as a parent, not after.
- **THE "EVERY CHAMPION OF THIS LINE FALLS TO THE JUNK PERFECT" LOOP NEEDS `&& !$0.evolutions.isEmpty`
  IN EVERY DEVICE-TREE FILE A SWEEP TOUCHES.** US-148 fixed Nightmare Soldiers; US-149 had to fix
  Virus Busters and Metal Empire the same way, because a sweep always leaves the rung above as
  leaves. Wind Guardians and Deep Savers still have the unguarded version and will fail the moment
  a sweep puts an Adult on them — which US-150 will, for `penc-ds`.
- **A HISTORICAL CLAIM STOPS BEING CHECKABLE THE MOMENT A LATER STORY WRITES TO THE SAME FILE — say
  so and keep the half that survives.** `ChildSweepAToFTests.testEachLineThatHadNoChampionRungGained
  AJunkFloor` asserted every Adult on its six lines was one US-148 authored, which WAS how "the line
  had nothing before" got checked from the file. US-149 put sixteen more Champions on `tamers`
  alone, so the assertion is now `authoredAdults.contains(junk)` — the junk floor is still one that
  story authored — and the "there was nothing here before" half moved into the comment and the
  notes. Do not delete such a check silently; replace it with what is still true and record why.
- **CHECK THE STRANDED LISTS BEFORE PICKING A PARENT — one substitution bought two reachable nodes
  for nothing here.** Gammamon's only free citable parent looked like Pusurimon, which is in
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests`' stranded set; Hiyarimon is on the SAME line (penc-vb), equally free, and
  not stranded, so Gammamon and BetelGammamon are reachable rather than being two more names on the
  list. Gaossmon could not be saved the same way — all three `xros` Baby II are stranded, because
  that line has no Digitama and US-144/145 spent all 57 eggs — so the list grew by exactly one Child
  and six Champions, every one of them hanging off something already on it.
- **`adventure02` IS THE LAST LINE WITHOUT A CHAMPION RUNG, AND IT IS US-150's.** Its three Children
  — V-mon, Wormmon, Tinkermon — are all M-Z, so US-150 must invent a junk Adult for it before any of
  them can branch, exactly as US-148 did for six lines and US-149 for `xros` and `vital`.
  `ChildSweepGToLTests.testTheLastTwoLinesWithoutAChampionRungGainedAJunkFloor` states it as a
  one-element list that US-150 either empties or fails.
- **THE JUNK-FALLBACK RULES ARE SCOPED TO Child AND Adult, NOT TO EVERY BRANCHING NODE.** The
  authoring script's first run rejected 61 shipped Perfects for having a gated `isDefault` edge —
  which is correct data: `EvolutionCriteriaTests.branchingNodes` is `child || adult`, and the
  Perfect rung's fallbacks legitimately carry criteria. A pre-write check copied from the test has
  to copy its scope too.
- **THE FOUR-ENERGY CEILING IS WHAT DECIDES WHERE AN X-ANTIBODY CHILD LIVES, and eight of them
  landed in one story.** Six sat on their base form's own In-Training. Gabumon X and Gomamon X
  could not — Tokomon X is full since US-148 and Pukamon is the ONLY In-Training the whole `penc-ds`
  line has — so both joined the X-Antibody thread on dmc-v3, the escape US-148 used for Dracomon X.
  Kokuwamon X is the case worth remembering: Caprimon is full too, but `penc-me` has a SECOND
  In-Training (Kozenimon), so the variant kept its base form's LINE without keeping its parent.
  "Hangs off its base form's line" is satisfiable far more often than "hangs off its base form's
  parent" — check the line for another Baby II before rehoming.
- **The knock-on list for this rung, all twelve files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests` AND
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests` (497 -> 548); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`; line
  sizes in `DigitamaSweepTests`, `BabyIISweepTests` AND `ChildSweepAToFTests`; `junkIds` and BOTH
  stranded lists in `EvolutionCriteriaTests`; the dmc-v3 and dmc-v5 verified sets in
  `SeedRosterTests` plus its Pagumon branch list; the earned-branch count and the wired-onward
  ledger in `BabyIISweepTests`; `inLine.count` and the story-scope `sweepEggs` set in
  `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests`, `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests` and
  `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests`; and the line count in `DMCVersion5TreeTests`, excluded by NAME
  rather than bumped so "US-137 added nothing" stays the claim it was.
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `EggHatchingTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and the two `lineDefaults`
  did NOT move: no new line, and no thread newly reached an Ultimate.
- **The authoring-script pattern earned its keep again.** `/tmp/us149/author.py` + `data.py` held
  the whole story as data and refused to write until it had checked, in one pass: every id is a
  playable roster entry at the right rung, no id is already a node, no edge crosses a line or skips
  a rung, no edge points at a dexOnly Digimon, no Baby II branches twice on one energy, no Child or
  Adult has fewer than two or more than five out-edges or more than one fallback, no fallback is
  gated, no hint is blank or contains a digit, no repeated symbol|tint within a line, and no
  repeated `signatureName` globally. It caught a real collision before a byte hit the repo —
  Greymon 2010's "Mega Burst" was already GeoGreymon's.
- REMAINS: US-150 onward (36/56 passing). US-150 (Child M-Z) faces sixteen leaves and eighteen
  orphans, plus `adventure02`'s junk floor. The dead-end ledger is still
  `ChildSweepAToFTests.testTheOnlyDeadEndsBelowUltimateAreTheOnesTheSweepsHaveOpened`, now 78
  entries — 16 Children for US-150 and 62 Champions for US-151..US-153 — and both halves are meant
  to be edited down. Orphans by stage now: Ultimate 166, Perfect 114, Adult 67, Child 18,
  Armor-Hybrid 16.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-150 - Orphan sweep: Child M-Z (the rung is finished)

Wired the M-Z third of the Child rung. 51 new nodes: the 18 orphaned Children M-Z and the 33
Champions above them. 18 new branch edges across 14 Baby II, and out-edges on the 16 Children
US-147 opened as M-Z leaves. `evolutions.json` 548 -> 599.

- Files: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`, new
  `Tests/ChildSweepMToZTests.swift` (26 tests), and 17 existing test files for counts and for
  three historical claims that stopped being checkable.
- Build green. 2057 tests, 0 failures. Validator zero findings over the whole file. The 26 new
  tests were also observed passing on their own.
- ORPHAN COUNT (Appendix B, over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`): whole file 381 -> 330.
  Child 18 BEFORE, 0 AFTER. Adult fell 67 -> 34 as a side effect of authoring the rung above.
  Remaining: Ultimate 166, Perfect 114, Adult 34, Armor-Hybrid 16.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **`care.battleCount` is answerable ONLY over the `lifetime` window, and every other `care.*`
  counter ONLY over `stage`.** `ConditionContext.careValue` returns `.unknown` for
  `(.careBattleCount, .stage)`, so four edges first authored with `"window": "stage"` on a battle
  criterion were UNREACHABLE rather than merely hard. It was caught by
  `BabyIISweepTests.testEveryBabyIIBranchIsTakenByTheEngineWhenItIsEarned` — the engine test, not
  the validator, which has no opinion about windows. `ChildSweepMToZTests` now pins the rule over
  the whole file.
- **An egg's promise is worth re-running when a sweep WIRES a species an earlier egg doubled up
  for.** US-145 parked `meicoo_digitama`, `phasco_digitama` and `vorvo_digitama` on someone else's
  Baby I because their own species had no node; this story gave all three a node, and choosing
  Phascomon's parent by that BFS (Kozenimon on `penc-me`, its cited Caprimon's line) rather than by
  flavour (Sunmon on `penc-nso`) made all three eggs arrive at their species. The cost was moving
  Solarmon onto its other cited parent, Gigimon, on `tamers`. `DigitamaSweepLToZTests`' two "the
  species is still unwired" guards were replaced by the arrival check they were deferring.
- **A device tree's In-Training claim is the thing a Child sweep breaks, and scoping beats
  relaxing.** `PendulumNatureSpiritsTreeTests.testTheUnlockableSixthSlotIsTheOnlyEarnedInTrainingEdge`
  read "Koromon's ONLY conditioned edge is Angoramon"; hanging YukiAgumon there falsifies it. It is
  now scoped to the three Rookies the SECTION draws, plus an assertion naming the one extra target
  — so a fourth Rookie hung there silently still fails.
- **Three historical claims were replaced rather than bumped, and each says why in its comment.**
  US-149's "every Adult on `vital`/`xros` is one US-149 authored" (ten more landed there; the junk
  FLOOR half survives); the Nature Spirits one above; and `DexScreenTests`' "the roster dwarfs the
  graph" — 599 nodes against 1,025 entries is past half, so the floor is now the 157 idle-only
  Digimon, which can NEVER gain a node because `edgeToDexOnlyNode` forbids it. That last one had
  already been rewritten once from `> 800`; a claim Phase E keeps eroding needs a floor Phase E
  cannot reach.
- **The variant rule again, and the better of the two escapes.** Eight of nine variants sat on
  their base form's line and three on its own In-Training. Shakomon X could not — `penc-ds` has
  exactly ONE In-Training and Pukamon carries all four energies, the trap US-149's Gomamon X hit —
  but instead of a flavour rehome it followed its OTHER Wikimon-cited parent, Chocomon, onto
  `tamers`. Prefer a second citation over a rehome: it is checkable.
- **The knock-on list for this rung, all seventeen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests` and `ChildSweepGToLTests` (548 -> 599);
  the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`; line sizes in `DigitamaSweepTests`,
  `BabyIISweepTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests` and `ChildSweepGToLTests`; `junkIds` and BOTH stranded
  lists in `EvolutionCriteriaTests`; the dmc-v3 verified set in `SeedRosterTests`; the
  earned-branch count and the wired-onward ledger in `BabyIISweepTests`; the dead-end ledger in
  `ChildSweepAToFTests`; `inLine.count` and the `sweepEggs` set in `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTree
  Tests`, `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests`, `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests` and
  `PendulumNatureSpiritsTreeTests`; the doubled-up-egg reasons in `DigitamaSweepLToZTests`; and the
  roster/graph proportion in `DexScreenTests`. `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `EggHatchingTests`,
  `DexModel.lineTitles` and the two `lineDefaults` did NOT move: no new line, and no thread newly
  reached an Ultimate.
- REMAINS: US-151 onward (37/56 passing). The Adult rung is next and it is the same shape one rung
  up: 34 orphaned Adults over seven stories, and 95 dead ends in
  `ChildSweepAToFTests.testTheOnlyDeadEndsBelowUltimateAreTheOnesTheSweepsHaveOpened` — the Child
  half is now EMPTY and the Adult half is 95 Champions for US-151..US-156 to wire onward. Note the
  arithmetic the Adult sweeps face: the Perfect rung has 114 orphans and only 95 Adults to hang
  them off, so doubling up starts there.
---

## 2026-07-22 - US-151 - Orphan sweep: Adult A-D
Wired the seven playable Champions whose display name begins A-D that had NO edge at all:
Akatorimon, BlackGaogamon, BlackTailmon, Burgermon Mama, Burgermon Papa, DarkLizamon, Deckerdramon.
Each gained one earned in-edge from a Child of its own line and one earned out-edge to a Perfect of
that line, plus the line's unconditioned junk fallback. Orphans 330 -> 319 (Appendix B over a
regenerated `roster.generated.json`): Adult 34 -> 27, Perfect 114 -> 110. 599 -> 610 nodes.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (7 new Champions, 4 new Perfects, 7 new Child branches),
`Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json` (11 entries each), new
`Tests/AdultSweepAToDTests.swift` (18 tests), and the knock-on edits listed below.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **The Adult rung's scope reading is NOT the Child rung's, and the criteria say so.** US-148..150
  read "in-edge AND out-edge on every Digimon in range" as the rung-and-range and swept dead ends
  too. US-151's criteria say "every remaining ORPHAN at stage Adult whose displayName starts A-D",
  and the 95 leaves US-149/US-150 left are not orphans - they have an in-edge. So this story owns
  only the seven with no edge at all, and the 95 stay in
  `ChildSweepAToFTests.testTheOnlyDeadEndsBelowUltimateAreTheOnesTheSweepsHaveOpened` for
  US-152..US-156. Doing it the other way would have meant 95 new Perfects in one iteration.

- **THE PERFECT RUNG IS WHERE THE FILE RUNS OUT, and it is the Adult sweeps' version of the junk
  floor problem US-148/US-149 hit one rung down.** An Adult's out-edge must land on a Perfect of
  its OWN line (`testNoEdgeCrossesALine`, plus a per-line boundary test in all eleven device-tree
  files), and `EvolutionCriteriaTests` demands a junk fallback drawn from `junkIds`. Nine lines
  still have no Perfect at all: `wanyamon` and `tamers` were opened here (BlackMachGaogamon +
  Karakurumon, MegaloGrowmon + CatchMamemon), leaving `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`,
  `commandramon`, `diablomon` and `penc-sw` for the sweeps that need them. Budget TWO nodes per
  such line: the earned branch and the junk floor under it, and add the floor to `junkIds`.

- **`tamers` is the line to open early and this story did.** It is the largest in the file (71
  nodes) and holds 22 more leaf Champions; every one of them will fall to CatchMamemon.

- **A `parent` for an Adult is almost always a Child an earlier sweep pinned at "exactly two
  edges".** `ChildSweepGToLTests` and `ChildSweepMToZTests` both assert
  `node.evolutions.count == 2` over their swept lists, and Gaomon and Monodramon are on them. The
  fix is the scoping the Codebase Patterns already prescribe: a named exception dictionary
  (`["gaomon": 3]`) rather than dropping the equality, so a Child that grows a third branch nobody
  wrote down still fails.

- **Two of a device tree's Perfects are pinned by an EXACT parent set, not a superset.**
  `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests.testAndromonIsTheOneNodeThatJoinsTwoOfTheDocumentsThreads` and
  `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests.testHolyAngemonCarriesBothOfTheDocumentsDrawingsOfIt` both do
  `XCTAssertEqual(Set(graph.parents(of:)))`. Hanging a swept Champion onto either one falsifies
  them; both were rescoped by NAMING the third parent and saying which arrow it is, since the claim
  each makes is about the document's two drawings.

- **`Roster.bundled` is `Resources/roster.json` (1,022 entries) and is NOT
  `roster.generated.json` (1,025).** The generated mirror carries three line-scoped aliases the
  shipped file does not. Count a story's range off the SHIPPED roster when the number goes into a
  test - Appendix B's orphan count is the generated one, and the two disagree (46 vs 41 playable
  Adults A-D).

- **The blanket "did everything right" `met` context cannot take an `atMost` edge.** Two edges here
  are gated on FEW training sessions and SHORT nights, and the shared fixture every sweep copies
  sets both high. `AdultSweepAToDTests.context(for:)` derives the context from the edge's own
  conditions instead - copy that helper rather than loosening a criterion to fit the fixture.

- **Wikimon wikitext beats the rendered page.** `curl -s "https://wikimon.net/index.php?title=<Page>
  &action=raw"` gives the exact `==Evolves From==` / `==Evolves To==` bullet lists; a summarised
  fetch of the HTML drops and invents entries. Redirects show up as `#REDIRECT [[Real Page]]`
  (DarkLizamon -> Dark Lizamon, BlackGaogamon -> Black Gaogamon).

- **A rung can be unwireable rather than merely missing, and `dexOnly` is why.** All three of
  Burgamon Adult's Wikimon parents are unusable - Ebi Burgamon has no sheet, Tyumon and Burgamon
  are idle-only, and `edgeToDexOnlyNode` forbids an edge to an idle-only Digimon. The rehome went
  to `dmc-v4` because the FILE already holds that family: Torikara Ballmon (whose only canon
  relatives anywhere are the two Burgamon Adult) is a Baby II of that line and Digitamamon, a cited
  Evolves To, is its Perfect. When the parent rung cannot exist, argue from the line the rest of
  the family is already on.

- **A class-level citation is a real citation and is checkable.** Deckerdramon's whole Evolves From
  on Wikimon is "Any Blue Lv.3 Digimon from the Digimon Card Game", and its Evolves To gives "Any
  Digimon that also Evolves from Cyborg Lv.4" - Andromon is reached here from Guardromon, this
  line's Cyborg Champion, so the out-edge satisfies the clause literally and the test asserts that
  parent edge exists. Say in the `comment` which half is cited and which is flavour.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all fifteen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests` and
  `ChildSweepMToZTests` (599 -> 610); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`; line sizes in
  `DigitamaSweepTests`, `BabyIISweepTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests` and `ChildSweepMToZTests`;
  `junkIds` in `EvolutionCriteriaTests`; the dead-end ledger in `ChildSweepAToFTests` (95 -> 99);
  the "exactly two edges" claim in `ChildSweepGToLTests` and `ChildSweepMToZTests`; Muchomon's
  exact targets in `DMCVersion4TreeTests`; `inLine.count` in `PendulumWindGuardiansTreeTests`,
  `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests` and `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests` plus the `sweepEggs` set in the
  latter two and the line-node count in the first; the exact parent sets in
  `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests` and `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests`; and BOTH the verified set and
  the Champion split in `SeedRosterTests`. `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `EggHatchingTests`,
  `DexScreenTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and the two `lineDefaults` did NOT move: no new line, and
  the DexScreen floor is now the 157 idle-only Digimon, which Phase E cannot reach.

- REMAINS: US-152 onward (38/56 passing). Six Adult sweeps are left and they hold the 27 orphaned
  Champions E-Z; the 95 leaves in the dead-end ledger are theirs too, and the seven lines still

## 2026-07-22 - US-152 - Orphan sweep: Adult E-G
Wired the five playable Champions whose display name begins E-G that had NO edge at all: Ebidramon,
FlareLizamon, Gawappamon, Growmon Orange, GulusGammamon. Each gained one earned in-edge from a Child
of its own line and one earned out-edge to a Perfect of that line, plus the line's unconditioned junk
fallback. Orphans 319 -> 314 (Appendix B over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`): Adult 27 -> 22,
and NO other bucket moved. 610 -> 615 nodes.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (5 new Champions, 5 new Child branches, 0 new Perfects),
`Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json` (5 entries each), new
`Tests/AdultSweepEToGTests.swift` (20 tests), and the knock-on edits listed below.
Full suite 2095 tests green (2075 before), build green.

The five, with the citation each rests on:
  ebidramon      penc-ds  shakomon    -> anomalocarimon        (Pendulum COLOR 2 Deep Savers)
  gawappamon     penc-ds  gomamon     -> pencds_megaseadramon  (Wikimon Da-199 + plain Evolves To)
  flarelizamon   tamers   clearagumon -> megalogrowmon         (closes US-151's half-drawn arrow)
  growmon_orange tamers   guilmon     -> megalogrowmon         (both edges cited; variant, no rehome)
  gulusgammamon  penc-vb  gammamon    -> holyangemon           (Pendulum COLOR ZERO Virus Busters)

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **AN ADULT SWEEP CAN COST NOTHING AT THE PERFECT RUNG, and checking that FIRST is what makes it a
  five-node story instead of a nine-node one.** US-151 had to open two Perfect rungs; this story
  opened none, because every one of the five had a cited Perfect that was ALREADY on the line the
  citation put it on. The order that produced that: fetch the orphan's Wikimon `Evolves From` AND
  `Evolves To` together, intersect BOTH against the graph, and only then choose the line. Choosing
  the line off the parent alone is what forces a new Perfect later.

- **A HANDOVER CLAIM IS A TEST, AND WHEN THE NEXT STORY HONOURS IT THE TEST FLIPS RATHER THAN DIES.**
  US-151 wrote `testMegaloGrowmonsOtherCitedParentIsLeftForTheEToGSweep`, asserting
  `graph.node(id: "flarelizamon") == nil`. Wiring FlareLizamon necessarily broke it. The fix is not
  to delete it: it became `...WasPickedUpByTheEToGSweep`, asserting MegaloGrowmon's exact parent set
  is now `[darklizamon, flarelizamon, growmon_orange]`. Same fact, other side, still fails if a later
  story quietly hangs a fourth parent there. Leave the next sweep a claim of the same shape.

- **WHEN THE BOLDED WIKIMON PARENT IS idle-only, TAKE THE NEXT CITED PARENT, NOT A REHOME.** Kamemon
  is the bolded name in Gawappamon's `Evolves From` and is `dexOnly` in this pack, which
  `edgeToDexOnlyNode` forbids - the identical trap US-151 hit with Burgamon and had to rehome out
  of. Here Gomamon was three bullets further down the SAME list and is already `penc-ds`'s own
  Rookie, so the citation survived intact and the line argument never had to be made. Read the whole
  Evolves From before deciding a rung is unwireable.

- **`Set(graph.parents(of:))` EQUALITY IS THE FRAGILE ASSERTION AT THIS RUNG, and there are now
  three of them.** `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests.testHolyAngemonCarriesBothOfTheDocumentsDrawingsOf
  It` went two -> three (US-151) -> four (US-152) parents; `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests`' Andromon
  one and US-151's own MegaloGrowmon one are the others. Each time the fix is to NAME the new parent
  and say which arrow it is in the comment, since the claim is about the document's own drawings and
  not about a count. `grep -rn 'Set(graph.parents' Tests` before choosing an out-edge target.

- **THE `sweepEggs` ESCAPE HATCH IS THE STANDARD WAY TO ADD A NODE TO A DEVICE LINE.** Every device
  tree file ends with a "the N orphans this story removed" test whose `mine.count` is the line minus
  a `sweepEggs` set of ids later stories parked there. Adding to that set (rather than bumping the
  count) keeps the tree's own claim about its own thirty-one nodes true. Both files touched here
  wanted it: `penc-ds` took `ebidramon`/`gawappamon`, `penc-vb` took `gulusgammamon`.

- **A Child at THREE earned branches is one short of the ceiling, and that is worth asserting rather
  than remembering.** Shakomon and Gomamon now carry three apiece (four energy types is the hard
  ceiling, per `SeedRosterTests`' distinct-energy rule). `AdultSweepEToGTests.testEveryChildThisStory
  BranchedStillUsesDistinctEnergies` pins the 3 so the next sweep prices a fourth honestly instead of
  discovering the ceiling by failing.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all thirteen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, `AdultSweepAToDTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests`
  and `ChildSweepMToZTests` (610 -> 615); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`; line sizes in
  `DigitamaSweepTests`, `BabyIISweepTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests`,
  `ChildSweepMToZTests` and `AdultSweepAToDTests` (`tamers` 71->73, `penc-ds` 34->36, `penc-vb`
  43->44); the "exactly two edges" exception dict in `ChildSweepAToFTests` (new, `clearagumon`) and
  `ChildSweepGToLTests` (`gammamon`, `guilmon`); `inLine.count` plus `sweepEggs` in
  `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests` and `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests`; and HolyAngemon's exact parent
  set. `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`, the dead-end ledger, `MinigameAssignmentTests`,
  `EggHatchingTests`, `DexScreenTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and both `lineDefaults` did NOT move:
  no new line, no new node at Perfect or above, and no thread newly reached an Ultimate.

- REMAINS: US-153 onward (39/56 passing). Four Adult sweeps hold the 22 orphaned Champions H-Z, then
  twelve Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one. The seven lines still with no Perfect
  rung - `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon`, `penc-sw` - are
  untouched, and the 99 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end ledger are still owed an out-edge
  by whichever story claims them.

## 2026-07-22 - US-153 - Orphan sweep: Adult H-L
Wired the THREE playable Champions whose display name begins H-L that had no edge at all:

and one earned out-edge to a Perfect of that line, plus the line's unconditioned junk fallback.
Orphans 314 -> 311 (Appendix B over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`): Adult 22 -> 19, and NO
other bucket moved. 615 -> 618 nodes.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (3 new Champions, 3 new Child branches, 0 new Perfects),
`Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json` (3 entries each), new
`Tests/AdultSweepHToLTests.swift` (20 tests), and the knock-on edits listed below.
Full suite 2115 tests green (2095 before), build green.

The three, with the citation each rests on:
  kausgammamon  penc-vb  gammamon -> pencvb_weregarurumon  (Pendulum COLOR ZERO Virus Busters, both
                                                            arrows; its Wikimon family is literally
                                                            "Virus Busters")
  kinkakumon    penc-ds  jellymon -> zudomon               (Vital Bracelet BE, both arrows)
  kougamon      penc-wg  mushmon  -> jyureimon             (D-alpha-508 + Digimon Story: Sunburst &
                                                            Moonlight, both arrows)

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE PRD'S PER-LETTER ESTIMATES ARE STALE, AND CHECKING THE REAL RANGE IS THE FIRST THING TO DO.**
  The AC says "roughly 25 orphaned Adult"; there were three. The estimate was taken when the rung
  held 168 orphans, and eleven device trees plus three Child sweeps had already spent 146 of them.
  Run Appendix B and bucket by first letter BEFORE planning the story — US-154..US-156 hold 19
  between them (M-R 9, S-T 5, U-Z 5), not the ~75 the descriptions imply.

- **TWO CITED LINES IS A REAL CHOICE, AND THE TIEBREAK IS THE RUNG ABOVE.** Kinkakumon is an Oni of
  the Journey-to-the-West set and Wikimon cites Fujamon and Takinmon, both `penc-sw` Children, to
  *Pendulum COLOR 6 Saiyu Warriors* — the thematically right home. It also cites Jellymon below and
  Zudomon above to *Vital Bracelet BE*, and both of those were already on `penc-ds`. The first
  reading costs an earned Perfect plus a junk floor under it (`penc-sw` has NO Perfect rung, the bill
  US-151 paid twice); the second costs nothing. Took the second, wrote the first into the node
  `comment`, and pinned it from both ends in `testKinkakumonTookTheCitedLineThatAlreadyHadAPerfect
  Rung`: Fujamon and Takinmon still do not reach it, and `penc-sw` still has no Perfect. That test
  FLIPS the day someone opens that rung, which is the point.

- **A CHILD IS FULL AT THREE EARNED BRANCHES, AND US-153 FILLED ONE.** Gammamon now carries
  BetelGammamon (spirit), GulusGammamon (strength) and KausGammamon (stamina) plus its junk
  fallback. Four energy types is the ceiling `EvolutionEngine` imposes — a fourth earned branch
  cannot be told apart from one of the three — so `ChildSweepGToLTests`' `branchedByALaterSweep`
  entry for `gammamon` is at 4 and can never move again. Said out loud in
  `testEveryChildThisStoryBranchedStillUsesDistinctEnergiesAndGammamonIsFull` so US-154, which has
  WezenGammamon (the last of the four Gammamon Champions) in range, prices the problem before it
  starts rather than discovering it as a failing test: **WezenGammamon cannot hang off Gammamon
  even though Gammamon is its bolded cited parent** — every energy is spoken for. The way out is
  already on the page and was checked while writing this: `Wezen Gammamon`'s `Evolves From` also
  cites **Gabumon** to *Pendulum COLOR ZERO Virus Busters*, and `pencvb_gabumon` is on the same
  line with room left. Prefer that second citation to a rehome, the US-150 rule.

- **THE BOLDED `Evolves To` IS NOT ALWAYS THE ONE TO TAKE.** KausGammamon's is Canoweissmon, which
  has a full Perfect sheet on disk and no node — taking it would have spent a Perfect for nothing,
  because WereGarurumon is cited on the SAME page to the SAME device and was already on the line.
  The arrow NOT taken is named in the comment and pinned in
  `testTheGammamonThreadsLeftForTheLaterSweepsAreStillOpen`, which fails the day Canoweissmon is
  wired and makes whoever wires it say which arrow it is.

- **`PendulumWindGuardiansTreeTests`' UNGUARDED "every Champion falls to the junk Perfect" LOOP
  SURVIVED, and the reason is worth knowing.** The Codebase Patterns section warns it "fails the
  moment a sweep puts an Adult on them". It did not, because a sweep Adult carries a junk fallback
  BY CONSTRUCTION — `EvolutionCriteriaTests` demands one. What actually breaks that loop is an Adult
  with NO edges at all, which is what a Child sweep produces and an Adult sweep does not. Deep
  Savers and Wind Guardians can still be broken by a future story that authors a leaf Champion.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all fourteen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, `AdultSweepAToDTests`, `AdultSweepEToGTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`,
  `ChildSweepGToLTests` and `ChildSweepMToZTests` (615 -> 618); the per-line dict in
  `EvolutionGraphTests` (`penc-ds` 36->37, `penc-wg` 33->34, `penc-vb` 44->45) and the same three in
  `AdultSweepAToDTests` and `AdultSweepEToGTests`; `inLine.count` plus `sweepEggs` in
  `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests`, `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests` and `PendulumWindGuardiansTreeTests`
  (Wind Guardians had no `sweepEggs` set at all and got one rather than a bumped total);
  `branchedByALaterSweep` in `ChildSweepGToLTests` (`gammamon` 3 -> 4); Zudomon's exact parent set in
  `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests` (a FOURTH `Set(graph.parents(of:))` equality — the pattern note's
  count of three is now four); and Jellymon's row in that file's per-Rookie reachability table.
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`, the dead-end ledger (still 99), `MinigameAssignmentTests`,
  `EggHatchingTests`, `DexScreenTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and both `lineDefaults` did NOT move:
  no new line, no new node at Perfect or above, and no thread newly reached an Ultimate.

- REMAINS: US-154 onward (40/56 passing). Three Adult sweeps hold the 19 orphaned Champions M-Z,
  then twelve Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one. The seven lines still with no
  Perfect rung - `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon`, `penc-sw` -

The nine, with the citation each rests on:
  meramon_x      tamers   blucomon       -> grademon         (Digital Monster X Ver.3, both arrows)

  pegasmon_x     tamers   lopmon_x       -> grademon         (Digital Monster X Ver.3, both arrows)
  pteranomon_x   tamers   monodramon     -> mametyramon      (Bx-42/Da-484 in, Bx-43 out)

                                                              "Any Yellow Lv.5" CLASS citation)
  nefertimon_x   penc-vb  plotmon_x      -> pencvb_angewomon (Bx-98/DMX Ver.2 in, St-445 out)
  morishellmon   penc-ds  ganimon        -> anomalocarimon   (Digimon World 2, BOTH arrows)
  musyamon       penc-nso picodevimon    -> vamdemon         (DSSM in, Bo-214 out)
