**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **AN ADULT SWEEP CAN COST TWO PERFECTS AND STILL BE CHEAP, IF THE CITATIONS PAIR UP.** Four of the
  nine are X-Antibody Champions of the `tamers` X thread, and EVERY Perfect any of them cites is a
  sheet on disk with no node - Cyberdramon X, Mamemon X, OmegaShoutmon X, Angewomon X, Hisyaryumon,
  Monzaemon X, Triceramon X, MegaloGrowmon X, Andromon, Blossomon. US-152's "intersect both ends"
  rule finds nothing there, so the rung above HAD to open. The move that made it two nodes instead
  of four was to intersect the four orphans' `Evolves To` lists **with each other** before choosing:
  Grademon is in Meramon X's AND Pegasmon X's, both to Digital Monster X Ver.3; Mametyramon is
  Bx-43, the card that fuses Monochromon X and Pteranomon X, so both pages cite it from their own
  side. **Do the pairwise intersection across the story's own range, not just orphan-by-orphan
  against the graph.** US-157 onward have twelve Perfect and Ultimate sweeps where the same trick
  applies, and the X thread is where it pays.

- **A LINE THAT ALREADY HAS A JUNK FLOOR MAKES A NEW PERFECT COST ONE NODE, NOT TWO.** The two-node
  bill US-151 paid twice (earned Perfect + junk floor + the floor into `junkIds`) is only owed by a
  line with NO Perfect rung. `tamers` got CatchMamemon in US-151, so Grademon and Mametyramon cost a
  node each and `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` did not move. Check for the floor before pricing.

- **PLOTMON IS FULL, AND PICO DEVIMON WAS ALREADY FULL WHEN THIS STORY USED IT.** Plotmon now carries
  Tailmon (vitality), Wizarmon (spirit), BlackTailmon (strength) and Mikemon (stamina) plus junk:
  five edges, the ceiling `EvolutionCriteriaTests` sets, and all four energies spent. Pico Devimon
  had only strength left and its junk edge to Gokimon is ALSO gated on strength - that is the Scumon
  arrangement US-133 recorded, not a collision, because the earned edge asks 60 and the junk one 0.
  `AdultSweepMToRTests.testMusyamonSharesStrengthWithPicoDevimonsJunkEdgeAndStillWins` proves both
  halves through the engine. **An energy shared with the junk fallback is legal; an energy shared
  with another EARNED branch is not.**

- **A CLASS CITATION IS THE ANSWER WHEN EVERY NAMED ARROW IS UNUSABLE, AND IT IS PINNABLE FOUR WAYS.**
  Mikemon's whole `Evolves To` is unreachable in this pack: Bastemon and Betsumon have no sheet,
  Majiramon is idle-only (`edgeToDexOnlyNode` forbids it), Zudomon is on `penc-ds` where no cited
  parent of Mikemon lives. The same page's "Any Yellow Lv.5 Digimon from the Digimon Card Game" is
  a real citation - US-151's Deckerdramon reading - and Plotmon is a Yellow Lv.3 with Angewomon a
  Yellow Lv.5 above it, so ONE line satisfies both halves of the clause. The test asserts the two
  absent sheets are still absent, Majiramon is still `dexOnly` and Zudomon is still `penc-ds`, so
  the day any of those changes the story is told to revisit.

- **A HISTORICAL "this line has exactly N Perfects" COUNT ROTS; SCOPE IT TO THE NAMES.**
  `AdultSweepAToDTests.testTheTwoLinesWithoutAPerfectRungGainedAJunkFloor` asserted `tamers` had
  exactly two Perfects. US-154 opened two more without touching US-151's pair, so a count failed on
  work that did nothing wrong. Replaced with `wanyamon`'s exact pair plus a superset check on
  `tamers` - the half that stays true - which is the same repair US-149 made to
  `ChildSweepAToFTests`' "this line had no Champion before".

- **`testEveryNodeInTheLineIsReachableFromItsDigitama` CARRIES ITS OWN `inLine.count`, SEPARATE FROM
  THE `sweepEggs` TEST.** Four device-tree files failed on it after the data landed, and it is NOT
  the closing "the N orphans this story removed" assertion the notes list - it is a second count in
  a different test in the same file. `grep -n 'inLine.count' Tests` alongside `grep -n sweepEggs`.

- **WEZENGAMMAMON IS US-156's, NOT US-154's.** US-153's handover note said it was an M-R orphan; its
  display name starts with W, so it is U-Z. The advice it carried is still right and still needed:
  Gammamon is full at four energies, so WezenGammamon cannot hang there and must take the Gabumon
  citation (`pencvb_gabumon`, same line). `AdultSweepMToRTests.testThePerfectSheetsLeftForTheLater
  SweepsAreStillUnwired` re-pins Gammamon's edge count at 4 so that stays true until US-156 acts.
  **Derive a handover's range from the roster, not from memory of the letter bands.**

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all seventeen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, `AdultSweepAToDTests`, `AdultSweepEToGTests`, `AdultSweepHToLTests`,
  `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests` and `ChildSweepMToZTests` (618 -> 629); the per-line
  dict in `EvolutionGraphTests` (`tamers` 73->79, `penc-vb` 45->47, `penc-ds` 37->38, `penc-nso`
  42->43, `penc-wg` 34->35) and the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows in `AdultSweepAToDTests`,
  `AdultSweepEToGTests`, `AdultSweepHToLTests`, `BabyIISweepTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`,
  `ChildSweepGToLTests`, `ChildSweepMToZTests` and `DigitamaSweepTests`; `branchedByALaterSweep` in
  all three Child sweeps (`blucomon` 3, `guilmon_x` 3, `lopmon_x` 3, `monodramon` 3->4,
  `plotmon_x` 3); `sweepEggs` AND `inLine.count` in `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests`,
  `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests`, `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests` and
  `PendulumWindGuardiansTreeTests`; the dead-end ledger in `ChildSweepAToFTests` (99 -> 101, the two
  new Perfects); and `AdultSweepAToDTests`' Perfect-count claim, rescoped. `EvolutionCriteriaTests.
  junkIds`, its stranded lists, `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `EggHatchingTests`, `DexScreenTests`,
  `DexModel.lineTitles` and both `lineDefaults` did NOT move: no new line, and no thread newly

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (5 new Champions, 5 new Child branches, 1 new Perfect),
`Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json` (6 entries each), new
`Tests/AdultSweepSToTTests.swift` (22 tests), and the knock-on edits listed below.
Full suite 2159 tests green (2137 before), build green.

The five, with the citation each rests on:
  saberdramon   dmc-v4    muchomon  -> megadramon     (Da-511 in, Digimon World -next 0rder- out)
  shimaunimon   penc-nso  bakumon   -> mammon         (Digimon World 2, BOTH arrows)
  siesamon_x    tamers    dorumon   -> grademon       (Digital Monster X Ver.3, both arrows)
  tyrannomon    dmc-v1    agumon    -> mamemon        (Digital Monster Ver. 1, both arrows)
  tyrannomon_x  dmc-v3    agumon_x  -> metalgreymon_x (Digital Monster X, both arrows; NEW Perfect)

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **US-133's "Tyranomon has no colour sheet at all" WAS WRONG, and the reason is worth the note more
  than the fix is.** `DMCVersion1TreeTests.testTheTwoUndrawableNamesAppearNowhere` had carried, since
  the very first device tree, that the Version 1 document's Tyranomon could not be drawn - only
  `Black and White Sprites/Adult/Tyranomon.png` existed. The pack spells the COLOUR sheet with two
  n's: `Adult/Tyrannomon.png`, roster id `tyrannomon`, playable, animated. So the arrow was drawable
  the whole time and Agumon shipped with four of the document's five Champions for twenty-two
  stories. The test is now `testTheOneUndrawableNameAppearsNowhereAndTyranomonIsASpelling` and pins
  BOTH halves - the one-n id must never be a node (it would duplicate art), and the two-n one must be
  playable and on this line. Betamon is genuinely still idle-only. **Wikimon's spelling is not the
  pack's; resolve every name through the roster's display names before believing an absence.**

- **FOUR OF FIVE PLACEMENTS COST NOTHING ONE RUNG UP, WHICH IS THE HIGHEST RATE OF THE FIVE ADULT
  SWEEPS, AND IT IS NOT LUCK.** US-152's rule - intersect `Evolves From` AND `Evolves To` against the
  graph before choosing the line - gets CHEAPER as the file fills, because more Perfects are nodes
  each time. Saberdramon had sixteen cited parents and twenty-odd cited children and exactly one line
  held a node at both ends. ShimaUnimon's Bakumon and Mammon are both cited to Digimon World 2, one
  source for both arrows. Do the intersection before pricing anything; the orphan-by-orphan version
  is enough at this point and US-154's pairwise-across-the-range trick was not needed once.

- **A SWEEP CAN FILL THREE ROOKIES AT ONCE, AND THE KNOCK-ON REACHES THE SEED TESTS.** Agumon,
  Bakumon and Muchomon each spent their LAST free energy here (four earned branches plus junk = five
  edges, the `EvolutionCriteriaTests` ceiling). That is expected late in the rung - a Rookie with one
  energy left is exactly the one whose line already holds both ends - but Agumon is the seed, so its
  branch list is pinned in FIVE places outside the sweep files: `SeedRosterTests` (twice),
  `EnergyBarsTests` (which asserted vitality had NOTHING to reach for), `DexScreenTests`,
  `ConditionRevealTests` and `EvolutionTreeTests` (node count, Adult column, rowCount AND connector
  count). `grep -rn '"agumon"' Tests` before branching a seed Rookie.

- **`SeedRosterTests`' per-line verified-available SETS are a third knock-on family nobody listed.**
  `patamonLineVerifiedSet` (dmc-v3) and `piyomonLineVerifiedSet` (dmc-v4) are closed lists of display
  names that every Adult-and-up node on those lines must be in - US-148 through US-151 appended to
  them, and so did this story. They are the record of which sheets were actually eyeballed, so append
  with a comment naming the sweep; never relax the containment check.

- **AN ADULT'S JUNK ENERGY MUST MATCH ITS DOMINANT FOR `evolutionTarget`, BUT NOT FOR
  `scheduledEvolutionTarget`.** A first draft of `AdultSweepSToTTests` asserted a neglected vitality
  Agumon X falls to Scumon through `EvolutionEngine.evolutionTarget` and got `nil`: that entry point
  matches on the dominant energy, and Scumon's junk edge is on strength. US-154's Musyamon test
  worked only because its junk edge and its dominant were the same energy. The path the app actually
  takes is `scheduledEvolutionTarget`, which falls to `isDefault` whatever the dominant is - use that
  for every "neglect" assertion and keep `evolutionTarget` for the earned ones.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all sixteen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, `AdultSweepAToDTests`, `AdultSweepEToGTests`, `AdultSweepHToLTests`,
  `AdultSweepMToRTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests` and `ChildSweepMToZTests`
  (629 -> 635); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests` (`dmc-v1` 29->30, `dmc-v3` 46->48, `dmc-v4`
  26->27, `penc-nso` 43->44, `tamers` 79->80) and the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows in
  `AdultSweepAToDTests`, `AdultSweepEToGTests`, `AdultSweepMToRTests`, `BabyIISweepTests`,
  `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests`, `ChildSweepMToZTests` and `DigitamaSweepTests`;
  `branchedByALaterSweep` in `ChildSweepAToFTests` (`agumon_x` and `dorumon`, both 2->3); `sweepEggs`
  AND `inLine.count` in `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests`; Grademon's exact parent set in
  `AdultSweepMToRTests` (a FIFTH `Set(graph.parents(of:))` equality); the dead-end ledger in
  `ChildSweepAToFTests` (101 -> 102, the one new Perfect); `targets(of:)` for Agumon in
  `DMCVersion1TreeTests` and for Muchomon in `DMCVersion4TreeTests`; the two verified-available sets
  and Agumon's branch list in `SeedRosterTests`; and the Agumon rows in `ConditionRevealTests`,
  `DexScreenTests`, `EnergyBarsTests` and `EvolutionTreeTests`. `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`,
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `EggHatchingTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and both `lineDefaults` did
  NOT move: no new line, and the one new Perfect is a leaf, so no thread newly reached an Ultimate.

- REMAINS: US-156 onward (42/56 passing). ONE Adult sweep holds the last five orphaned Champions
  (U-Z: V-dramon Black, WezenGammamon, XV-mon Black, Xiquemon, Youkomon - pinned as still-unwired in
  `AdultSweepSToTTests.testTheFiveChampionsLeftForUS156AreStillUnwired`, which also re-pins Gammamon
  at four edges so US-156 is still told to take the `pencvb_gabumon` citation for WezenGammamon).

  102 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end ledger are still owed an out-edge by whichever story

## 2026-07-22 - US-156 - Orphan sweep: Adult U-Z (the Adult rung is finished)
Wired the LAST FIVE playable Champions with no edge at all: V-dramon Black, WezenGammamon, XV-mon
Black, Xiquemon and Youkomon. Each gained one earned in-edge from a Child of its own line and one
earned out-edge to a Perfect of that line, plus the line's unconditioned junk fallback. THREE new
Perfects were opened, one each on `penc-vb`, `dmc-v4` and `tamers`. Orphans 294 -> 286 (Appendix B
over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`): **Adult 5 -> 0 — the bucket is empty, the first rung
above Child to be finished** — AND Perfect 107 -> 104. 635 -> 643 nodes.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (5 new Champions, 5 new Child branches, 3 new Perfects),
`Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json` (8 entries each), new
`Tests/AdultSweepUToZTests.swift` (26 tests), and the knock-on edits listed below.
Full suite 2185 tests green (2159 before), build green, validator zero findings.

The five, with the citation each rests on:
  v-dramon_black  penc-wg  pencwg_piyomon -> aerov-dramon   (out-edge cited 8 cards incl. Bo-1113;
                                                             in-edge is a LINE argument, said so)
  xv-mon_black    penc-wg  mushmon        -> aerov-dramon   (St-768 in, Bo-935/Bo-1113 out)
  wezengammamon   penc-vb  gammamon       -> canoweissmon   (Ghost Game 12 + Pendulum COLOR ZERO
                                                             Virus Busters in, GG26/VB/BT10-011 out)
  xiquemon        dmc-v4   piyomon        -> huankunmon     (Digimon New Century, BOTH arrows)
  youkomon        tamers   renamon        -> blackrapidmon  (nine citations in, Digimon
                                                             Championship out)

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **"GAMMAMON IS FULL" WAS WRONG FOR THREE STORIES, AND THE BUG IS IN WHICH COUNT YOU READ.** US-153
  recorded Gammamon as full at "three earned branches plus the junk fallback"; US-154 and US-155
  both forwarded that as advice, and `AdultSweepHToLTests` pinned it as
  `Set(gammamon.evolutions.compactMap(\.requiredEnergy)).count == 3`. The node had spirit, strength
  and stamina earned and a junk edge on spirit — so vitality was free the whole time. The ceiling is
  FOUR EARNED BRANCHES (one per `EnergyType`) plus the fallback, five edges, which is exactly what
  Plotmon has carried since US-154. **`evolutions.filter { !$0.isDefault }.compactMap(\.requiredEnergy)`
  compared against `Set(EnergyType.allCases)` is the only honest test of fullness**; distinct
  energies over ALL edges under-counts by one whenever the junk edge shares, which it usually does.
  US-156 drew the bolded Ghost Game arrow instead of the stand-in, corrected the claim in US-153's
  own test file rather than deleting it, and left `pencvb_gabumon` the vitality it was told to spend.
  Cost: one test run to notice, ten minutes to fix, and a better citation than the handover offered.

- **THE AC'S "A VARIANT HANGS OFF ITS BASE FORM'S LINE" CAN OUTRANK THE ONLY CITATION THERE IS, AND
  IT IS THE RIGHT CALL WHEN THE OTHER END PAYS FOR IT.** V-dramon Black's whole Wikimon `Evolves
  From` is Guilmon and Guilmon X, both `tamers` — and `tamers` holds NOT ONE of its cited children,
  so US-152's intersection is empty there and taking the citation costs a Perfect on a line with no
  claim on the Digimon. `penc-wg` is the opposite: no source draws Piyomon into it, but AeroV-dramon
  is cited eight cards over, is already a Perfect there, and the base V-dramon and RedV-dramon both
  hang off the same Rookie. **Price both readings before taking the cited one**, and when the
  in-edge ends up resting on a line argument, WRITE "LINE argument" into the comment and grep for it
  in a test — this story does, so the day someone finds a real citation they know what they are
  replacing.

- **TWO ORPHANS OF ONE STORY SHARING A TARGET IS US-154'S PAIRWISE TRICK, AND IT LANDS ON A CARD.**
  Bo-1113 draws AeroV-dramon out of V-dramon (Black) *with or without* XV-mon (Black): one card,
  both of this story's variants, one existing Perfect, zero nodes above. That is two of five
  placements free. Different ENERGIES are what keep them from being the same branch twice (spirit
  off Piyomon, stamina off Mushmon), and a test asserts the pair is distinct rather than assuming it.

- **A REJECTED READING THAT IS THE BETTER THEME IS THE ONE MOST WORTH PINNING.** Xiquemon belongs on
  `penc-sw` — Fujamon and Kamemon are cited to *Pendulum COLOR 6 Saiyu Warriors*, which IS that
  line, and Huankunmon/Sagomon/Sanzomon are the same device's Perfects. It lost only on cost:
  `penc-sw` has no Perfect rung, so that reading is three nodes plus a `junkIds` entry against
  `dmc-v4`'s two. US-153's Kinkakumon set this precedent and this story kept it — the rejected
  reading is in the node `comment` AND pinned four ways
  (`testThePencSwReadingOfXiquemonIsStillTheCheaperOneNotTaken`: `penc-sw` still has no Perfect,
  Fujamon is still on it, Kamemon and Falcomon 2006 are still idle-only). Whoever opens `penc-sw`'s
  Perfect rung is TOLD Xiquemon is a rehome candidate.

- **BOTH OF A DIGIMON'S BOLDED PERFECTS CAN BE IDLE-ONLY, AND THEN THE CITED ALTERNATIVE IS THE
  ANSWER, NOT A CLASS CITATION.** Youkomon's canonical thread is Doumon and Taomon; both exist only
  in `Idle Frame Only/` and `edgeToDexOnlyNode` forbids either edge. BlackRapidmon is cited to
  *Digimon Championship* — the same game that draws three of Youkomon's parents — and `tamers`
  already carries Terriermon, Terriermon X and Galgomon, so the new Perfect lands on a line with a
  claim on it beyond the single arrow. A test asserts both bolded names are STILL idle-only, so the
  day either gains an animated sheet the placement is re-opened.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all nineteen files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, all six `AdultSweep*Tests` and all three `ChildSweep*Tests`
  (635 -> 643); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests` (`penc-wg` 35->37, `penc-vb` 47->49,
  `dmc-v4` 27->29, `tamers` 80->82) and the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows in `AdultSweepAToDTests`,
  `AdultSweepEToGTests`, `AdultSweepHToLTests`, `AdultSweepMToRTests`, `AdultSweepSToTTests`,
  `BabyIISweepTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests`, `ChildSweepGToLTests`, `ChildSweepMToZTests` and
  `DigitamaSweepTests`; `branchedByALaterSweep` in `ChildSweepGToLTests` (`gammamon` 4->5) and
  `ChildSweepMToZTests` (`renamon` 3); `earnedCounts["pencwg_piyomon"]` 3->4 and `mushmon` 3->4 in
  `AdultSweepMToRTests`/`AdultSweepHToLTests`; `sweepEggs` AND `inLine.count` in
  `PendulumWindGuardiansTreeTests` (35->37) and `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests` (47->49);
  `targets(of: "piyomon")` in `DMCVersion4TreeTests`; `piyomonLineVerifiedSet` AND the line's
  `champions.sorted()` in `SeedRosterTests`; the dead-end ledger in `ChildSweepAToFTests`
  (102 -> 105, the three new Perfects); and THREE handover tests flipped rather than deleted —
  `AdultSweepHToLTests`' Gammamon claim (corrected), `AdultSweepMToRTests`' and `AdultSweepSToTTests`'
  "still unwired" pins (now "wired, and on this parent"). `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`, its
  stranded lists, `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `EggHatchingTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and both
  `lineDefaults` did NOT move: no new line, and all three new Perfects are leaves.

- REMAINS: US-157 onward (43/56 passing). **The Adult rung is DONE — no story after this one needs
  to touch it.** Twelve Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one hold the remaining 286
  orphans: 104 Perfect, 166 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid. The seven lines still with no Perfect rung —
  `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon`, `penc-sw` — are untouched
  and are pinned as a set in `AdultSweepUToZTests.testWhatTheAdultRungHandsToThePerfectSweeps`. The
  105 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end ledger are still owed an out-edge by whichever story
  claims them; Galgomon (BlackRapidmon's obvious second parent), Greymon X and now Canoweissmon,
  Huankunmon and BlackRapidmon are among them.

## 2026-07-22 - US-157 - Orphan sweep: Perfect A-C (the first sweep at the Perfect rung)
Wired the NINETEEN playable Perfect whose display name begins A-C that had no edge at all. Each
gained one earned in-edge from a Champion of its own line and one `isDefault` climb into an Ultimate
of that line. TEN cost nothing above; the other NINE opened an Ultimate that had no node anywhere.
Orphans 286 -> 257 (Appendix B over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`): **Perfect 104 -> 84 and
Ultimate 166 -> 157**. 643 -> 672 nodes.

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (19 new Perfects, 9 new Ultimates, 1 new junk Perfect, 19 new
Champion branches and 9 new junk-floor edges), `Resources/elements.json` and `Resources/moves.json`
(29 entries each), new `Tests/PerfectSweepAToCTests.swift` (25 tests), the throwaway-but-kept
authoring script `scripts/us157_author.py`, and the knock-on edits listed below.
Full suite 2210 tests green (2185 before), build green, validator zero findings.

The nineteen, with the citation each rests on:
  andiramon_data        penc-vb   turuiemon           -> cherubimon_vice      (BOTH bolded)
  angewomon_x           penc-vb   tailmon_x           -> ophanimon_x  NEW     (bolded in, cited out)
  anomalocarimon_x      penc-ds   ebidramon           -> aegisdramon          (NO CITATION, LINE x2)
  archnemon             penc-nso  dokugumon           -> piemon               (both cited)
  astamon               penc-me   porcupamon          -> pencme_venomvamdemon (bolded in, cited out)
  atlurkabuterimon_red  penc-nsp  pencnsp_kabuterimon -> heraklekabuterimon   (BOTH bolded)
  baalmon               tamers    icedevimon          -> beelzebumon   NEW    (both cited)
  blackmegalogrowmon    tamers    blackgrowmon        -> chaosdukemon  NEW    (BOTH bolded, St-731/Bo-550)
  bluemeramon           penc-nso  pencnso_meramon     -> pencnso_boltmon      (both cited, zero cost)
  boutmon               penc-me   thunderballmon      -> kazuchimon    NEW    (cited in, bolded out)
  cannonbeemon          palmon    waspmon             -> tigervespamon NEW    (BOTH bolded)
  cargodramon           penc-me   tankmon             -> pencme_mugendramon   (both cited)
  caturamon             penc-vb   pencvb_leomon       -> pencvb_saberleomon   (both cited)
  cerberumon_x          penc-me   raptordramon        -> pencme_wargreymon    (both cited)
  chimairamon           dmc-v1    airdramon           -> millenniumon  NEW    (BOTH bolded)
  chohakkaimon          penc-sw   hakubamon           -> shakamon      NEW    (cited in, bolded out)
  crescemon             tamers    lekismon            -> dianamon      NEW    (BOTH bolded)
  cryspaledramon        tamers    paledramon          -> hexeblaumon   NEW    (BOTH bolded)
  cyberdramon_x         penc-me   revolmon            -> pencme_mugendramon   (NO CITATION, LINE x2)

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A PERFECT SWEEP PAYS THE DEAD-END LEDGER DOWN, NOT UP, AND THAT IS THE WHOLE SHAPE OF THIS RUNG.**
  Every Champion sweep added leaves; this one removed nine. The reason is structural: a Perfect needs
  a Champion beneath it, and after six Adult sweeps most Champions ARE leaves — so the cheapest
  in-edge is almost always one that also clears a debt. `ChildSweepAToFTests`' ledger fell 105 -> 97
  (nine cleared, Pandamon added). Price the in-edge off the ledger FIRST: nine of nineteen came free
  that way, and each one that does saves a later story a whole edit.

- **BUT EVERY LEAF CHAMPION YOU BRANCH COSTS A JUNK FLOOR EDGE IN THE SAME BREATH.** A leaf has no
  `isDefault` edge because it has no edges; the moment it gains an earned branch,
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.testEveryNonTerminalChildAndAdultFallsToAJunkEvolution` requires one onto a
  junk Perfect of its OWN line. Eight of the nine floors already existed (`andiramon_virus`,
  `locomon` twice, `catchmamemon` four times, `jyagamon`); only `penc-sw` had none. Write the
  fallback in the same edit as the branch or the suite fails on the node you just wired.

- **`Roster.bundled` IS `Resources/roster.json`, WHICH IS ONE ENTRY PER SHEET — APPENDIX B'S 37 AND
  THE TEST'S 34 ARE BOTH RIGHT.** The script in Appendix B reads `roster.generated.json`, which
  mirrors `evolutions.json` and therefore carries the LINE-SCOPED ALIASES (`pencme_andromon`,
  `pencvb_angewomon`, `pencvb_asuramon` in this range alone). A range test written off
  `roster.entries` will disagree with the orphan count by exactly the number of aliases in the band.
  Use `Roster.bundled` for "every Digimon on disk is obtainable" and the generated file only for the
  Appendix B number, and say which is which in the test.

- **OPENING A LINE'S TOP RUNG PROMOTES ITS EGGS, AND `EggHatchingTests` IS WHERE THAT SHOWS UP.**
  `MainScreenModel.startingDigitamaId` filters candidates on `graph.reachesUltimate`, so giving
  `tamers` its first four Ultimates turned FIVE Digitama (Guil, BlackGuil, Imp, Lop, Bluco) from
  unraisable into legal starting eggs in one edit. This is the first promotion since US-146 that came
  from the TOP of a thread rather than the middle. Any Ultimate sweep that opens a rung on `wanyamon`
  — the last line with Perfects and no Mega — should expect the same and grep
  `reachesUltimate` before assuming the egg lists are inert.

- **`penc-sw`'s PERFECT RUNG COST EXACTLY THE THREE NODES US-153 AND US-156 QUOTED, AND PAYING IT
  FLIPS FOUR OLDER TESTS RATHER THAN DELETING THEM.** Cho-Hakkaimon + Shakamon + the junk floor
  Pandamon + one `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` entry. The knock-on nobody listed:
  `AdultSweepHToLTests.testKinkakumonTookTheCitedLineThatAlreadyHadAPerfectRung` and
  `AdultSweepUToZTests.testThePencSwReadingOfXiquemonIsStillTheCheaperOneNotTaken` both asserted the
  rung was still SHUT, and `testWhatTheAdultRungHandsToThePerfectSweeps` pinned `penc-sw` in the
  no-Perfect set. All three were flipped, not removed — they now name Kinkakumon and Xiquemon as live
  rehome candidates, which is the record those stories were trying to leave. **Neither was rehomed
  here, deliberately**: a rehome drags a Champion, its Perfect, its Rookie's energy budget and four
  device-tree tests across a line, and that is a story of its own.
  ALSO: the whole line stays STRANDED (`penc-sw` has no Digitama), so all three new nodes joined
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests`' stranded list in two new groups, `strandedPerfect` and `strandedUltimate`,
  with the same "parents are all stranded too" loop the rungs below use.

- **A PERFECT'S CLIMB IS ITS `isDefault` EDGE, AND THAT IS THE HOUSE STYLE — DO NOT PUT CONDITIONS ON
  IT.** Every Perfect in this file since US-134 carries one edge: `isDefault`, `requiredEnergy`,
  `minEnergy 150`, `maxCareMistakes 2`, NO conditions. `EvolutionCriteriaTests.branchingNodes` filters
  to Child and Adult, so the 2..5 ceiling and the junk-floor rule do NOT apply at this rung — a
  single-edge Perfect is legal and is what the file already had 81 of. The AC's "no edge is
  unconditional" binds the EARNED edges, which is the reading every rung below recorded; a condition
  on an `isDefault` edge is data that lies, because US-020 takes it whatever the gates say.

- **THE 29-NODE EDIT WAS SCRIPTED, AND THAT IS SAFE ONLY BECAUSE THE JSON ROUND-TRIPS EXACTLY.**
  `json.dumps(d, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)` reproduces `evolutions.json`, `elements.json` and
  `moves.json` byte-for-byte (no trailing newline). Verify that first, then author from a table —
  hand-editing 29 nodes across three files invites exactly the drift these tests exist to catch.
  `scripts/us157_author.py` is kept as the record of what was authored and why.

- **CHECK moves.json SIGNATURE NAMES AGAINST THE WHOLE FILE, NOT THE LINE.** `projectileSymbol|tint`
  is unique PER LINE but `signatureName` is unique GLOBALLY, and six of the first draft's names
  collided with the base form they were named after (Angewomon X/Ophanimon X/Cyberdramon X shared
  their base's attack, BlackMegaloGrowmon shared MegaloGrowmon's). Variants are exactly where this
  bites. Also keep `signatureSymbol` inside the 21 SF Symbols the file already uses — the render test
  is the only thing that would catch an invented one, and it runs on the simulator.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all twenty-two files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, all six `AdultSweep*Tests` and all three `ChildSweep*Tests`
  (643 -> 672); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests` (`dmc-v1` 30->32, `palmon` 24->26,
  `penc-ds` 38->39, `penc-me` 44->50, `penc-nso` 44->46, `penc-nsp` 33->34, `penc-sw` 9->12,
  `penc-vb` 49->53, `tamers` 82->90) and the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows in every `*Sweep*Tests`;
  `inLine.count` AND `sweepEggs` in `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests`, `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests`,
  `PendulumNatureSpiritsTreeTests`, `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests` and
  `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests`; `pencme_mugendramon`'s parent set in `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests`
  and Turuiemon's earned list in `PendulumVirusBustersTreeTests`; the dmc-v1 tree in
  `EvolutionTreeTests` (30->32 nodes, 44->46 connectors); BOTH egg lists in `EggHatchingTests`;
  `junkIds` and the stranded list in `EvolutionCriteriaTests`; the four leaf lists in
  `AdultSweepHToLTests`/`MToR`/`SToT`/`UToZ`; the dead-end ledger in `ChildSweepAToFTests`
  (105 -> 97); `AdultSweepEToGTests`' "exactly two edges" claim about Ebidramon, relaxed to "exactly
  one fallback"; `AdultSweepMToRTests`' still-unwired list (Cyberdramon X and Angewomon X left it);
  and the three `penc-sw` pins above. `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and both
  `lineDefaults` did NOT move: no new line.

- REMAINS: US-158 onward (44/56 passing). Eleven Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one
  hold the remaining 257 orphans: 84 Perfect, 157 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid. Six lines still have no
  Perfect rung — `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon` — and
  `wanyamon` is now the LAST line with Perfects and no Ultimate above them. Cargodramon (for
  `commandramon`) and Boutmon (for `vital`) are pinned as rehome candidates the day either of those
  rungs opens, as are Kinkakumon and Xiquemon for `penc-sw`. The 97 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`'
  dead-end ledger are still owed an out-edge; nine of this story's own Ultimates are NOT on it, since
  the ledger stops below the top rung.

The fourteen, each `Champion -> Perfect -> Ultimate`:
  DarkKnightmon      tailmon(penc-nsp)        -> darkknightmon_x  NEW
  DarkSuperstarmon   starmon(tamers)          -> titamon          NEW
  Delumon            kiwimon(penc-wg)         -> griffomon

  Duramon            raptordramon(penc-me)    -> pencme_wargreymon
  Entmon             cockatrimon(penc-vb)     -> cherubimon_virtue
  Fantomon           wizarmon(penc-nso)       -> piemon
  Flaremon           firamon(penc-nso)        -> apollomon        NEW
  Garudamon X        pencwg_birdramon(penc-wg)-> hououmon
  Gigadramon         devidramon(dmc-v5)       -> mugendramon
  Gogmamon           gaogamon(wanyamon)       -> ancientvolcamon  NEW
  Gokuwmon           ginkakumon(penc-sw)      -> seitengokuwmon   NEW
  Grappleomon        gryzmon(wanyamon)        -> dinotigermon     NEW
  Gusokumon          ebidramon(penc-ds)       -> plesiomon

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **AN "ORPHAN" IN APPENDIX B'S COUNT CAN BE A DIGIMON THAT IS ALREADY ON SCREEN — CHECK THE
  SPRITE FILE, NOT ONLY THE ID.** `ex-tyranomon` was the fifteenth orphan in this band and needed
  no node at all: `dmc-v5` had drawn it since US-137 under `extyranomon`, the same `spriteFile`
  with the hyphen dropped. Appendix B reads `roster.generated.json`, which carries the SHEET id
  from disk AND the graph's id, so a graph node whose id does not match its own sheet leaves the
  sheet looking unwired. The fix was a rename — node id, three in-edges, the `elements.json` and
  `moves.json` rows — and it cleared the orphan, retired the drift `DMCVersion5TreeTests` had
  pinned since US-137, and took `extyranomon` off `RosterTests`' alias list where it never
  belonged. **Before authoring a node for an orphan, grep the graph for its `spriteFile`.** One
  more of these may be hiding: `hiandromon`/`hi-andromon` is a KNOWN and deliberate divergence
  (two real sheets, one node) and must NOT be "fixed" the same way — `RosterTests` pins it.

- **A PERFECT SWEEP THAT PICKS ITS PARENTS OFF THE DEAD-END LEDGER PAYS FOR ITSELF TWICE, AND THE
  SECOND SWEEP CAN DO IT WITHOUT AUTHORING A FLOOR.** US-157 cleared nine leaves but had to invent
  Pandamon for `penc-sw`; this story cleared seven and every floor it needed
  (`catchmamemon`, `andiramon_virus`, `darumamon`, `karakurumon`, `pandamon`) already existed, so
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` did not move at all. Ledger 105 -> 97 -> 90. Expect the H-Z
  sweeps to keep this shape: after seven Adult sweeps the cheap parent is nearly always a leaf.

- **`wanyamon` WAS THE LAST LINE WITH PERFECTS AND NO MEGA, AND OPENING IT PROMOTED THE WHOLE
  LINE'S EGGS AT ONCE.** All four `wanyamon` Digitama (Gao, Bear, Koe, Lioll) went from unraisable
  to legal starting eggs in one edit, because `MainScreenModel.startingDigitamaId` filters on
  `graph.reachesUltimate`. That is a bigger jump than US-157's five and it is the LAST of its kind
  — `linesWithAPerfect.subtracting(linesWithAnUltimate)` is now empty, and `PerfectSweepAToCTests`'
  claim about it was flipped rather than deleted. The remaining promotions have to come from the
  MIDDLE of a thread, like Monodra Digitama did here (DORUgamon was a leaf until DORUguremon and
  DORUgoramon went over it). Six lines still have no Perfect rung at all: `xros`, `vital`,
  `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon` — open one of those and the same egg
  arithmetic applies again.

- **THE MOVES-TABLE COLLISION CHECK MUST RUN BEFORE THE EDIT, NOT AFTER: EIGHT OF THIS STORY'S
  TWENTY-ONE FIRST-DRAFT MOVES COLLIDED.** `signatureName` is unique GLOBALLY and
  `projectileSymbol|tint` is unique PER LINE, and the second is the one that bites at this rung —
  a story adding three nodes to one line is competing with 49 rows already on it, and `flame.fill`
  on `penc-nso` had only two free tints left. Script the check against the real JSON and re-run it
  after every edit to the table; changing the SYMBOL is usually better than reaching for an odd
  tint (Flaremon became `hand.raised.fill`, Apollomon `star.fill`).

- **THE VARIANT RULE READS FROM THE TOP AS WELL AS THE BOTTOM.** DarkKnightmon X hangs off the
  DarkKnightmon this story authored, so "a variant sits on its base form's line" was satisfied by
  authoring the base form first and letting the X follow it — the same shape as US-157's Angewomon
  X but with the base form new. And when a variant's base form has NO node yet (DarkSuperstarmon;
  Superstarmon is an S-Z orphan), say in the node `comment` and in a test where the base form is
  going to have to go, so the later sweep is told rather than free to disagree.

- **A LINE ARGUMENT CAN BE THE CHEAP HALF OF A REHOME, AND SAYING SO IS WHAT MAKES IT DEFENSIBLE.**
  Gokuwmon's three cited parents (Hanumon `penc-nso`, Kinkakumon `penc-ds`, Turuiemon `penc-vb`)
  are all off `penc-sw`, the Saiyu Warriors line it obviously belongs to, so the in-edge rests on
  Ginkakumon — the twin of the Kinkakumon that US-153 and US-157 both pinned as this line's rehome
  candidate. Rehome Kinkakumon and the arrow becomes a citation. Entmon is the other one and is the
  first LINE argument this series has had to make about a CLIMB rather than an in-edge: all three
  of its cited `Evolves To` are undrawable (Ancient Troiamon idle-only, Ornismon and Xuanwumon no
  sheet at all).

- **TWO SHEETS OF ONE DIGIMON ARE TWO NODES — THE OPPOSITE OF US-143's ANSWER, AND FOR THE SAME
  REASON.** `Perfect/Fantomon.png` and `Perfect/Phantomon.png` are both on disk, so the roster has
  two entries and the graph now has two nodes; US-143 merged HolyAngemon and MagnaAngemon because
  ONE sheet served two names. The rule is the roster's: **one entry per sheet.** What must not
  happen is one Champion offering the same Digimon twice under two spellings, so Fantomon hangs off
  Wizarmon while Phantomon keeps Bakemon, and a test pins that the two parent sets are disjoint.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all twenty-two files:** node count in `ElementCatalogTests`,
  `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, all six `AdultSweep*Tests`, all three `ChildSweep*Tests` and
  `PerfectSweepAToCTests` (672 -> 693); the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests` (`dmc-v5` 22->23,
  `penc-nsp` 34->36, `penc-ds` 39->40, `penc-nso` 46->49, `penc-wg` 37->39, `penc-me` 50->51,
  `penc-vb` 53->54, `tamers` 90->94, `wanyamon` 20->24, `penc-sw` 12->14) and the same lines'
  `sizes[...]` rows in every `*Sweep*Tests` and `DigitamaSweepTests`; `inLine.count` AND `sweepEggs`
  in ALL SIX `Pendulum*TreeTests`; the dead-end ledger in `ChildSweepAToFTests` (97 -> 90) and its
  twin in `PerfectSweepAToCTests`; BOTH egg lists in `EggHatchingTests`; `strandedPerfect` and
  `strandedUltimate` in `EvolutionCriteriaTests` (Gokuwmon and Seiten Gokuwmon inherit Ginkakumon's
  strandedness — `penc-sw` still has no Digitama); the `gazimonLineVerifiedSet` in `SeedRosterTests`
  (Gigadramon appended, per the "append, never widen" rule); the alias list in `RosterTests` and the
  matching comment in `Sources/DexModel.swift` (both lost `extyranomon`); `DMCVersion5TreeTests`
  throughout, plus its `laterSweeps` set; `AdultSweepSToTTests`' leaf list (Starmon left) and its
  `extyranomon` pin; the `penc-sw` Perfect-rung pins in `AdultSweepHToLTests` and
  `AdultSweepUToZTests`; `AdultSweepAToDTests`' `wanyamon` Perfect set, relaxed to a superset;
  `PerfectSweepAToCTests`' "raptordramon has exactly two edges", relaxed to "exactly one fallback";
  and the "names its device" tests in `BabyIISweepTests`, `ChildSweepAToFTests` and
  `DigitamaSweepBabyITests`, which is why Seiten Gokuwmon's comment says "Saiyu Warriors".
  `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles` and both `lineDefaults` did NOT move: no new line.

- REMAINS: US-159 onward (45/56 passing). Ten Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one
  hold the remaining 235 orphans: 69 Perfect, 150 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid. Ebidramon is now one
  earned branch off the ceiling (only spirit free) and is pinned as such. Kinkakumon and Xiquemon
  are still `penc-sw` rehome candidates, Cargodramon still `commandramon`'s and Boutmon still
  `vital`'s. Sagomon, Sanzomon and Shawujinmon are the three Saiyu Warriors Perfects still owed.
  The 90 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end ledger are still owed an out-edge; the seven
  Ultimates this story opened are NOT on it, since the ledger stops below the top rung.
---

## 2026-07-23 - US-159: Orphan sweep: Perfect H-L

Wired the ELEVEN playable Perfect whose display name begins H-L that were still orphans, for eleven
new Perfect nodes plus FIVE new Ultimates. Third story at the Perfect rung.

**Orphan count, Appendix B over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`: 235 BEFORE -> 219 AFTER.**
Perfect bucket 69 -> 58 (the H-L band 11 -> 0), Ultimate bucket 150 -> 145. Graph 693 -> 709.
Files changed: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`,
`scripts/us159_author.py` (new, the record of what was authored), `Tests/PerfectSweepHToLTests.swift`
(new, 27 tests), and eighteen existing test files. Full suite 2264 green (2237 before), build green,
validator zero findings.

The eleven, each `Champion -> Perfect -> Ultimate`:
  Hangyomon          ebidramon(penc-ds)        -> vikemon
  Hisyaryumon        omekamon(penc-me)         -> ouryumon         NEW
  Insekimon          icemon(penc-nso)          -> pencnso_boltmon
  Jazarichmon        jazardmon(tamers)         -> metallicdramon   NEW
  Karatenmon         igamon(wanyamon)          -> tengumon         NEW
  LadyDevimon        kyubimon(tamers)          -> beelzebumon
  LadyDevimon X      numemon_x(tamers)         -> beelstarmon_x    NEW
  Lavogaritamon      lavorvomon(penc-nso)      -> volcanicdramon   NEW
  Lilamon            sunflowmon(palmon)        -> rosemon
  Lilimon X          togemon_x(palmon)         -> rosemon
  Lucemon Falldown   pencnso_devimon(penc-nso) -> venomvamdemon

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **NINE OF ELEVEN IN-EDGES CAME OFF A LEAF CHAMPION — THE LARGEST FALL THE DEAD-END LEDGER HAS
  TAKEN (90 -> 81) — AND EVERY JUNK FLOOR ALREADY EXISTED, SO `junkIds` DID NOT MOVE FOR THE SECOND
  STORY RUNNING.** US-157 cleared nine and had to invent Pandamon; US-158 cleared seven and invented
  nothing; this cleared nine and invented nothing. **Price the in-edge off `ChildSweepAToFTests`'
  ledger FIRST**: at this rung the cheap parent is nearly always a leaf, and a leaf costs only an
  `isDefault` edge onto a junk Perfect its line already has. Expect the M-Z sweeps to keep the shape.

- **A JUNK CHAMPION IS A LEGAL PARENT, AND SOMETIMES THE ONLY ONE — AND THAT IS WHAT PROMOTED THE
  TERRIER EGG.** Numemon X is `tamers`' junk Champion (US-148) and is the ONLY cited parent in this
  graph for LadyDevimon X: the bolded one is LadyDevimon itself (a Perfect, so never an in-edge) and
  Velgrmon is Armor-Hybrid. So the earned branch hangs off the junk fall — the Scumon arrangement
  US-133 recorded, now the third of its kind after Raremon and Scumon. The consequence is the
  strangest thread in the file: **Terriermon's ONLY onward edge is the junk fall, so Terrier Digitama
  reaches a Mega only by being neglected first**, which is what took it and Rena Digitama off
  `EggHatchingTests`' unraisable list. Prove a junk parent in BOTH directions through the engine —
  earned branch for a raised Digimon, junk fall for a neglected one — rather than reasoning about it.

- **THAT WAS THE LAST EGG PROMOTION ANY PERFECT SWEEP CAN MAKE.** After US-159 no egg on a line that
  HAS a Perfect rung is unraisable: the eleven still on `EggHatchingTests`' list sit on
  `commandramon`, `algomon`, `diablomon`, `vital` and `adventure02`, and not one of those five lines
  has a Perfect rung at all. Pinned as a disjointness claim rather than a name list in
  `PerfectSweepHToLTests`, so it fails the day someone opens one of those rungs and forgets the eggs.

- **A VARIANT'S ONE POSSIBLE PARENT CAN DECIDE WHERE ITS BASE FORM GOES — READ THE PAIR TOGETHER
  BEFORE CHOOSING EITHER LINE.** LadyDevimon has forty cited parents across nine lines and Piemon on
  `penc-nso` was the obvious reading; LadyDevimon X has exactly one usable parent anywhere,
  Numemon X on `tamers`. Choosing LadyDevimon's line off its OWN citations would have split the pair
  across two lines and broken the variant rule. Same shape as US-158's DarkKnightmon/DarkKnightmon X
  but read from the constrained end: **when a range holds a base form and its X, solve the X first.**

- **A BOLDED PARENT CAN BE UNDRAWABLE FOR A REASON OF SHAPE RATHER THAN OF ART, AND THAT IS A NEW
  KIND OF "cannot".** Lucemon Falldown's sole bolded `Evolves From` is Lucemon — which is a CHILD on
  `dmc-v3`, and `GraphValidationError.invalidStageTransition` refuses a Child -> Perfect edge. Every
  earlier "cannot" in this series was dexOnly art or a missing sheet; check the STAGE of a bolded
  parent before pricing it, and when the canonical arrow is illegal say so in the comment (a test
  greps for it) instead of quietly substituting a Champion.

- **TWO REHOME PINS LEFT, BOTH BECAUSE THE CITED PARENT SITS ON A LINE WITH NO PERFECT RUNG.**
  Hisyaryumon's bolded parents (Ginryumon, Ryudamon) are `commandramon`, so it took the cited
  Omekamon on `penc-me` and is pinned as `commandramon`'s rehome candidate; LadyDevimon X's other
  drawable parent, Mantaraymon X, is `vital`, so it joins Boutmon as that line's. Both pins are node
  comments AND tests. That makes the standing list: Kinkakumon and Xiquemon for `penc-sw`,
  Cargodramon and Boutmon and LadyDevimon X for `vital`/`commandramon`, Hisyaryumon for
  `commandramon`. Opening one of the six Perfect-less rungs should sweep that list first.

- **`EBIDRAMON IS NOW FULL` — the handover US-158 wrote was spent by the very next story.** The
  bolded Hangyomon arrow took its last free energy (spirit); vitality/stamina/strength went to
  Anomalocarimon, Anomalocarimon X and Gusokumon. Four earned branches plus the junk fall is five
  edges, which is `EvolutionCriteriaTests`' ceiling exactly. `PerfectSweepDToGTests`' claim was
  FLIPPED to `Set(EnergyType.allCases)` rather than deleted. A `penc-ds` Perfect after this needs a
  different Champion, not a fifth edge.

- **SCRIPT THE MECHANICAL KNOCK-ONS, BUT NOT WITH "APPEND TO THE LAST STRING LITERAL".** The
  node-count and per-line-size edits span twenty files, so they were done with a small Python pass;
  it appended its note to the last string in the XCTAssertEqual call, which for a message-less
  `XCTAssertEqual(sizes["palmon"], 26)` is the DICTIONARY KEY — three assertions silently became
  `sizes["palmon, plus US-159's two"]` and failed with `nil is not equal to`. Cheap to spot, cheaper
  to avoid: only append when the call already has a message argument.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all nineteen files:** node count 693 -> 709 in
  `ElementCatalogTests`, `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, all six `AdultSweep*Tests`, all three
  `ChildSweep*Tests` and both `PerfectSweep*Tests`; the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`
  (`palmon` 26->28, `penc-ds` 40->41, `penc-me` 51->53, `penc-nso` 49->53, `tamers` 94->99,
  `wanyamon` 24->26) and the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows in every `*Sweep*Tests` and
  `DigitamaSweepTests`; `inLine.count` AND `sweepEggs` in `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests`,
  `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests` and `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests`; the dead-end ledger in
  `ChildSweepAToFTests` (90 -> 81, nine cleared) and its twin in both `PerfectSweep*Tests`; the leaf
  lists in `AdultSweepHToLTests` (five left), `AdultSweepMToRTests` (two) and `AdultSweepSToTTests`
  (two); `AdultSweepMToRTests`' still-unwired list (Hisyaryumon left it, re-pinned with the parent it
  took); `AdultSweepUToZTests`' "LadyDevimon is still unwired" claim, FLIPPED to name Kyubimon;
  `PerfectSweepAToCTests`' `beelzebumon` parent SET (Baalmon + LadyDevimon) and its `rena`/`terrier`
  egg pins; `PerfectSweepDToGTests`' Ebidramon energies, its `wanyamon` Ultimate set (relaxed to a
  superset for Tengumon) and its egg pins; BOTH lists in `EggHatchingTests`. `EvolutionCriteriaTests`
  did NOT move at all — no new junk floor and no new stranded node, which is the first sweep at this
  rung where that file was untouched. `MinigameAssignmentTests`, `DexModel.lineTitles`, `RosterTests`
  and both `lineDefaults` did not move either: no new line.

- REMAINS: US-160 onward (46/56 passing). Nine Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one
  hold the remaining 219 orphans: 58 Perfect, 145 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid. Six lines still have no
  Perfect rung — `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`, `diablomon`. Sagomon,
  Sanzomon and Shawujinmon are still the three Saiyu Warriors Perfects owed. Ogudomon is pinned in
  Lucemon Falldown's comment as belonging over whichever Demon Lord line a later sweep opens. The 81
  leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end ledger are still owed an out-edge; the five Ultimates
  this story opened are NOT on it, since the ledger stops below the top rung.

## 2026-07-23 - US-160: Orphan sweep: Perfect M

Wired the TWENTY-ONE playable Perfect whose display name begins with M that were still orphans —
the biggest band the Perfect rung has — for 21 Perfect nodes, FIVE new Ultimates and ONE junk
Perfect floor. Fourth story at the Perfect rung.

**Orphan count, Appendix B over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`: 219 BEFORE -> 193 AFTER.**
Perfect bucket 58 -> 37 (the M band 21 -> 0), Ultimate bucket 145 -> 140. Graph 709 -> 736.
Files changed: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`,
`scripts/us160_author.py` (new, the record of what was authored), `Tests/PerfectSweepMTests.swift`
(new, 28 tests), and twenty-six existing test files. Full suite 2292 green (2264 before), build
green, validator zero findings.

The twenty-one, each `Champion -> Perfect -> Ultimate`:
  MachGaogamon          gaogamon(wanyamon)          -> ancientvolcamon
  Mamemon X             greymon_blue(dmc-v1)        -> banchomamemon
  Mammon X              shimaunimon(penc-nso)       -> pencnso_skullmammon
  Manticoremon          growmon(tamers)             -> dukemon             NEW
  MarinBullmon          shellmon(dmc-v3)            -> ryugumon            NEW
  MarinChimairamon      octmon(penc-ds)             -> plesiomon
  MegaSeadramon X       hyougamon(penc-nsp)         -> metalseadramon
  MegaloGrowmon Orange  growmon_orange(tamers)      -> dukemon             NEW
  MegaloGrowmon X       blackgalgomon(tamers)       -> chaosdukemon
  Meicrackmon           meicoomon(diablomon)        -> rasielmon           NEW
  Meicrackmon Vicious   meicoomon(diablomon)        -> raguelmon           NEW
  Mephismon             wizarmon(penc-nso)          -> piemon
  Mephismon X           pencnso_devimon(penc-nso)   -> dinorexmon          NEW
  Mermaimon             ikkakumon(penc-ds)          -> vikemon
  MetalGreymon Virus X  devimon(dmc-v1)             -> blitzgreymon
  MetalMamemon X        thunderballmon(penc-me)     -> princemamemon
  MetalPhantomon        bakemon(dmc-v3)             -> gokumon
  MetalTyranomon V2     darktyranomon(dmc-v5)       -> mugendramon
  MetalTyranomon X      cyclomon(dmc-v5)            -> mugendramon
  Monzaemon X           numemon(dmc-v1)             -> dmcv1_shinmonzaemon
  Mummymon              pencnso_bakemon(penc-nso)   -> deathmon
plus the junk floor `diablomon_gerbemon` under Meicoomon.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A JUNK FLOOR CAN HAVE TO BE A LINE-SCOPED ALIAS, BECAUSE THE JUNK-FLAVOURED SHEETS ARE GONE.**
  US-148/151/157 each spent an unused sheet — Numemon X, CatchMamemon, Karakurumon, Pandamon — so
  each floor also removed an orphan. By this story not ONE of the 58 Perfect still orphaned is a gag
  Digimon (they are Okuwamon, Paildramon, Rapidmon, Vamdemon X…), so `diablomon`'s floor draws the
  Gerbemon sheet under a scoped id, the `dmcv2_vademon` pattern. **Consequences to price in
  advance:** it removes NO orphan, `RosterTests`' alias list moves, and `EvolutionCriteriaTests.
  junkIds` gains its first scoped name. Every remaining line without a Perfect rung — `xros`,
  `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon` — will pay the same way.

- **FIFTEEN OF TWENTY-ONE PLACEMENTS WERE FREE, AND THE RATIO IS CUMULATIVE RATHER THAN LUCKY.**
  US-157 managed 10/19, US-158 7/14, US-159 6/11, this one 15/21 — because three sweeps' worth of
  Megas are now in place, so US-152's "intersect `Evolves From` against `Evolves To`" closes on a
  line that already has both ends far more often. **Price an M-Z or Ultimate sweep off that**: the
  expensive node is now the one whose whole family is on a line with no Mega, not the average one.

- **THE VARIANT RULE HAS A STRONGER FORM THAN "same line": SAME PARENT — AND AT THE PERFECT RUNG IT
  IS USUALLY AVAILABLE AND ALWAYS CHEAPER.** Six of this story's nine variants hang off the very
  Champion their base form hangs off (Mammon X off ShimaUnimon, MetalGreymon Virus X off Devimon,
  MetalTyranomon V2 off DarkTyranomon and X off Cyclomon, Monzaemon X off Numemon, MegaloGrowmon
  Orange off Growmon (Orange)), which costs no new argument at all and makes the climb the base
  form's own Mega for free. Look up `graph.parents(of: base)` BEFORE reading the variant's own
  `Evolves From` — it is often a better answer than the citation list, and it is what
  `AdultSweepEToGTests.testTheOneVariantSitsWithItsBaseForm` already asserts.

- **AND THE RULE HAS A LIMIT: A BASE FORM'S LINE CAN HOLD THE CLIMB AND NO CITED PARENT.**
  MetalMamemon is `dmc-v2`, whose Metal Garurumon IS cited — but `dmc-v2` has no Champion on
  MetalMamemon X's page, so honouring the line meant inventing an arrow at BOTH ends. It followed
  Thunderballmon on `penc-me` to the cited Prince Mamemon instead, which is
  `ChildSweepMToZTests.testEveryVariantSitsWithItsBaseFormOrFollowsACitedParent`'s escape hatch.
  **Check both ends of the base form's line before promising the variant to it.**

- **A BOLDED PARENT CAN BE WORTH SPENDING ON SOMETHING ELSE — SAY SO IN THE COMMENT.** Growmon is
  MegaloGrowmon Orange's bolded parent AND `tamers`' last leaf Champion. The Orange form is pinned
  to Growmon (Orange) by the variant rule anyway, while Manticoremon's only other readings were
  Mimicmon (`algomon`), Reppamon and Tia Ludomon (`vital`) — each of which would have opened a
  Perfect rung, a junk floor and a Mega for one node. So the leaf went to Manticoremon and bought
  Dukemon, the Mega `tamers` had been owed since US-151. **When a leaf is contested, give it to the
  claimant whose alternatives cost a whole rung.**

- **`diablomon` COST THREE EXTRA NODES AND PROMOTED TWO EGGS, AND FOUR LINES ARE LEFT.** Meicoomon is
  the only parent this pack can draw for either Meicrackmon, so the rung had to open; US-158's rule
  ("owe a Mega in the same story") made it Perfect + Ultimate + junk floor at once, and
  `MainScreenModel.startingDigitamaId` then promoted Kera and Meicoo Digitama — `EggHatchingTests`
  moved in BOTH directions. US-159 said no Perfect sweep could promote another egg; that was right
  about lines that HAVE a Perfect rung and wrong about opening one. The nine eggs still unraisable
  sit on `commandramon`, `algomon`, `vital` and `adventure02`. **`vital` is the cheapest rung left
  to open — 33 nodes, ten Champions, every one of them a leaf — and it already has three pinned
  rehome candidates (Boutmon, Cargodramon, LadyDevimon X).**

- **AN ORPHAN'S "no drawable parent" CAN BE TOTAL, NOT JUST INCONVENIENT.** Mephismon X's whole
  `Evolves From` is Mephismon (a Perfect) and Velgrmon (Armor-Hybrid, and not a node at all) — one
  worse than US-159's LadyDevimon X, which at least had Numemon X. The answer is the variant rule
  plus a flavour argument among the chosen line's Champions, and the comment has to ADMIT it; the
  new test greps for "NO DRAWABLE CITED PARENT". Same for MachGaogamon's climb: both its bolded
  `Evolves To` (Mirage Gaogamon, Z'd Garurumon) are idle-only, so `edgeToDexOnlyNode` forbids the
  canonical top of that thread forever.

- **WIKIMON PAGE TITLES FOR X-ANTIBODY FORMS ARE SPACED, AND THE UNSPACED GUESS RETURNS AN EMPTY
  BODY RATHER THAN A REDIRECT.** `MegaSeadramon (X-Antibody)` is 0 bytes; `Mega Seadramon
  (X-Antibody)` is the page. Same for Megalo Growmon, Metal Greymon (Virus), Metal Mamemon, Metal
  Tyranomon. **Fetch with the spaced spelling first and treat a zero-length body as "try the other
  spacing", not as "no page".** Plain forms redirect (`MachGaogamon` -> `Mach Gaogamon`); the
  parenthesised ones do not.

- **`Set(graph.parents(of:))` EQUALITY ON AN EARLIER STORY'S ULTIMATE IS THE ASSERTION A PERFECT
  SWEEP BREAKS, AND THERE ARE THREE SUCH FILES NOW.** This story hung MegaloGrowmon X under
  US-157's ChaosDukemon and MachGaogamon under US-158's AncientVolcamon. Fix by NAMING the new
  parent in that story's `authoredUltimates` table, never by loosening to a superset — and grep
  `authoredUltimates` across `PerfectSweep*Tests` BEFORE choosing a climb, the same way US-151 said
  to grep `Set(graph.parents`.

- **A `junkFloors` / `swept` table in an earlier sweep asserts `evolutions.count == 2`, and that
  breaks the moment you branch that Champion again.** Three did here: Gaogamon in
  `PerfectSweepDToGTests`, ShimaUnimon in `AdultSweepSToTTests`, and this story's own Meicoomon
  (which carries two Perfects). The fix that keeps the claim is a NAMED exception
  (`parent == "gaogamon" ? 3 : 2`), not a `>=`. Add `grep -n "evolutions.count, 2" Tests` to the
  pre-flight list beside `inLine.count` and `sweepEggs`.

- **The knock-on list for this rung, all twenty-six files:** node count 709 -> 736 in
  `ElementCatalogTests`, `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, all six `AdultSweep*Tests`, all three
  `ChildSweep*Tests` and all three `PerfectSweep*Tests`; the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`
  (`dmc-v1` 32->35, `dmc-v3` 48->51, `dmc-v5` 23->25, `diablomon` 17->22, `penc-ds` 41->43,
  `penc-me` 53->54, `penc-nso` 53->58, `penc-nsp` 36->37, `tamers` 99->103, `wanyamon` 26->27) and
  the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows in every `*Sweep*Tests`, `BabyIISweepTests` and
  `DigitamaSweepTests`; `inLine.count` AND `sweepEggs` in `PendulumDeepSaversTreeTests`,
  `PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests`, `PendulumNatureSpiritsTreeTests` and
  `PendulumNightmareSoldiersTreeTests`; `laterSweeps` in `DMCVersion5TreeTests`; `nodes.count` and
  `connectors.count` for `dmc-v1` in `EvolutionTreeTests`; the dead-end ledger in
  `ChildSweepAToFTests` (81 -> 77) and its twin in all three `PerfectSweep*Tests`; the leaf lists in
  `AdultSweepHToLTests` (Hyougamon) and `AdultSweepMToRTests` (Meicoomon); `AdultSweepMToRTests`'
  still-unwired list (Mamemon X and Monzaemon X left it, re-pinned with the parents they took) and
  `AdultSweepSToTTests`' MetalTyranomon X claim, FLIPPED to name Cyclomon; the "lines with no
  Perfect rung" set in `AdultSweepUToZTests` and all three `PerfectSweep*Tests` (`diablomon` gone);
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds`; `RosterTests`' alias list; `SeedRosterTests`' `patamonLine`
  and `gazimonLine` verified sets; BOTH lists in `EggHatchingTests`. `MinigameAssignmentTests`,
  `DexModel.lineTitles` and both `lineDefaults` did not move: no new line.

- REMAINS: US-161 onward (47/56 passing). Eight Perfect and Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one
  hold the remaining 193 orphans: 37 Perfect, 140 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid. Five lines still have
  no Perfect rung — `xros`, `vital`, `adventure02`, `algomon`, `commandramon`. Sagomon, Sanzomon and
  Shawujinmon are still the three Saiyu Warriors Perfects owed. Ogudomon is still pinned in Lucemon
  Falldown's comment. The 77 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end ledger are still owed an

## 2026-07-23 - US-161: Orphan sweep: Perfect N-R

Authored the fifteen orphaned Perfect whose displayName starts N-R, the seven Ultimates they climb
into, and the two junk Perfect floors the two lines this story OPENS needed first — 24 nodes,
736 -> 760. Perfect orphans 37 -> 22; total playable orphans 193 -> 171 (Ultimate 140 -> 133,
Armor-Hybrid still 16).

Files: `Resources/evolutions.json` (+24 nodes, +6 junk-floor edges on former leaf Champions),
`Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`, new `Tests/PerfectSweepNToRTests.swift`,
new `scripts/us161_author.py`, and the 26-file knock-on set the US-160 note predicted.

Build green, 2322 tests pass, `testShippedEvolutionsJsonIsValid` reports zero validator findings.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE TWO CHEAPEST REMAINING RUNGS ARE NOW OPEN, AND `vital` COST EXACTLY WHAT US-160 PRICED IT
  AT.** US-160 called `vital` "the cheapest rung left to open — 33 nodes, ten Champions, every one
  of them a leaf". It was: Kokeshimon and Tia Ludomon each needed a floor before either could
  branch, and one alias (`vital_darumamon`) served BOTH, because the floor is per-LINE and not
  per-Champion. `xros` paid the same bill with one alias for one Champion. **A line that opens with
  N leaf Champions still buys only ONE junk floor** — price the alias once per line, not once per
  parent, or you will over-estimate the next rung by a factor of N.

- **A PRE-EXISTING JUNK FLOOR THAT IS NOT ITSELF A LEAF IS THE ONLY FREE ONE.** Four of the six
  floors here pre-dated the story, but they are not equivalent: CatchMamemon and Karakurumon are
  terminal, so leaning on them adds a dead end to the ledger, while `locomon` already climbs to
  GrandLocomon and cost `penc-me` nothing at all. **Prefer a junk Perfect that already has an
  out-edge when the line offers a choice** — `grep -n '"'"'junkIds'"'"' Tests/EvolutionCriteriaTests.swift`
  and check each candidate's `evolutions` before picking.

- **THE COUNT-THE-FLOORS ASSERTION IS THE ONE A REUSED FLOOR BREAKS, AND IT FAILS AS "test wrong",
  NOT "data wrong".** The only red in the whole 2322 was
  `testTheSixLeafChampionsGainedTheirLinesJunkFloor`, whose bookkeeping line said two floors
  pre-dated the story when three did — it had been written from the two aliases and never
  re-counted after `locomon` was chosen for Kuwagamon X. **When a sweep's own new test fails on a
  set-difference of its own tables, check the TABLE against `evolutions.json` before touching the
  data**; here the data was right and the assertion was stale.

- **WRITE THE `subtracting(...)`/`intersection(...)` LEDGERS LAST.** Every sweep since US-157 has
  had a pair of these lines partitioning "authored by me" from "already there". They are derived
  from choices made while authoring, so authoring them from the plan rather than from the finished
  `JUNK_FLOORS` dict is how this failure happens. Generate them from the script's own tables at the
  end of the run.

- **THE KNOCK-ON SET IS NOW STABLE AT THE 26 FILES US-160 LISTED** — node count 736 -> 760 in
  `ElementCatalogTests`, `EvolutionGraphValidatorTests`, all six `AdultSweep*Tests`, all three
  `ChildSweep*Tests` and all four `PerfectSweep*Tests`; the per-line dict in `EvolutionGraphTests`
  and the same lines' `sizes[...]` rows everywhere; `inLine.count` AND `sweepEggs` in the four
  Pendulum tree tests; `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` (two scoped names) and `RosterTests`' alias
  list. **The list in the US-160 note is still accurate — read it before starting a Perfect or
  Ultimate sweep rather than rediscovering it.**

- REMAINS: US-162 onward (48/56 passing). 171 orphans — 22 Perfect, 133 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid.
  Only `adventure02`, `algomon` and `commandramon` still lack a Perfect rung, and each will pay the
  line-scoped-alias price. Sagomon, Sanzomon and Shawujinmon are still the three Saiyu Warriors
  Perfects owed; Ogudomon is still pinned in Lucemon Falldown's comment. The Ultimate rung is now
  the bulk of the work: 133 orphans against seven remaining sweeps.

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **A LINE'S PERFECT RUNG OPENS UNDER ITS JUNK CHAMPION, NOT UNDER ITS BEST ONE — AND THAT IS WHAT
  PROMOTES THE EGGS.** US-161 left `adventure02` closed because XV-mon carries only V Digitama and
  branching it would have stranded Worm Digitama. The answer it missed is Nise Drimogemon, the
  line's junk Adult, which takes the `isDefault` fall of V-mon, Wormmon AND Tinkermon — so ONE
  earned branch off it promoted both eggs at once. **Before pricing a rung, look at which Champion
  every Child of the line falls into, not at which Champion is cited**; the junk one is reachable
  from every thread by construction, and US-133's Scumon rule already makes an earned branch off it
  legal. Same shape one line over: `commandramon`'s Damemon catches both its Children's falls.

- **A LINE CAN BE PERMANENTLY UNOPENABLE, AND `algomon` IS ONE.** Its only egg, Ghost Digitama,
  descends to Algomon (Adult), Mimicmon and Witchmon and stops; the Labramon -> Siesamon thread —
  the only `algomon` Champion any Perfect orphan cites — hangs off `paomon`, one of the thirteen
  Baby I no Digitama can reach since US-145 spent all fifty-seven. So opening the rung under
  Siesamon would have broken US-159's "no unraisable egg on a line that HAS a Perfect rung"
  invariant, and the Perfect rung is now closed, so no story can open it with a real orphan again.
  Shishimamon went to `vital` under Reppamon instead, with the cited Zanbamon already above it.
  **Check `reachesUltimate` from the line's own eggs BEFORE choosing the Champion, not after** — the
  test that catches this is `PerfectSweepNToRTests.testVitalsFiveDigitamaWereAllPromotedAtOnce`, and
  it fires from another story's file, which is easy to miss.

- **A JUNK FLOOR CAN BE UNCITED, AND THEN THE COMMENT HAS TO SAY THE WORD FLAVOUR.** Every floor
  from US-157 through US-161 was on its own Champion's Wikimon `Evolves To`. Neither Damemon nor
  Ginryumon nor Nise Drimogemon cites a junk Perfect at all, so `commandramon_karakurumon` (a
  clockwork automaton over a line of mechanised soldiers) and `adventure02_jyagamon` (a fake mole
  digging up a potato) rest on shape alone. `RosterTests`' alias list and
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.junkIds` both move, and the new test greps each comment for "FLAVOUR".

- **THE `Set(graph.parents(of:))` LEDGERS ARE NOW THE BULK OF THE KNOCK-ON WORK, AND SEVEN BROKE.**
  Shakamon (+3), Seiten Gokuwmon, Kazuchimon, Ryugumon, Zanbamon, `pencme_mugendramon` (in TWO
  files) and Andromon's thread test. Every one was fixed by NAMING the new parent in the earlier
  story's `authoredUltimates` table. Four `evolutions.count` exceptions moved the same way
  (Musyamon 2->3, Firamon and Ginkakumon 2->3, Omekamon 3->4, Kuwagamon X 3->4, XV-mon Black 3->4).
  **Run `grep -rn 'Set(graph.parents' Tests` and `grep -rn 'evolutions.count,' Tests` for every
  climb target and every parent BEFORE authoring** — it is cheaper than reading 152 failures.

- **A "still owed" PIN FLIPS IN THREE PLACES AT ONCE.** The three Saiyu Warriors Perfects US-157
  pinned were asserted `XCTAssertNil(graph.node(id:))` in `PerfectSweepAToCTests`,
  `PerfectSweepDToGTests` AND `PerfectSweepNToRTests`. Each became "…is on `penc-sw`" rather than
  being deleted. Likewise `penc-sw`'s Perfect-rung census is pinned in two Adult sweep files.
  `grep -rn '<the id>' Tests` for every orphan in the band before starting.

- **EVERY `penc-sw` NODE'S COMMENT MUST CONTAIN "Saiyu Warriors"** — three separate tests enforce it
  (`ChildSweepAToFTests`, `BabyIISweepTests`, `DigitamaSweepBabyITests`). It is the only line in the
  file with that rule, and it is invisible from the node you are writing.

- **SUPERSTARMON SPLIT FROM DARKSUPERSTARMON, WHICH IS THE FIRST BASE-FORM/VARIANT PAIR ON TWO
  LINES.** Starmon is the bolded parent and a `tamers` Adult, but `tamers` holds no cited climb for
  Superstarmon at all, while `penc-me` holds Omekamon AND Prince Mamemon — and Revolmon and
  Thunderballmon, the two other cited `penc-me` parents, are both FULL at three earned branches. So
  the pair is split on purpose and `PerfectSweepDToGTests.testTheVariantsLandedBesideTheirBaseForm`
  records it. **A "full" claim is worth re-counting (US-156's lesson) — here it held.**

- REMAINS: US-163 onward (49/56 passing). 146 orphans — 130 Ultimate, 16 Armor-Hybrid, 0 below.
  Every line now has a Perfect rung except `algomon`, which cannot gain one. Six Ultimate sweeps and
  the Armor-Hybrid one are all that is left. Rehome candidates still pinned: Kinkakumon on `penc-sw`,
  Hisyaryumon and Cargodramon on `commandramon` (whose rung is now OPEN, so both are live),
  Boutmon and LadyDevimon X on `vital`, Paildramon on `adventure02` (also live now). Ogudomon is
  still pinned in Lucemon Falldown's comment. The 67 leaves in `ChildSweepAToFTests`' dead-end
  ledger are still owed an out-edge; the three Ultimates this story opened are not on it.

## 2026-07-23 - US-163: Orphan sweep: Ultimate-Super Ultimate A-B (the first sweep at the top rung)

Wired all THIRTY orphaned Ultimate whose displayName starts A-B, for exactly thirty nodes — the
first Phase E story whose orphan count and node count are the same number, because **an Ultimate
sweep is an IN-EDGE sweep and nothing else**. The rung is terminal, so the AC's out-edge clause does
not bind; `EvolutionCriteriaTests.branchingNodes` filters to Child and Adult, so a forked Perfect
owes no junk floor; and every one of the thirty joined a line that already had a Perfect rung.

**Orphan count, Appendix B over a regenerated `roster.generated.json`: 146 BEFORE -> 116 AFTER.**
Ultimate bucket 130 -> 100, Armor-Hybrid still 16, nothing below either. 787 -> 817 nodes.
Files: `Resources/evolutions.json`, `Resources/elements.json`, `Resources/moves.json`,
`scripts/us163_author.py` (new, the record of what was authored), `Tests/UltimateSweepAToBTests.swift`
(new, 29 tests) and a 29-file knock-on set. Build green, 2382 tests pass (2353 before),
`testShippedEvolutionsJsonIsValid` and this story's own validator test both report zero findings.

The thirty, `Perfect -> Ultimate`:

  Alphamon Ouryuken    doruguremon(tamers)            spirit

  AncientBeatmon       atlurkabuterimon_red(penc-nsp) stamina
  AncientMegatheriumon mammon(penc-nso)               vitality
  AncientMermaimon     mermaimon(penc-ds)             vitality
  AncientSphinxmon     mummymon(penc-nso)             spirit
  Anubimon             cerberumon_x(penc-me)          spirit
