  Brigadramon          cargodramon(penc-me)           strength

**Learnings for future iterations:**

- **THE ULTIMATE RUNG IS THE CHEAPEST RUNG IN PHASE E, AND THE NEXT FIVE SWEEPS SHOULD BE SCOPED
  THAT WAY.** No out-edge is owed (terminal), no junk floor is owed (`branchingNodes` is Child and
  Adult only), and no line can be opened because every line except `algomon` already has a Perfect.
  So one orphan costs exactly one node and one edge. Budget US-164..US-168 at ~20 orphans each with
  no structural work at all — the whole cost is the knock-on, which was 204 failures here.

- **THIS IS THE FIRST STORY TO FORK A PERFECT, AND THAT IS WHAT BROKE 204 TESTS.** Every Perfect in
  the file carried exactly one `isDefault` climb until now, and six `PerfectSweep*Tests` assert
  `evolutions.count == 1` over their own `swept` list while four device-tree files assert an exact
  `targets(of:)` list. Fix by NAMING (`branchedByUS163[perfect] ?? 1`) and by reading the climb as
  `first(where: \.isDefault)` rather than as `first` — never by loosening to a `>=`. **Run
  `grep -n "is not a single climb" Tests` and `grep -rn 'XCTAssertEqual(try targets(of:' Tests` for
  every parent BEFORE authoring**; those two greps are the new pre-flight for this rung.

- **A LEAF PERFECT'S FIRST EDGE MUST BE `isDefault`, SO IT CANNOT CARRY CRITERIA.**
  `SeedRosterTests.testEveryNonTerminalNodeHasExactlyOneDefaultEdge` fails a node with edges and no
  fallback, so an in-edge onto a leaf is the climb itself. That is also the AC-4 reading every rung
  below recorded: "no edge is unconditional" binds the EARNED edges, because US-020 takes an
  `isDefault` edge whatever its gates say. Five leaves were cleared this way (67 -> 62 on the ledger).

- **`SeedRosterTests.earnedPath` IS A TRAP AT THIS RUNG AND IT COST TWO PLACEMENTS.** That test
  walks US-002's three named lines by preferring the EARNED edge at every rung, so giving
  `lilimon` or `metalgreymon` an earned branch silently redirects "Palmon -> Togemon -> Lilimon ->
  Rosemon" or "MetalGreymon -> WarGreymon" to the new node. BanchoLilimon went to Lilamon (the
  sister form, cited on the same page) and Agumon YnK to MetalGreymon (Virus) (the same fork one
  arrow over) because of it. **`grep -n earnedPath Tests/SeedRosterTests.swift` before branching any
  Perfect on `palmon`, `dmc-v1` or `dmc-v2`.**

- **A LINE CAN BE CLOSED TO A NODE BY ART RATHER THAN BY SHAPE, AND `diablomon` IS THE FIRST.**
  Armagemon is what the Kuramon swarm becomes and `diablomon` is that line — but its bolded parent
  Kuramon is a Baby I (`invalidStageTransition`) and BOTH Perfect rungs the swarm climbs through,
  Chrysalimon and Infermon, are idle-only (`edgeToDexOnlyNode`). No story can author a Perfect into
  that line either, since US-162 closed the rung. Check the CITED line's Perfect rung for dexOnly
  art before assuming a thematic home is available.

- **AN X-ANTIBODY MEGA USUALLY HAS NO DRAWABLE PARENT OF ITS OWN, BECAUSE ITS WHOLE `Evolves From`
  IS ULTIMATES.** Barbamon X, Beelzebumon X and Belphemon X each cite only Ultimates (their own
  base form is the bolded one), so the strong variant rule — same PARENT, not merely same line — is
  the only reading available and is free: hang the variant on the Perfect its base form hangs on,
  with a distinct energy. Expect the same for every `*mon X` in the C-Z bands.

- **TWO WIKIMON PAGE TITLES IN THIS BAND ARE UNGUESSABLE AND `opensearch` IS THE ANSWER.**
  `Agumon YnK` is `Agumon -Yuki no Kizuna-` and `BlackWarGreymon X` is `Black War Greymon
  (X-Antibody)` — the spaced-title rule US-160 recorded, plus a sheet name that is an abbreviation
  of a subtitle. Use
  `curl -s "https://wikimon.net/api.php?action=opensearch&search=<name>&limit=50&format=json"`
  before concluding a Digimon has no page; a raw fetch of a wrong title returns an empty body, not
  a 404.

- **THE STRANDED LIST GAINS AT MOST ONE NODE PER SWEEP AT THIS RUNG, AND IT IS ALWAYS `xros`.**
  Armamon's only cited Perfect parent anywhere is OmegaShoutmon, and `xros` has no Digitama. Any
  A-Z Ultimate whose citations point only at `xros` or `penc-sw` inherits the same thing; add it to
  `EvolutionCriteriaTests.strandedUltimate` and let the parent loop prove it is inheritance.

- REMAINS: US-164 onward (50/56 passing). 116 orphans — 100 Ultimate (C-Z), 16 Armor-Hybrid, 0
  below. Five Ultimate sweeps and the Armor-Hybrid one are all that is left. 62 Perfect leaves are
  still owed a climb (`ChildSweepAToFTests`' ledger); MetalGreymon X, Huankunmon and
  BlackMachGaogamon are among them. Rehome candidates still pinned: Kinkakumon on `penc-sw`,
  Hisyaryumon and Cargodramon on `commandramon`, Boutmon and LadyDevimon X on `vital`, Paildramon
  on `adventure02`. Ogudomon is still pinned in Lucemon Falldown's comment and belongs to US-167.
---

## 2026-07-23 - US-164 (Orphan sweep: Ultimate-Super Ultimate C-D)
- Wired 20 of 22 orphaned Ultimate C-D as evolution nodes; left Chaosdramon and Chaosmon alone
  because they are Jogress results the DMC Ver.5/Ver.4 + Metal Empire trees reserve as non-nodes.
- Orphans 116 -> 96 (Ultimate 100 -> 80 by edge-count, 78 true once the two Jogress are set aside;
  Armor-Hybrid 16). Nodes 817 -> 837. Dead-end ledger 62 -> 60 (metalgreymon_x, huankunmon cleared).
- Files: Resources/{evolutions,elements,moves}.json (data), scripts/us164_author.py (authoring
  record), Tests/UltimateSweepCToDTests.swift (new), plus ~19 knock-on test files.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **A JOGRESS RESULT IS OBTAINABLE, SO IT IS NOT ALWAYS AN ORPHAN TO WIRE — BUT ONLY WHEN A DEVICE
    TREE RESERVES IT.** Chaosdramon and Chaosmon are drawn as the Jogress Ultra row in their device
    documents, and DMCVersion5TreeTests / DMCVersion4TreeTests / PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests each
    assert `graph.node(id:) == nil` for them. Wiring them breaks those tests. BUT aegisdramon,
    millenniumon and cernumon are ALSO jogress results and ARE wired as nodes (no tree reserves
    them). So the rule is: before wiring an Ultimate, run `grep -l "<id>" Tests/*TreeTests.swift`
    and check jogress.json — if a tree pins it to no node, treat it as obtainable and exclude it
    from the sweep (coverage test reads "in-edge OR jogress-result"); otherwise wire it.
  - Appendix B's orphan script counts by EVOLUTION edges only, so a reserved jogress result still
    shows as an "orphan" by that metric. Report both numbers: the raw edge-count and the true
    remainder with jogress results subtracted.
  - **A VARIANT WHOSE BASE FORM IS NOT A NODE (dexOnly, OR a reserved jogress result) follows a
    cited parent.** Dynasmon (dexOnly) -> Dynasmon X on doruguremon; Chaosdramon (jogress) ->
    Chaosdramon V2 on metalgreymon_x. Chaosdramon cites Metal Greymon (X-Antibody), so the V2 hangs
    on the base form's cited parent, same shape as US-163's BlackWarGreymon X escape hatch.
  - The `branchedByUS163` dicts in the six PerfectSweep*Tests are the per-file record of which
    Perfects have been forked; renamed to `branchedBySweeps` and appended when US-164 forked more.
    A Perfect that gains a SECOND earned branch (deathmeramon, meicrackmon got two each: demon+demon_x,
    diablomon+diablomon_x) goes to 3 edges. Grep `evolutions.count, 2` / `branchedBy` before authoring.
  - HolyAngemon is now the FIRST four-edge Perfect (cherubimon_virtue, blackseraphimon, dominimon,
    seraphimon) and is CLOSED — all four energies spent. A later sweep wanting the Virus Busters
    HolyAngemon thread must take a different Perfect.

## 2026-07-23 - US-165 (Orphan sweep: Ultimate-Super Ultimate E-H)
- Wired all 14 orphaned Ultimate E-H as evolution nodes. No jogress result in the E-H range, so no
  reservations to skip. Orphans: Ultimate 80 -> 66 (Appendix B), Armor-Hybrid 16 untouched; total
  96 -> 82. Nodes 837 -> 851. Dead-end ledger 60 -> 59 (Pandamon cleared). Validator: zero findings.
- Files: Resources/{evolutions,elements,moves}.json (data), scripts/us165_author.py (authoring
  record), Tests/UltimateSweepEToHTests.swift (new, 25 tests), plus ~20 knock-on test files.
- Build green, 2433 tests, 0 failures.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **A "seadra" (or any keyword-rule) roster-only fixture DIES when its last member is wired.**
    US-165 made GigaSeadramon a node, and DexTypeBadgeTests / ElementCatalogTests both pick a
    roster-only Seadramon at RUN TIME to exercise the keyword fallback. There were none left, so
    both broke. FIX: repoint at one of the 157 permanently-`dexOnly` Digimon (ankylomon -> earth) —
    those can NEVER become nodes, so no later sweep can strand the test again. Before choosing a
    keyword fixture, prefer a dexOnly id over any playable one.
  - **A "second design" whose Wikimon page is the OTHER spelling follows a cited parent, the
    Chaosdramon V2 shape.** `hi-andromon` (sprite Hi-Andromon) and `hiandromon` (HiAndromon) are two
    roster entries; Wikimon has only `HiAndromon` (the dmc-v3 node under Andromon). So hi-andromon is
    the pack's 2nd Andromon sprite and hangs on the OTHER Andromon (`pencme_andromon`, penc-me), not
    a duplicate of the first. Run `opensearch` when a page 404s — Hi-Andromon 404s, HiAndromon is the
    real title.
  - **A sweep can make a Perfect a FOUR-EDGE node, and two prior test files pin that Perfect's edge
    count.** doruguremon (was 3) and pencme_andromon (was 3) each gained a 4th edge here. That breaks
    UltimateSweepCToDTests' "these five carry three edges" list AND PerfectSweepDToGTests'
    `branchedBySweeps` dict AND PendulumMetalEmpireTreeTests' `earned` set AND the doruguremon
    edge-order assertion. Grep the parent id across Tests/*.swift BEFORE authoring a 4th edge; each
    hit is a hardcoded count to bump.
  - **The whole-graph live numbers move for EVERY prior sweep, not just the adjacent one.** Bulk
    edits needed: `graph.nodes.count` 837->851 (19 files), `graph.nodes(at:.ultimate).count`
    158->172 (6 Perfect-sweep files), the ultimate orphan bucket 80->66 and true-remainder 78->64
    (both A-B and C-D Ultimate sweeps), dead-end ledger 60->59 (7 files), and 8 line sizes
    (tamers 116->117, penc-nso 73->75, penc-me 70->71, penc-nsp 41->43, penc-wg 43->45, dmc-v4
    31->34, dmc-v5 25->26, penc-sw 18->20) plus the EvolutionGraphTests byLine dict. The tree files
    exclude a sweep's additions via a `sweepEggs`/`notThisStorys` set so their census stays fixed —
    ADD your nodes there, do not bump the census.
  - **A node on the stranded penc-sw (Saiyu Warriors) line must (a) say "Saiyu Warriors" in its
    comment** (ChildSweepAToFTests / BabyIISweepTests / DigitamaSweepBabyITests iterate every penc-sw
    node) **and (b) be added to EvolutionCriteriaTests.strandedUltimate** (the line has no Digitama,
    so nothing on it is egg-reachable). enmamon and erlangmon both landed there — the honest home,
    since enmamon's every citation is an Ultimate and erlangmon's only bolded on-line parent is the
    Pandamon leaf.
  - **Comment keyword assertions are CASE-SENSITIVE `.contains("Wikimon")`.** "ON WIKIMON" fails;
    write "Wikimon" exactly. Three comments here needed a fix before the new test's citation check
    passed.
  - REMAINS: US-166 onward (52/56 passing). 66 Ultimate orphans (I-Z) + 16 Armor-Hybrid = 82 total.
    Four sweeps left: three Ultimate (I-M, N-R, S-Z) and the Armor-Hybrid one (US-169). Ogudomon is
    still pinned for US-167 (display name O).

## 2026-07-23 - US-171 - Reusable dash-bar component
- Shipped Sources/DashBar.swift: the single visual language every value bar (meat, charges, sleep,
  US-172..192) will render through. `DashBar(filled:total:tint:)` draws `total` equal-width dashes,
  the first `filled` solid (RoundedRectangle.fill) and the rest outline-only (strokeBorder, 1pt),
  NO digits. Pure `DashBarLayout.dashes(filled:total:) -> [Dash]` holds all the clamping so a test
  counts solid vs outline without a view graph.
- Files: Sources/DashBar.swift (new), Tests/DashBarTests.swift (new, 4 tests).
- Verified: full `xcodebuild test` on Series 11 (46mm) => TEST SUCCEEDED, 2472 tests 0 failures.
  DashBar tests cover counts across filled in {0, half, total, total+1}, total==0/negative empties,
  and solid-leads-outline-follows order. Visual AC verified on the 41mm sim (Series 9, 10.4) with a
  throwaway ImageRenderer probe at 162pt content width: the PNG showed exactly 6 solid + 10 outline
  dashes, no number, no horizontal overflow (174pt wide). Probe deleted after; not shipped.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - The narrowest CURRENT-OS sim is 42mm (Series 11); a true 41mm needs Series 9 on watchOS 10.4,
    which was SHUTDOWN and unmatchable by name — boot it and pass `-destination 'id=<UDID>'`
    (FB045EDB-DEB9-40AA-B8FB-819E9E742517). Deployment target is 10.0, so 10.4 devices are valid.
  - To screenshot a bare SwiftUI view (no app run): a gated XCTest using `@MainActor ImageRenderer`
    -> `uiImage.pngData()` written to an ABSOLUTE path. Simulator processes run on the host, so
    "/tmp/foo.png" lands on the HOST /tmp (NOT under CoreSimulator/Devices) — read it there.
    Pass the env var to the test host with the `TEST_RUNNER_` prefix (TEST_RUNNER_DASHBAR_RENDER=1).
  - `strokeBorder` (not `stroke`) for the outline dash: it insets the 1pt line so it stays inside
    the dash frame instead of bleeding onto its neighbour. RoundedRectangle is InsettableShape so it
    has strokeBorder.
  - The xcodegen "generate AFTER the test file exists" rule (US-166) held again: generated once
    after both DashBar.swift + DashBarTests.swift existed; `grep -c DashBarTests pbxproj == 4` and
    the count climbed. Re-generated a THIRD time after deleting the probe to drop it from the target.
- REMAINS: US-172..US-192 (24 stories). US-172 (bottom-align action row) is next by priority.
---

## 2026-07-23 — US-172: Bottom-align the action row and grow the play area
- ContentView's `digimon` VStack now carries, after the map/scrim preference layers:
  `.padding(.bottom, MainScreenLayout.actionRowBottomInset)` then
  `.ignoresSafeArea(.container, edges: .bottom)`. The ignore lets the stack draw into the bottom
  safe-area band watchOS reserves for the corner curvature (26pt on 41mm, 36pt on 46mm); the 4pt
  padding, applied INSIDE the ignore, keeps the row off the very edge. Every reclaimed point lands
  on the sprite's `GeometryReader` because it is the one row at `maxHeight: .infinity`.
- New `MainScreenLayout` enum (actionRowBottomInset = 4) beside `SpriteScale`, pinned by
  `MainScreenLayoutTests.testTheActionRowKeepsExactlyFourPointsBelowIt`.
- Files: Sources/ContentView.swift, Tests/MainScreenLayoutTests.swift.
- Build green (Series 11 46mm). 2473 tests (2472 + 1 new), 0 failures.
- MEASURED before/after, both watch sizes, pre- vs post-story builds. Baseline = HEAD 09c7ea8
  built in a git worktree; identical launch `-healthAnswered -noNotificationPrompt
  -battleAffordableDemo -mapDemo=01_grassland`.
  - AC1 action-row bottom inset: 41mm gap 26pt -> 4.0pt; 46mm gap 36pt -> 4.0pt. Measured as the
    dim colored disc band's lowest row (y421/430 on 41mm, y487/496 on 46mm).
  - AC2 play area grew: map slot 49.0 -> 71.0pt on 41mm (+22, sprite scale 3->4); 63.5 -> 95.5pt on
    46mm (+32, scale 4->5). So the Digimon is a WHOLE step bigger after. MapBackgroundView grows
    with the slot by construction (same SpriteSlotBoundsKey). The before numbers reproduce US-120's
    49.0/64.0pt baseline, which validates the method.
  - AC3 no overlap / chrome unchanged: sprite stays inside its slot (SpriteScale.fitting floors, so
    scale 5 fits); action row is a separate row below the energy bars. Toolbar (lamp/clock/Dex) and
    energy bars (STEP/KCAL/Zz/EXER) byte-identical before and after.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - The two SCREENSHOT patterns added to Codebase Patterns this iteration: a stale SpringBoard
    system alert can survive uninstall/reinstall and only a sim reboot clears it (cost me four dead
    screenshots), and the map slot is measured by a contiguous full-width scan down from its fixed
    top edge — colour/edge-column probes leak into the sprite or the bars.
  - The slot now sits at 71pt (41mm) / 95.5pt (46mm), i.e. scale 4 / 5. US-120's razor-thin 0.5pt
    slack over a 16pt quantum is GONE — the play area has whole points to spare now, so a later
    polish row is no longer one point of font away from shrinking the Digimon. But the 4pt inset is
    load-bearing and pinned; do not pad the action row further without re-measuring the slot.
- REMAINS: US-173..US-192 (20 stories). US-173 (bigger widget sprite) is next by priority.
---

## 2026-07-23 — US-173: Enlarge the Digimon image in the circular complication
- CircularComplicationView drew the sprite at a flat `side: 24` inside a ~52pt circle, so it read
  small at watch-face size. Now the view is a `GeometryReader` wrapping the ZStack, and the sprite
  gets `CircularComplicationLayout.spriteSide(diameter:) = diameter / √2` — the side of the square
  inscribed in the circle. That frame is as big as it can be while its corners only just touch the
  bezel, so the sprite grows to fill the face and clips on no watch size (37pt on a 52pt face, and
  proportionally smaller on a 41mm where a fixed 36pt would have clipped). `.scaledToFit()` and
  `.interpolation(.none)` are untouched, so the pixel art stays crisp.
- New `CircularComplicationLayout` enum beside the view; pinned by
  `ComplicationTests.testTheCircularSpriteFillsTheCircleWithoutClipping` (corner distance == radius,
  and side > the old 24). Updated two stale "24pt sprite in a 52pt circle" comments.
- Files: Sources/ComplicationViews.swift, Tests/ComplicationTests.swift.
- Build green (Series 11 46mm). 2474 tests (2473 + 1 new), 0 failures.
- VISUAL AC verified with `-complicationDemo` before/after screenshots (HEAD build vs this build,
  same 46mm sim). The circular egg goes from ~35% of its AccessoryWidgetBackground square to ~65%,
  well inside the square so a real circular face won't clip it. Confirmed the frame really is the
  inscribed square with a throwaway red `Text("\(Int(diameter))")` overlay: it printed 52, i.e. the
  demo hands the view the full 52pt face and side resolves to ~37pt. Overlay removed before shipping.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - THE SCREENSHOT TRAP THAT COST THE MOST HERE: `xcrun simctl install` was silently installing a
    STALE app from the wrong DerivedData folder, so four rounds of before/after looked byte-identical
    and I nearly concluded the change did nothing. The main project builds to a DerivedData hash you
    must read from `xcodebuild -showBuildSettings | grep BUILT_PRODUCTS_DIR`, NOT the newest
    `DigiVPet-*` dir (a git worktree build creates its own hash and pollutes an `ls -td` guess). Always
    resolve BUILT_PRODUCTS_DIR per build; `simctl uninstall` before `install`; and prove the running
    binary is yours with a temporary on-screen marker before trusting any pixel measurement.
  - A `GeometryReader` as a *sibling* inside a ZStack (`ZStack { background; GeometryReader {...} }`)
    negotiates its size DOWN to the other children and does not report the container size — it read
    ~34pt not 52. Wrap the whole ZStack in the GeometryReader instead to read the real face size.
  - The `-complicationDemo` screen republishes a LIVE snapshot each launch, so the Digimon (an egg in
    the Simulator, HealthKit empty) differs run to run — compare sprite-to-square RATIO, not absolute
    pixels, across a before/after pair.
- REMAINS: US-174..US-192 (19 stories). US-174 is next by priority.

## 2026-07-23 — US-174: Meat is the global feed currency
- Feeding moved off per-Digimon Vitality onto a global meat larder.
  - `PlayerProfile` gained `var meat: Int = 0` (+ init param). The inline default is the migration:
    SwiftData adds the new attribute with it, so every existing save opens with an empty larder.
    Pinned by PlayerProfileTests — the round-trip test now writes/reads meat=12, and the
    pre-migration-fixture test asserts the migrated profile's meat == 0.
  - `FeedAction.feed` now takes `profile:` and spends `meatCostPerFeed` (1). The funds guard sits
    AFTER the hunger>0 refusal guard (a full Digimon still refuses for free, even at 0 meat) and
    blocks with "No meat — go battle." `stageEnergy`/`lifetimeEnergy` are untouched now.
  - `FeedOutcome.fed(cost:)` -> `.fed` (the cost value was consumed by no production code; ~15 test
    call sites updated).
  - `MainScreenModel.feed()` passes `profile`; new `meat`/`meatCap` (=`ConsumptionConfig.bundled.meatCap`)
    computed props. `ContentView` draws `DashBar(filled: meat, total: meatCap, tint: .orange,
    dashHeight: 5)` above `ActionControls`. 5pt is deliberate — it keeps US-172's sprite scale
    (41mm slot 71->66, floor(66/16)=4; 46mm 95.5->90.5, floor=5; both unchanged).
- Files: Sources/PlayerProfile.swift, Sources/FeedAction.swift, Sources/TrainAction.swift (stale
  comment), Sources/MainScreenModel.swift, Sources/ContentView.swift; Tests: FeedingTests,
  CareMistakeTests, WanderingTests, SleepStateTests, LightSwitchTests, FeedMotionTests,
  WakeOnActionTests, PlayerProfileTests.
- Build green (Series 11 46mm). 2474 tests, 0 failures.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - THE RIPPLE: changing a shared *action* (feed) touches every apply-layer suite that drives
    `model.feed()`. They each have their own `startedModel`/`makeModel` helper — the cheap fix is to
    seed `model.profile?.meat = 10` right after `await model.start()` in that ONE helper per file
    (profile is `private(set)` but a class, so mutating its property from a @testable test is fine),
    then only the `.fed(cost:)` -> `.fed` and any energy assertions remain per-test. `perl -0pi -e
    's/\.fed\(cost: FeedAction\.vitalityCostPerFeed\)/.fed/g'` cleaned the mechanical ones.
  - Adding a fixed-height row to the main VStack (spacing 0) costs the sprite slot exactly that
    height, straight off US-172's play area. 41mm has ~7pt of slack over the scale-4 boundary (64pt)
    and 46mm ~15pt over scale-5 (80pt); budget any new bar against that before adding it. The meat
    bar spent 5 of the 41mm 7.
  - Later consumption stories (battle charges, train charges, sleep, HP) each want their own bar.
    There is NOT room for four more full rows without dropping the 41mm sprite a scale step — those
    stories will likely need to co-locate bars or overlay them, not stack them. `meat`/`meatCap` on
    the model is the pattern to copy; per-Digimon charges live on GameState, not the profile.
- REMAINS: US-175..US-192, US-167..US-169 (orphan sweep tail). US-175 (battle wins drop meat) is
  next by priority and is the earning half of this larder.

## 2026-07-23 - US-175 (Battle wins drop meat)
- MeatReward.rolled (Sources/ConsumptionConfig.swift): rolls meatPerBattleWin off an injected
  generator, clamps to max(0, cap - current). The banked value and the displayed value are one thing.
- MainScreenModel.finishBattleRound: on a WIN only, rolls from the SAME generator the fight was
  resolved from (the only half with a generator in hand) and credits profile.meat; the in-memory
  credit persists on finishBattle's existing save beside recordBattle, exactly as the energy cost does.
- BattleBout gains meatGained (default 0); BattleView result screen shows orange fork-and-knife '+N'
  only when >0.
- Tests added to Tests/BattleTests.swift (reused BattleApplyTests.makeModel/fixtureGraph, so no new
  file and no xcodegen-glob trap): MeatRewardTests (pure range/cap arithmetic) +
  testAWonBattleCreditsMeatWithinRangeToTheGlobalLarder (shipped path, first winning seed) +
  testALostBattleDropsNoMeat.
- Build green, 2478 tests, 0 failures.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - "Winning (or completing)" in the AC was read as WIN-only, matching the title "Battle wins drop
    meat" and the reward framing; a loss dropping meat would make losing free. If US-176+ expect
    completion-credit, revisit finishBattleRound's `if report.playerWon`.
  - The battle flow has TWO halves: battle() charges energy + picks opponent + sets pendingBattleRound;
    finishBattleRound(result) resolves the report, builds BattleBout, sets pendingBattle. The generator
    lives on PendingBattleRound and is only alive in finishBattleRound - anything seeded off the fight
    (meat, future drops) must roll there, not in finishBattle.
  - To exercise a WIN through the model without guessing a seed: loop seeds with a strong Digimon
    (strength 40) and `guard bout.report.playerWon else { continue }`. The known loss fixture is
    strength 0, seed 3.
  - profile.meat is surfaced by MainScreenModel.meat / the ContentView DashBar (US-174) and spent by
    FeedAction; US-175 is the earner that closes the walk->battle->feed loop.

## 2026-07-23 - US-176 (Battle charges accrue from steps, per Digimon)
- GameState: added `battleCharges` (0..10) and `battleChargeSteps` (remainder toward the next
  charge), both migration-safe optional storage like every other field here. `creditBattleCharges(
  steps:stepsPerCharge:maxCharges:)` adds whole charges from a step delta, banks the sub-300
  remainder so short walks across many refreshes are not lost, and drops the remainder at the cap.
- Wiring: `MainScreenModel.creditMapSteps` now credits charges from the SAME `MetricLedger.claim`
  step delta it credits the map from — one claim, two consumers, as the ledger's own doc requires.
  Credited to `state` (the Digimon that is OUT), so charges are per-Digimon; frozen Digimon don't
  refresh and so accrue nothing.
- battle(): a `guard state.battleCharges > 0` (message "No charge — go walk.") sits after
  wakeIfAsleep and before the energy guard; a started battle spends one charge beside
  `EnergyPurchase.charge`, saved by the same flush. The energy cost was KEPT.
- UI: `MainScreenModel.battleCharges`/`battleChargeCap`; ContentView draws a purple charge DashBar
  co-located with the orange meat bar in one HStack (not a second stacked row) to protect US-172/173.
- Tests: BattleChargeCreditTests (pure: 900->3, 3300->cap10, remainder carry, spend-keeps-remainder,
  two-Digimon independence); two model tests in the battle apply class (spends exactly one charge;
  unavailable at 0 charges and says so); one end-to-end in BackgroundRefreshTests (900 stepped
  refresh banks 3 charges). Seeded `state.battleCharges = ConsumptionConfig.bundled.maxBattleCharges`
  in every battle-driving test helper (PreBattleRound, Battle, BattleCost, DigitamaDrop, Wandering,
  WakeOnAction, LightSwitch, BackgroundRefresh).
- Build green (Series 11 46mm). 2486 tests, 0 failures.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - THE RIPPLE (again): adding a hard gate to `battle()` breaks every apply-suite that drives
    `model.battle()` and does not seed the new resource — 8 files. Same cheap fix as US-174's meat:
    seed the resource right where each helper already stocks energy/meat (before `save()` for the
    build-a-state helpers, after `await start()` for the post-start `startedModel` ones). Placing the
    charge guard AFTER the death/training/wake guards and keeping the energy guard means all existing
    REFUSAL tests (dead, broke, training-in-progress) still fire unchanged once charges are seeded.
  - DECISION: US-176's AC says "spends exactly one charge" but — unlike US-177 for train — never says
    "replacing the energy cost". So the energy cost was KEPT and the charge is an ADDITIONAL gate.
    Removing energy would have gutted US-108's BattleCostTests/PreBattleRoundTests for no AC. If a
    later story wants charges to be the SOLE battle cost, that is a separate, explicit change.
  - The shared `MetricLedger.claim(.healthSteps,...)` SPENDS the delta — a second independent claimer
    gets 0. Any future step-derived consumer (US-179's MetricCreditor) must read the delta
    `creditMapSteps` already claims, not claim its own. Charges follow that rule; copy it.
  - Play-area budget: co-locate new currency bars in the existing meat HStack (US-174), never add a
    stacked row — the 41mm sprite has no more scale slack after meat spent its ~5pt.
- REMAINS: US-177..US-192 (consumption/battle-stats/polish tail), US-167..US-169 (orphan sweep tail).
  US-177 (train charges from calories) is next by priority and per its AC DOES replace the train
  energy cost — mirror this story's GameState field + creditFromDelta pattern, but remove the
  TrainAction energy spend rather than keep it.

## 2026-07-23 - US-177 (Train charges accrue from active calories, per Digimon)
- Repriced training onto a per-Digimon charge burned from active calories, mirroring US-176's battle charge exactly.
- Source changes:
  - GameState.swift: added trainCharges/trainChargeKcal (optional storage, nil reads as 0, migration-safe) + creditTrainCharges(kcal:kcalPerCharge:maxCharges:), a copy of creditBattleCharges' shape with kcal in place of steps.
  - ConsumptionConfig.swift + Resources/consumption.json: added maxTrainCharges (10) and to the caps validator list. kcalPerTrain (50) already existed (US-170).
  - TrainAction.swift: begin() now spends one trainCharge and NO Strength/Stamina energy; blocks at 0 with noChargeReason "No training charge — go exercise." Removed energyCostPerTraining/payableWith/insufficientEnergyReason and the EnergyPurchase call. TrainOutcome=.trained(gain:), TrainingStart=.started (dropped spent/cost).
  - Battle.swift: BattleCost decoupled from TrainAction — now owns energy=5, payableWith=[.strength,.stamina], its own reason string. Battle is the last action that spends energy.
  - MainScreenModel.swift: PendingTraining dropped spent/cost; finishTraining caption is "Grade +N STR"; refresh() calls new creditTrainCharges(_:) reading dayReadings.quantities[.activeEnergy] and claiming it off MetricLedger (shared delta, same rule the map steps use); added trainCharges/trainChargeCap computed props.
  - ContentView.swift: third red DashBar (dashHeight 5) in the meat/battle HStack — same row, no added height, US-172/US-174 sprite scale untouched.
- Tests: 2491 total, 0 failures (Series 11 46mm). New TrainChargeCreditTests (150 kcal->3, cap, remainder, two-Digimon independence + decrement) and ClosedAppRecomputeTests.testExerciseCreditsTrainChargesToTheDigimon (refresh end-to-end). Rewrote the three training suites for the charge currency; stocked trainCharges in ~10 fixture helpers that used to fund training with strength energy; replaced BattleCostTests' "identical to TrainAction" test with one pinning BattleCost's own numbers; added maxTrainCharges to ConsumptionConfigTests' 4 constructors.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **Battle charge is the template for every "spendable charge" story.** creditBattleCharges (GameState), the MetricLedger.claim shared delta in creditMapSteps, the DashBar in ContentView's currency HStack, and model.battleCharges/battleChargeCap are the exact five seams a new charge copies. US-177 mirrored all five.
  - **Active energy day-total is dayReadings.quantities[.activeEnergy]; steps is [.steps].** Both come off the ONE HealthEnergySource.dayReadings read in refresh, keyed by QuantityMetric. Claim it via metricLedger.claim(.healthActiveEnergy, ...) — that is a ConditionMetric, distinct from the QuantityMetric key. .healthActiveEnergy has no other claim caller today, so it is a clean single consumer.
  - **BackgroundRefreshTests' refresh-level class is ClosedAppRecomputeTests, not "BackgroundRefreshTests".** -only-testing:DigiVPetTests/BackgroundRefreshTests runs 0 tests. The DailyStepFetcher there filters by metric==.steps and returns [] otherwise; a calorie test needs its own fetcher filtering metric==.activeEnergy (added DailyActiveEnergyFetcher).
  - **Changing an action's currency ripples to every test that funded it the old way.** Training was funded with strength energy in ~12 files; all had to seed trainCharges instead or the 0-charge default silently blocks the round (and blocked rounds count no session, so stageTrainingSessions assertions flip). grep 'TrainAction.begin|TrainAction.train(|model.train()' before assuming a fixture is unaffected.
  - **When action A borrows action B's constants and B changes, decouple A first.** BattleCost borrowed TrainAction.energyCostPerTraining etc.; removing them from TrainAction broke Battle.swift's compile. Gave BattleCost its own copies.

## 2026-07-23 - US-178 (Cleaning poop costs a global handwash charge)
- Closed the last arm of the care loop: clearing the mess now spends a charge walked up from HealthKit handwashing, capped at 2 and shared globally across the box.
- Source changes (the battle-charge template, adapted for a GLOBAL currency read from a CATEGORY metric):
  - PlayerProfile.swift: added cleanCharges + handwashProgress (plain stored props with = 0 defaults, migration-safe the way `meat` is, NOT the optional-storage GameState pattern — a fresh @Model attribute with a default is lighter and meat proved it) + init params; creditCleanCharges(events:eventsPerCharge:maxCharges:) (a copy of GameState.creditBattleCharges' while-loop, cap and dropped-remainder), and spendCleanCharge()->Bool. Global like meat, because a habit is the player's, not one pet's.
  - MainScreenModel.swift: added injected `metricReader: HealthMetricReader = HealthMetricReader()`; refresh() calls new `await creditCleanCharges()` after creditTrainCharges; that method reads .healthHandwashing over HealthDay.interval(containing: now) via the reader, claims the day-total off the SHARED MetricLedger under .healthHandwashing (dedup), and credits the profile at handwashPerCleanCharge; added cleanCharges/cleanChargeCap computed props; clean() now guards poopCount>0 FIRST then `profile.spendCleanCharge()`, showing "No charge — go wash." and returning false at zero.
  - ContentView.swift: fourth teal DashBar (dashHeight 5, tint .teal to match the Clean sparkles) in the SAME meat/train/battle HStack — no added height, sprite scale untouched.
  - consumption.json/ConsumptionConfig.swift: NO change needed — handwashPerCleanCharge (1) and maxCleanCharges (2) already shipped in US-177's config and were already in the caps validator list.
- Tests: 2501 total, 0 failures (Series 11 46mm). New CleaningChargeTests.swift (10): charge arithmetic (1->1, cap-drops-remainder, sub-threshold accumulation at eventsPerCharge=3, spend/refuse-at-zero), AC4's two clean() cases + a two-spend-then-empty run, refresh crediting off a HandwashFetcher fixture, dedup (two refreshes count once), and the bar's profile/config inputs. Stocked cleanCharges in 6 existing clean-success tests (CleanTrainMotionTests helper, ComplicationTests x2, MainScreenTests x3, LightSwitchTests helper, NotificationTests x2) exactly the way US-176 stocked battle charges.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **A CATEGORY health metric (handwashing, toothbrushing, mindful, stand-hours) is NOT in dayReadings.** dayReadings.quantities is keyed by QuantityMetric = steps/activeEnergy/exercise only. Category/event metrics are read via HealthMetricReader.read(ReadableHealthMetric(.healthX)!, in: HealthDay.interval(...)) and deduped by claiming off MetricLedger under the ConditionMetric key. US-178 is the FIRST Sources caller of HealthMetricReader (it was test-only before, per US-118's note).
  - **The default metricReader is LIVE, so refresh-calling tests do a live handwashing query.** It is harmless: the Simulator has no handwashing data (the CLAUDE.md premise), so the query returns noData deterministically and credits nothing — verified non-hanging across the whole suite. Only inject a fixture reader when you are TESTING the credit; everything else can ignore it. (This is unlike the energy path, which every test injects — but energy tests assert on energy; handwashing tests are the only ones that assert on washes.)
  - **clean() ordering: poopCount>0 guard BEFORE the charge guard.** "Nothing to clean" must stay a silent no-op (the two existing no-op tests need no charge stock); the "go wash" message only makes sense when there IS a mess being refused. Same reason battle() checks state before charges.
  - **The face-tapped clean (applyPendingCleanRequest) runs clean() too**, so it also spends a charge — correct, and the ComplicationTests fixture for it needed stocking. It runs at the TOP of refresh, before that refresh's own creditCleanCharges, so it spends charges banked on a PRIOR refresh.
  - **Global currency (meat, cleanCharges) lives on PlayerProfile with a plain `= 0` stored prop; per-Digimon currency (battleCharges, trainCharges) lives on GameState with optional storage.** Pick the home by whether the fact outlives putting one Digimon away — a habit/larder does, a pet's earned charges do not.

## 2026-07-23 - US-179 (Wire the metric ledger into the health-read flow)
- Revived the dead health-condition pipeline: MetricCreditor.credit had 0 callers in Sources (test-only), so stageMetricTotals/lifetimeMetricTotals/stageBestDayMetrics were always empty and every health.* evolution condition was dead (atLeast never passed, atMost passed for free, standing metrics forced to .unknown). Now refresh() calls it beside EnergyCreditor.credit and supplies ConditionContext.readings from HealthMetricReader at every build point.
- Source changes:
  - HealthMetricReader.swift: added `readings(of:in:) -> [ConditionMetric: HealthReading]`, a sequential batch read (matches TodayHealthReader.readToday), used by both models. Callers pass ReadableHealthMetric.all.
  - MainScreenModel.swift: new `healthReadings(dayReadings:)` seeds .healthSteps/.healthActiveEnergy/.healthExerciseMinutes from dayReadings.quantities and .healthSleep from dayReadings.sleep (no double HealthKit read), reads every other ReadableHealthMetric.all over today's window, and KEEPS ONLY .value entries. refresh() calls it, stores conditionReadings, then `MetricCreditor.credit(metrics, ledger: metricLedger, ...)` -> creditedMetrics. The three charge helpers became pure delta consumers: creditMapSteps(_ steps: Double), creditTrainCharges(_ kcal: Double), creditCleanCharges(_ events: Double) — the last is no longer async (its handwashing read folded into the shared metric read). The 4 real ConditionContext builds (jogressBoard, mapDetailContext, evolveIfReady, checkForDigitamaDrop) now pass `readings: conditionReadings`.
  - DexModel.swift + DexView.swift: DexModel gained injected metricReader + calendar and `loadHealthReadings(now:) async`; DexView's new `.task` calls it (sync load() still paints the grid first). load()'s ConditionContext now carries self.readings.
- Tests: 2507 total (2501 + 6 new), 0 failures (Series 11 46mm), ~48s. New MetricWiringTests.swift: AC4 (credited sleep 480 clears atLeast 400, fails atMost 400 through the full chain), AC5 (standing resting-HR via readings answerable, unit), AC1 (a refresh credits flightsClimbed=12 to all three totals — non-evolving graph so enterStage does not wipe them), AC3 (second same-day refresh credits once), AC2/AC5 end-to-end (a resting-HR-52 read drives an atMost-60 gated evolution; 72 blocks it).
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **MetricCreditor.credit is now the SINGLE claimer of the day's metrics off MetricLedger; the map/battle/train/clean charge paths consume the deltas it RETURNS.** This was forced: those paths already claimed steps/activeEnergy/handwashing, so a second claim from MetricCreditor gets 0 and the stage totals never grow. If you add a new consumer of a health metric, take it from `creditedMetrics[.healthX]` in refresh() — do NOT add a fresh `metricLedger.claim(.healthX, ...)`, that is now a double-claim that steals the delta. The one place claim() is called from Sources is MetricCreditor.credit.
  - **conditionReadings is .value-ONLY on purpose.** Dropping .noData/.unavailable keeps ConditionContext's line-96 "unavailable -> unknown" override switched OFF, so accumulating atMost freebies are UNCHANGED (US-180's job to fix). This is why wiring readings into every build point did not break a single one of the 2501 prior tests: in the Simulator all reads are .unavailable -> filtered -> conditionReadings empty -> identical to the old empty-dict behaviour. On a real device with data, standing metrics become answerable (Problem 4) and accumulating totals fill (Problem 1).
  - **Adding ~22 live HealthKit reads per refresh did NOT slow the suite** (2501->2507 tests, ~48s, was already ~47s). Real reads return .unavailable fast in the Simulator (the same reason US-178's single handwashing read was harmless). ReadableHealthMetric.all is ~25; the 3 daily quantities + sleep are seeded from dayReadings so only ~21 are actually queried.
  - **A conditions-gated evolution test must NOT let the Digimon evolve for the wrong reason.** The credit tests (AC1/AC3) need a TERMINAL hero (no edges) because any evolution runs enterStage, which clears stageMetricTotals + stageBestDayMetrics — a passing credit into stage totals then reads back 0 while lifetime survives. The evolution tests (AC2) want the branching graph. Two graphs in one fixture file.
  - **DexModel does live reads now, off a `.task`, not `load()`.** load() stays synchronous (21 test call sites) and paints the grid with empty readings; loadHealthReadings() reads metrics and re-resolves ONLY the hint context. hasReadHealth guards the re-read; a -dexRevealDemo literal context is never overwritten.
  - **NOT DONE, tracked as US-180:** an accumulating atMost health gate still passes for free where the metric was never credited (reads .known(0)). The .value-only filter deliberately does not fire the unavailable-override for that. US-180 makes never-credited read as .unknown via the GameState accessor returning nil.

## 2026-07-23 - US-180 (No data is unknown, not zero)
- Closed the freebie US-179 tracked: an accumulating health `atMost` gate passed for free where the metric was never credited, because ConditionContext.healthValue read the totals through `MetricTotals.subscript`, which flattens an absent metric to 0, and 0 satisfies atMost.
- Source changes (only these two files):
  - MetricLedger.swift: added `MetricTotals.known(_ metric:) -> Double?` returning `values[metric.rawValue]` — nil when never credited. The subscript is unchanged (still flattens absent->0 for the `+= delta` arithmetic path); nothing ever writes an explicit 0, so present-in-`values` == really-credited and absent == never-touched. That distinction is invisible through the subscript and is exactly what the condition path needs.
  - ConditionEvaluator.swift: healthValue's accumulating branch now `guard let totals, let value = totals.known(metric) else { return .unknown }` instead of `.known(totals[metric])`. So an uncredited accumulating metric is `.unknown` even when the stage/lifetime/day totals struct is present; a metric credited to exactly 0 is present and stays `.known(0)`.
- Tests: 2510 total (2507 + 3 new), 0 failures (Series 11 46mm), ~48s. The 3 new (in ConditionEvaluationTests.swift) also observed passing on their own:
  - testMetricTotalsKnownDistinguishesUncreditedFromZero: known() nil for never-credited, 0 for credited-0; subscript still 0 either way.
  - testAnUncreditedAccumulatingMetricIsUnknownEvenWithTotalsPresent: healthValue .unknown over stage/lifetime/day when totals present but metric absent; credited-0 stays .known(0) (AC1/AC2).
  - testUncreditedFailsBothGatesWhileACreditedZeroSatisfiesAtMost: no credit -> atLeast(1) AND atMost(500) both false; credited-0 -> atMost(500) true, atLeast(1) false (AC3).
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **MetricTotals now has TWO readers with different jobs.** `subscript` = "the number for arithmetic", absent reads 0 — use it for `+= delta` accrual (MetricCreditor). `known(_:)` = "was this ever credited?", absent reads nil — use it on the condition/eligibility path where never-credited must be `.unknown`, not zero. Do not swap them: reading the subscript on a gate reintroduces the atMost freebie; reading known() in accrual crashes on the first credit.
  - **The `.unavailable` override (line 96) and the never-credited-unknown rule are SEPARATE fixes for the same trap.** US-179's conditionReadings is `.value`-only so the unavailable override stays off in the Simulator; US-180 makes the totals themselves report unknown for a metric that was never written. Together: on real hardware a denied metric (unavailable reading) AND a never-credited metric (absent from totals) both read `.unknown` and both fail atMost, rather than one path leaking a free 0.
  - **Why `Fixture.context(stageSteps: 0)` still satisfies atMost after this change:** it writes `totals[.healthSteps] = 0` through the subscript SETTER, so the key is present with value 0 — a *credited* 0, `.known(0)`. The change only affects metrics ABSENT from `values`. That is why not one of the 2507 prior tests broke.
---

## 2026-07-23 - US-181 (Accumulated sleep hours stored per Digimon)
- Each Digimon now remembers its lifetime HealthKit sleep, so switching which one is out shows the right progress toward its sleep evolution gate (US-183). Distinct from the nightly sleep ENERGY (that tops up stageEnergy via EnergyCreditor and resets) - this only ever grows.
- Source changes (only these two files):
  - GameState.swift: private `accumulatedSleepMinutesStorage: Double?` (optional for the same SwiftData migration reason as every other storage prop; nil reads as 0), inited to 0; computed `accumulatedSleepMinutes` (native unit MetricLedger credits health.sleep in), `accumulatedSleepHours` (minutes/60, the unit a gate is authored in - Agumon needs 16h), and `creditSleep(minutes:)` which guards >0 and just adds - NO cap (it climbs past any gate, like a map's recorded steps past its total).
  - MainScreenModel.swift: `state.creditSleep(minutes: creditedMetrics[.healthSleep])` in refresh(), beside creditMapSteps/creditTrainCharges/creditCleanCharges - the SAME US-179 MetricLedger delta they spend, so a night is de-duplicated once and shared.
- Tests: 2519 total (2510 + 9 new), 0 failures (Series 11 46mm), ~48s. New Tests/SleepAccumulationTests.swift, all 9 also observed passing on their own:
  - SleepAccumulationCreditTests (pure): 405 min -> 6.75 h; many reads sum without a cap (17 h); non-positive deltas are no-ops; two GameStates independent.
  - SleepAccumulationPersistenceTests (GameStore): a banked total survives a reopen; a box of two (active hero 405 + frozen agu_digitama 120) keeps each apart across a reopen.
  - SleepAccumulationRefreshTests (end to end): a fixture night 23:30-06:15 (405 min, wholly inside last night's 18:00-noon window) credits model.state 405 min / 6.75 h on start(); a SECOND refresh of the same night banks it ONCE (405, not 810); a FROZEN box-mate granted before the refresh accrues 0 while the active hero banks 405 (AC2, US-125).
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **The per-Digimon health accrual pattern is now three-strong: creditBattleCharges (steps), creditTrainCharges (kcal), creditSleep (minutes) all live on GameState and are all fed the RETURNED `creditedMetrics[.healthX]` delta in refresh().** Follow it for any new per-Digimon health accumulation: private optional storage + computed accessor + a credit(delta:) that adds; never call `metricLedger.claim` a second time (US-179's single-claimer rule).
  - **"A frozen Digimon does not accrue" is free by construction.** refresh() only ever passes the ACTIVE `state` to creditSleep; a frozen box-mate is never refreshed. So a per-record accumulation IS the freeze behaviour - no clock-offset trick needed here (unlike hunger/age which are Date-derived, US-125).
  - **health.sleep is credited in MINUTES** (MetricLedger.accumulatesOverTime true; SleepAnalysis.asleepMinutes -> .value(minutes)). Store the native minutes; expose hours as minutes/60. A gate authored in hours (US-183) compares against accumulatedSleepHours.
  - **To feed sleep end-to-end in a test:** inject a FixtureSleepFetcher into LastNightSleepReader, set `now` to the morning AFTER (last night's window is 18:00 prev day -> noon today), and the sample must fall wholly inside. 23:30-06:15 = 405 min. The model needs a real GameStore (not nil) for the MetricLedger to exist and MetricCreditor to run.
  - **US-182/US-183 seam:** model.state.accumulatedSleepHours is what the Zz DashBar (US-182) and the detail sleep bar + gate (US-183) read.

The other three slots (STEP/KCAL/EXER) stay energy bars, so the 2x2 grid keeps its exact shape and widths - the spirit *energy* still accrues underneath (EnergyProgress is unchanged), it just isn't the thing the Zz slot draws any more.

Added `seedSleepBarDemoIfRequested()` (DEBUG) beside the other seeds: `-sleepBarDemo` seeds 6 accumulated hours, `-sleepBarFullDemo` 14, both on a Child Agumon, so the Zz bar can be screenshotted with a real fill (the Simulator banks no HealthKit sleep).

The Zz slot draws a row of dashes with NO number where the spirit energy capsule/number used to be; `-sleepBarDemo` shows ~6 solid of 16 and `-sleepBarFullDemo` ~14 of 16 - clearly different fill. Screens at /tmp/us182/sleep6.png and sleep14.png.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **The Simulator queues a notification-authorization system alert AND a HealthKit onboarding gate on a fresh/erased device; both hide the main screen.** To screenshot the main screen, launch with BOTH `-noNotificationPrompt` (already existed, gates `requestNotificationAuthorization`) AND `-healthAnswered` (StubHealthAuthorizer.Outcome, bypasses HealthAuthorizationGate). A pending notif alert survives app uninstall - only `xcrun simctl erase` clears it - so never launch a screenshot build without `-noNotificationPrompt` first, or you have to erase and start over. System Events cannot see the watch-screen alert as a native button, so it can't be dismissed by AppleScript.

The change is purely in EnergyBarsView's rendering + two new model accessors. If US-183 wants the Zz bar to target the nearest sleep *gate* instead of the fixed cap, swap `sleepHoursTotal` for that - the seam is the one `EnergyBarsView(...)` call in ContentView.
  - **`sleepHoursCap` is a deliberate nominal (16), not the per-edge gate.** The PRD splits it: the main-screen Zz bar is at-a-glance "how rested" against a fixed length; the PRECISE required-vs-earned sleep bar is the DETAIL view (US-183). Don't wire the evolution gate into the main bar - that's US-183's detail bar.

## 2026-07-23 - US-183 (Sleep as an evolution gate with a detail dash bar)
- Made accumulated sleep a real evolution gate and drew it as a dash bar in the Dex detail view.
- Files changed:
  - Resources/evolutions.json: added a health.sleep / window:lifetime / atLeast 960 condition to the agumon -> greymon edge ("Let it bank a good long stretch of sleep" - digit-free hint). 960 min = 16 h; this is the "Agumon needs 16 hours" exemplar the PRD names.
  - Sources/SleepGate.swift (NEW): pure helper. requiredHours(in: [EvolutionCondition]) -> Int? = max of the health.sleep/lifetime/atLeast thresholds, /60, rounded (nil = no gate = no bar). earnedHours(in: ConditionContext) -> Int = context.value(.healthSleep, .lifetime) minutes /60 FLOORED, .unknown -> 0. atMost sleep excluded (a ceiling is not a fill-toward bar).
  - Sources/DexView.swift: DexDetailView gained `sleepBar` (moon.zzz icon + DashBar(filled: earnedHours, total: requiredHours, tint: .indigo), no numbers), drawn after the "Evolves into" heading only when SleepGate.requiredHours(over the candidates' conditions) is non-nil.
  - Tests/SleepGateTests.swift (NEW, 10 tests): the gate unmet at 6h/15.9h and met at 16h/20h; .unknown stays shut; the shipped graph authors >=1 accumulated-sleep gate with a non-blank hint; validator clean; the real agumon->greymon edge carries the 16h gate; the ENGINE (evolutionTarget on the real agumon node) falls to numemon at 6h and reaches greymon at 16h; the bar reports filled==earned, total==required; floor behaviour; no bar without an atLeast sleep gate.
  - Tests/ConditionRevealTests.swift: updated testTheDemoScenarioProducesAllThreeLevels expectation [.close,.far] -> [.close,.far,.far] (greymon now has a third, cold, sleep condition in that scenario).
- Tests: 2532 total (2522 + 10 new), 0 failures (Series 11 46mm), ~48s. Build green.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **The accumulated-sleep gate needed NO ConditionEvaluator change - it is just health.sleep/window:lifetime.** accumulatedSleepMinutes (US-181) and lifetimeMetricTotals['health.sleep'] (US-179) are fed the SAME creditedMetrics[.healthSleep] delta in refresh(), so they are equal by construction; both are lifetime-of-this-Digimon and never reset per stage. The gate reads the lifetime total via the existing pipeline (US-179 fills it, US-180 makes never-credited read .unknown not a free 0). So US-181's on-GameState field is effectively a mirror the Zz bar (US-182) reads; the gate + detail bar read the CONTEXT total instead, which guarantees the bar's solid count matches what the gate compares (no drift possible).
  - **health.sleep is authored in MINUTES everywhere (existing 119 conditions are stage/minutes too); the bar divides by 60 for the hours the player sees.** Do NOT author a sleep gate in hours - the evaluator compares against minute-valued totals, so "16" would mean 16 minutes and pass instantly. requiredHours() and earnedHours() are the ONLY /60 in the codebase.
  - **A lifetime-window condition on a SWEPT edge breaks the sweep tests.** Every sweep "met" context (e.g. ChildSweepAToF) sets stageTotals but NOT lifetimeTotals, so a health.sleep/lifetime gate reads .unknown and the sweep's earned-branch engine test fails. I gated agumon->greymon specifically because Agumon is EXCLUDED from ChildSweepAToF's sweptChildren (a pre-wired device tree) and nothing engine-evolves the real agumon->greymon with a partial context. If a future story adds a lifetime health gate to a SWEPT node, it must also add that metric to the sweep's `met` lifetimeTotals - or the sweep will fail.
  - **Adding a condition to a shipped edge can break a pinned demo-scenario test.** ConditionRevealTests.testTheDemoScenarioProducesAllThreeLevels asserts the EXACT reveal-level list of agumon->greymon; a third condition changed [.close,.far] to [.close,.far,.far]. Grep Tests for the node id you touch before adding a condition - the -dexRevealDemo screenshot pins agumon.

- Added the unanswerable-window validator rule (metric x window the evaluator only answers .unknown).
- Sources/EvolutionCondition.swift: ConditionWindow now CaseIterable.
- Sources/ConditionEvaluator.swift: ConditionContext.fullyPopulated(for:) probe; ConditionMetric.answerableWindows / canBeAnswered(over:) derived FROM that probe (so it can never drift from careValue/healthValue).
- Sources/EvolutionGraphValidator.swift: GraphValidationError.unanswerableConditionWindow(from:to:metric:window:), checked in validate(condition:) after the knownMetric guard.
- Sources/MapCatalogValidator.swift: MapValidationError.unanswerableConditionWindow(map:digitamaId:metric:window:), checked in validate(slot:) guarded on a KNOWN metric.
- Tests: fixture tests in EvolutionGraphValidatorTests + MapCatalogValidatorTests fire the rule for all three named pairs and pass over the answerable windows; ConditionEvaluationTests pins the full answerable-window matrix.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - evolutions.json is ALREADY clean under this rule (0 findings). Shipped maps.json has 20 mis-windowed Digitama slots (care.battleCount/care.battleWinRatio window=stage, one care.trainingSessions window=lifetime) — this is the bug class US-184 exists to catch. Per the AC this story adds the RULE only; the data fix is a SEPARATE pass.
  - Renamed MapCatalogValidatorTests.testTheShippedCatalogHasNoFindings -> testTheShippedCatalogHasOnlyTheKnownMisWindowedSlotFindings: it now allowlists the unanswerableConditionWindow class and asserts (a) no OTHER class appears and (b) the mis-windowed class is NON-empty. When the data-fix pass re-authors the slots, delete the allowlist and restore `== []`.

Fixed by moving them to window=lifetime (each metric's answerable window) so they exercise only their intended range rules. grep the Tests tree for care.battle* window=stage / care.trainingSessions window!=stage before adding a similar rule.
  - The answerable windows: health.* = {stage,day,lifetime}; care.trainingSessions/overfeeds/sleepDisturbances = {stage}; care.battleCount = {day,lifetime}; care.battleWinRatio = {lifetime}.

## 2026-07-23 - US-185 (Light-off evolution condition)
- Added `care.lightOff` to `ConditionMetric` (EvolutionCondition.swift): the one `care.*`
  member that is a STATE, not a counter. Reads 1 while `LightState.off`, 0 otherwise, so an
  edge says "light must be off" as `care.lightOff atLeast 1` — no new field on EvolutionCondition.
- `ConditionContext` gained a `lightState: LightState?` field (nil = unknown = fails, like every
  other field). Populated by `init(state:now:)` from `GameState.lightState` and by
  `fullyPopulated(for:)` (as `.off`). `careValue` answers it ONLY over the canonical `.stage`
  window; day/lifetime are `.unknown`, so the US-184 validator rejects an edge windowed otherwise.
- Handled the new case in every exhaustive switch: `ConditionMetric.defaultHint` (ConditionHints),
  `HealthMetricReader.source(for:)` (not readable — no HK grant). `readObjectType`/
  `accumulatesOverTime`/`conditionHealthMetrics` need no change (all key off `health.` prefix).
- Authored into 3 dark-line edges by REPLACING one care criterion each (kept count + family
  invariants): devimon->neodevimon, icedevimon->baalmon, blackguilmon->blackgrowmon.
- New Tests/LightOffConditionTests.swift: off evolves / on+semi+unknown blocked, `.stage`-only
  window, bundled graph uses it and validates to zero findings.
- Files: Sources/EvolutionCondition.swift, Sources/ConditionEvaluator.swift, Sources/ConditionHints.swift,
  Sources/HealthMetricReader.swift, Resources/evolutions.json, Tests/LightOffConditionTests.swift,
  Tests/ConditionEvaluationTests.swift (answerable-window table), and the three sweep-test context
  builders (ChildSweepAToF `met`, PerfectSweepAToC/NToR `context(for:)`) set `lightState: .off`.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - New evolution condition TYPES are added as new `ConditionMetric` vocabulary (a JSON edit),
    NOT as a new shape on `EvolutionCondition` — that is the documented growth path, and the
    exhaustive `defaultHint` switch (no `default:`) forces you to give the new metric a hint.
  - A non-numeric/boolean condition fits the metric/comparison/value model as 1/0 with `atLeast 1`;
    restrict its answerable window to `.stage` so US-184's validator enforces one canonical spelling.
  - Adding a condition to an edge in a sweep's range breaks that sweep's "every earned branch fires"
    test (its context builder does not satisfy the new criterion) AND, for PerfectSweepN-R, the
    strict "2 conditions = 1 health + 1 care" invariant. REPLACING a care criterion (not ADDING)
    preserves the count/family invariants; then only the context builder needs `lightState: .off`.
  - `care.lightOff` is a `care.*` STATE, so it needs no HealthKit grant and is excluded from
    `conditionHealthMetrics`/`HealthReadSet` automatically by the `health.` prefix routing.

## 2026-07-23 - US-186 (Light-off map condition)
- Made the light off a MAP condition too: a dark Digimon a map reveals only with the light out.
- The feature needed NO new engine code. `care.lightOff` (US-185) is ordinary condition vocabulary,
  `DigitamaSlot` reuses `EvolutionCondition`, and `DigitamaDropEngine` reads it through
  `ConditionReveal.allMet` against a `ConditionContext` that already carries `lightState`. So a
  light-off gate on a slot is honoured out of the box (off -> eligible, on/semi/unknown -> withheld).
- Files changed:
  - Resources/maps.json:
    - 15_dungeon/ghost_digitama now carries `care.lightOff` (window stage, atLeast 1, hint
      "Seek it in the dark, with the light off") in place of its old care.battleWinRatio — AC3.
    - AC2 required the shipped catalog to validate to ZERO findings, but it still carried the 20
      unanswerable-window slots US-184 deliberately deferred. Did that data-fix pass here: every
      `care.battleCount`/`care.battleWinRatio` authored per `stage` (windows neither counter is kept
      over, so those eggs could NEVER drop) is re-windowed to `lifetime`, and the lone
      `care.trainingSessions` per `lifetime` to `stage`. maps.json now validates clean (0 findings).
  - Tests/MapCatalogValidatorTests.swift: replaced testTheShippedCatalogHasOnlyTheKnownMisWindowedSlotFindings
    (the US-184 allowlist) with testTheShippedCatalogHasNoFindings asserting `validate() == []`.
  - Tests/DigitamaDropTests.swift: new LightOffMapConditionTests — pure-engine off/on eligibility,
    semi+unknown withhold, the shipped ghost slot honoured (20 lifetime battles + light off drops it,
    light on holds it), and the validator accepts a light-off slot with no finding.
  - Sources/EvolutionGraphValidator.swift: refreshed a doc comment that claimed maps.json still
    carries mis-windowed slots (US-186 fixed the last of them).
- Tests: 2546 total, 0 failures (Series 11 46mm), ~48s. Build green.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **A new evolution/map condition TYPE added as `ConditionMetric` vocabulary (US-185) is
    automatically a MAP condition too.** DigitamaSlot conditions ARE EvolutionConditions, the drop
    engine reuses ConditionReveal.allMet, and MainScreenModel builds the ConditionContext from
    GameState (lightState included) — so US-186 was authoring + tests, not plumbing. The seam to
    build a context by hand in tests is `ConditionContext(lightState:battlesLifetime:...)`.
  - **The 20 mis-windowed map slots US-184 flagged are now GONE — maps.json validates to `== []`.**
    care.battleCount/care.battleWinRatio live over {day|lifetime}/{lifetime}; care.trainingSessions/
    overfeeds/sleepDisturbances over {stage} only; care.lightOff over {stage} only. Author map slot
    conditions accordingly or the US-184 validator rejects them.
  - **Those slots were DEAD before the fix** (unanswerable window -> .unknown -> never met -> egg
    never dropped), so re-windowing them broke no drop-behaviour test — it made ~10 eggs reachable.
    If a future test wants to pin one of those eggs dropping, its context must satisfy the NEW window
    (e.g. battlesLifetime for care.battleCount, not a stage total).

## 2026-07-23 - US-187 (Every Digimon has HP, Attack and Agility)
- The per-stage base stat table (`StageStats` struct + `stageStats` in ConsumptionConfig.swift and
  Resources/consumption.json) was already SHIPPED by US-170's groundwork and pinned by
  ConsumptionConfigTests (covers every playable stage, strictly climbing base up the ladder). So the
  config half of this story needed nothing new. This story added the per-Digimon resolution, the UI,
  and the roster-wide guarantee.
- Sources/ConsumptionConfig.swift: added `stats(for entry: RosterEntry) -> StageStats?` — nil for a
  `dexOnly` entry (never playable) and nil for a Digitama (an egg has no combat stats, resolves
  through `stats(for: .digitama)` returning nil since the table omits that one stage), the stage row
  otherwise. So all 868 playable entries get all three stats off their stage with no companion file,
  and a Perfect out-stats a Child by construction.
- Sources/StatBarsView.swift (new): `StatBarsLayout` (budget), `BattleStat` enum (hp/attack/agility
  → value/symbol/tint/accessibilityName), `DexStatBars.stats(for:roster:config:)` resolver (nil for
  undiscovered/dexOnly/Digitama, mirroring DexMoveRow's discovery gate), and `StatBarsRow` view —
  three stacked labelled DashBars (heart red / burst orange / hare green), each `filled==total==base`
  so the bar length is the stat's magnitude, NO numbers drawn.
- Sources/DexView.swift: DexDetailView gained a `config: ConsumptionConfig = .bundled` injectable and
  a `statBars` @ViewBuilder placed after `attackRow` (the "what is this in a fight" identity block),
  before the Evolves-into divider.
- Tests/DexStatBarsTests.swift (new, 7 tests): AC3 whole-roster coverage (every non-dexOnly,
  non-Digitama entry resolves all three stats, each >0; guarded with a >700 battler floor so it can't
  pass vacuously), eggs/dexOnly resolve nil, sheet presence == discovered&battler over the whole
  roster, three labelled stats, layout budget.
- VERIFIED: `xcodebuild build` green; full `xcodebuild test` on Series 11 (46mm) => 2553 tests, 0
  failures. AC4 screenshot: rendered the real StatBarsRow for Child (Agumon 5/3/3) and Perfect
  (9/7/5) via a gated ImageRenderer probe (RENDER_STATBARS) -> /tmp/us187/agumon_detail.png; showed
  three labelled dash bars, no numbers, Perfect visibly longer than Child. Probe deleted after, not
  shipped.
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - **The battle-stat CONFIG (StageStats/stageStats) already ships from US-170 and is tested by
    ConsumptionConfigTests.** US-188..US-192 (HP bar in battle, agility dodge, element damage, train
    caps) should READ `ConsumptionConfig.stats(for: entry)` / `stats(for: stage)`, not re-author a
    table. `trainingCap` is already on `StageStats` waiting for US-192.
  - **`ConsumptionConfig.stats(for: RosterEntry)` is the one place that knows a Digimon's base
    stats** — dexOnly and Digitama both resolve nil there. Anything that needs a battler's stats
    should go through it so the "eggs/idle-only never fight" rule stays in one place.
  - **The `-dexDemo` screenshot path is currently CRASHING on a freshly-erased sim** — SwiftData
    `ModelContext.reset` fatal in `DexModel.loadHealthReadings` -> `GameState.stageMetricTotals`
    (reads a GameState off a reset context). Pre-existing, unrelated to stat bars. To screenshot a
    Dex detail view, the reliable route is the gated ImageRenderer probe (US-171 DashBar pattern):
    render the sub-views (name + StatBarsRow) in a plain VStack, NOT the whole DexDetailView — its
    body is a `ScrollView`, and ImageRenderer renders a ScrollView as an all-black blank.
  - `BattleStat` is a plain (no-associated-value) enum, so it's Hashable for free — `ForEach(...,
    id: \.self)` needs no manual conformance.

## 2026-07-23 - US-188: Dash-style HP bar in battle
- Per-Digimon max HP in the engine + a red HP DashBar per combatant in BattleView.
- Files changed:
  - Sources/Battle.swift — BattleReport gained playerMaxHitPoints/opponentMaxHitPoints (defaulted to startingHitPoints) and a maxHitPoints(side) accessor; BattleEngine.resolve gained playerMaxHitPoints/opponentMaxHitPoints params (defaulted, floored at 1); model doc updated to per-Digimon pool.
  - Sources/BattleView.swift — replaced the "N — N" text HP readout with two red HP DashBars (player left / opponent right, total = max HP, solid = current HP, no number); added maxHitPoints(side) + hpBar(for:); BattleView.hitPoints(afterTurn:) gained a defaulted maxHitPoints param.
  - Sources/MainScreenModel.swift — finishBattleRound feeds each side its per-stage baseHP from ConsumptionConfig; removed the now-redundant inner `let config`.
  - Tests/BattleTests.swift — new BattleDashHPBarTests (3 tests).
- Verified: build green; full suite 2556 tests, 0 failures (2553 + 3).
- **Learnings for future iterations:**
  - BattleReport and BattleEngine.resolve are back-compat via DEFAULTED stored props / params — a Swift synthesized memberwise init gives a default to any stored property with an initial value, so adding fields did NOT churn the ~15 existing BattleReport(...) / resolve(...) call sites. Reuse this pattern for US-189/190/191 rather than threading new required args everywhere.
  - Per-stage baseHP lives in ConsumptionConfig.stats(for: Stage)?.baseHP (Baby I 3 ... Ultimate 12). Effective HP = base only for now; US-191 training bonuses will add to it, and battle (US-188/189/190) reads the effective value.
  - BattleView.hitPoints(_:afterTurn:of:maxHitPoints:) is the pure "solid dash count" — assert the on-screen bar against it, no view graph needed (DashBarLayout.dashes renders the solid/outline split).
  - This story's AC has NO Simulator screenshot requirement (US-189's does). The HP bar is a pure DashBar pinned by tests.
